		<outline text="（1）邻接权的主体多为法人或其他组织，著作权的主体多为自然人。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E9%82%BB%E6%8E%A5%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%BB%E4%BD%93%E5%A4%9A%E4%B8%BA%E6%B3%95%E4%BA%BA%E6%88%96%E5%85%B6%E4%BB%96%E7%BB%84%E7%BB%87%EF%BC%8C%E8%91%97%E4%BD%9C%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%BB%E4%BD%93%E5%A4%9A%E4%B8%BA%E8%87%AA%E7%84%B6%E4%BA%BA%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="（2）邻接权的客体是传播作品过程中产生的成果，而著作权的客体是作品本身。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%E9%82%BB%E6%8E%A5%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E5%AE%A2%E4%BD%93%E6%98%AF%E4%BC%A0%E6%92%AD%E4%BD%9C%E5%93%81%E8%BF%87%E7%A8%8B%E4%B8%AD%E4%BA%A7%E7%94%9F%E7%9A%84%E6%88%90%E6%9E%9C%EF%BC%8C%E8%80%8C%E8%91%97%E4%BD%9C%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E5%AE%A2%E4%BD%93%E6%98%AF%E4%BD%9C%E5%93%81%E6%9C%AC%E8%BA%AB%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（3）邻接权中除表演者权外一般不涉及人身权，而著作权包括人身权和财产权双重内容。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%E9%82%BB%E6%8E%A5%E6%9D%83%E4%B8%AD%E9%99%A4%E8%A1%A8%E6%BC%94%E8%80%85%E6%9D%83%E5%A4%96%E4%B8%80%E8%88%AC%E4%B8%8D%E6%B6%89%E5%8F%8A%E4%BA%BA%E8%BA%AB%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%8C%E8%80%8C%E8%91%97%E4%BD%9C%E6%9D%83%E5%8C%85%E6%8B%AC%E4%BA%BA%E8%BA%AB%E6%9D%83%E5%92%8C%E8%B4%A2%E4%BA%A7%E6%9D%83%E5%8F%8C%E9%87%8D%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="289.简述对著作权限制（合理使用、法定许可）❶❷" _mubu_text="289.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E5%AF%B9%E8%91%97%E4%BD%9C%E6%9D%83%E9%99%90%E5%88%B6%EF%BC%88%E5%90%88%E7%90%86%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E3%80%81%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%EF%BC%89%E2%9D%B6%E2%9D%B7">
		<outline text="著作权的合理使用" _mubu_text="%E8%91%97%E4%BD%9C%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E5%90%88%E7%90%86%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8">
		<outline text="著作权的合理使用的概念" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E8%91%97%E4%BD%9C%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E5%90%88%E7%90%86%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5%3C/span%3E" _heading="1" _color="#75c940">
		<outline text="著作权的合理使用，属于对著作权的一种限制，它是指自然人、法人或者其他组织为了个人欣赏、评论、新闻报道、教学与艺术研究以及公益事业的目的，根据著作权法的规定，可以不经过作者同意而使用其已经发表的作品，并且不需要向其支付报酬的行为。" _mubu_text="%E8%91%97%E4%BD%9C%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E5%90%88%E7%90%86%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%EF%BC%8C%E5%B1%9E%E4%BA%8E%E5%AF%B9%E8%91%97%E4%BD%9C%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%80%E7%A7%8D%E9%99%90%E5%88%B6%EF%BC%8C%E5%AE%83%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E8%87%AA%E7%84%B6%E4%BA%BA%E3%80%81%E6%B3%95%E4%BA%BA%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%85%B6%E4%BB%96%E7%BB%84%E7%BB%87%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%3E%E4%B8%BA%E4%BA%86%E4%B8%AA%E4%BA%BA%E6%AC%A3%E8%B5%8F%E3%80%81%E8%AF%84%E8%AE%BA%E3%80%81%E6%96%B0%E9%97%BB%E6%8A%A5%E9%81%93%E3%80%81%E6%95%99%E5%AD%A6%E4%B8%8E%E8%89%BA%E6%9C%AF%E7%A0%94%E7%A9%B6%E4%BB%A5%E5%8F%8A%E5%85%AC%E7%9B%8A%E4%BA%8B%E4%B8%9A%E7%9A%84%E7%9B%AE%E7%9A%84%3C/span%3E%EF%BC%8C%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE%E8%91%97%E4%BD%9C%E6%9D%83%E6%B3%95%E7%9A%84%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E4%B8%8D%E7%BB%8F%E8%BF%87%E4%BD%9C%E8%80%85%E5%90%8C%E6%84%8F%E8%80%8C%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E5%85%B6%E5%B7%B2%E7%BB%8F%E5%8F%91%E8%A1%A8%E7%9A%84%E4%BD%9C%E5%93%81%EF%BC%8C%E5%B9%B6%E4%B8%94%E4%B8%8D%E9%9C%80%E8%A6%81%E5%90%91%E5%85%B6%E6%94%AF%E4%BB%98%E6%8A%A5%E9%85%AC%E7%9A%84%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E3%80%82" _note="@必须掌握的概念&nbsp;@口诀&nbsp;著作合用上坪暴雪依依" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%BF%85%E9%A1%BB%E6%8E%8C%E6%8F%A1%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E8%91%97%E4%BD%9C%E5%90%88%E7%94%A8%E4%B8%8A%E5%9D%AA%E6%9A%B4%E9%9B%AA%E4%BE%9D%E4%BE%9D">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="著作权的合理使用的对象是：" _mubu_text="%E8%91%97%E4%BD%9C%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E5%90%88%E7%90%86%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E7%9A%84%E5%AF%B9%E8%B1%A1%E6%98%AF%EF%BC%9A">
		<outline text="已经发表的作品。" _mubu_text="%E5%B7%B2%E7%BB%8F%E5%8F%91%E8%A1%A8%E7%9A%84%E4%BD%9C%E5%93%81%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="应当尊重作者的人身权利，应当指明作者姓名、作品名称并且不得影响作品的正常利用，也不得不合理地损害著作权人的合法利益。" _mubu_text="%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E5%B0%8A%E9%87%8D%E4%BD%9C%E8%80%85%E7%9A%84%E4%BA%BA%E8%BA%AB%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%EF%BC%8C%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E6%8C%87%E6%98%8E%E4%BD%9C%E8%80%85%E5%A7%93%E5%90%8D%E3%80%81%E4%BD%9C%E5%93%81%E5%90%8D%E7%A7%B0%E5%B9%B6%E4%B8%94%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E4%B8%8D%E5%BE%97%E5%BD%B1%E5%93%8D%E4%BD%9C%E5%93%81%E7%9A%84%E6%AD%A3%E5%B8%B8%E5%88%A9%E7%94%A8%3C/span%3E%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E4%B9%9F%E4%B8%8D%E5%BE%97%E4%B8%8D%E5%90%88%E7%90%86%E5%9C%B0%E6%8D%9F%E5%AE%B3%E8%91%97%E4%BD%9C%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%90%88%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		<outline text="合理使用也适用于对邻接权人的限制。" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%3E%E5%90%88%E7%90%86%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E4%B9%9F%E9%80%82%E7%94%A8%E4%BA%8E%E5%AF%B9%E9%82%BB%E6%8E%A5%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E9%99%90%E5%88%B6%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E" _color="#dc2d1e">

		<outline text="著作权的法定许可的概念" _mubu_text="%E8%91%97%E4%BD%9C%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">

		<outline text="（1）九年义务教育和国家教育规划的教科书" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E6%95%99%E8%82%B2%E5%92%8C%E5%9B%BD%E5%AE%B6%E6%95%99%E8%82%B2%E8%A7%84%E5%88%92%E7%9A%84%E6%95%99%E7%A7%91%E4%B9%A6" _note="数：教科书" _mubu_note="%E6%95%B0%EF%BC%9A%E6%95%99%E7%A7%91%E4%B9%A6">
		<outline text="为实施九年义务教育和国家教育规划而编写出版教科书，除作者事先声明不许使用的外，可不经著作权人许可，在教科书中汇编已经发表的作品片段或者短小的文字作品、音乐作品或者单幅的美术作品、摄影作品，但应当按照规定支付报酬，指明作者姓名、作品名称，并且不得侵犯著作权人依照本法享有的其他权利。" _mubu_text="%E4%B8%BA%E5%AE%9E%E6%96%BD%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E6%95%99%E8%82%B2%E5%92%8C%E5%9B%BD%E5%AE%B6%E6%95%99%E8%82%B2%E8%A7%84%E5%88%92%E8%80%8C%E7%BC%96%E5%86%99%E5%87%BA%E7%89%88%E6%95%99%E7%A7%91%E4%B9%A6%EF%BC%8C%E9%99%A4%E4%BD%9C%E8%80%85%E4%BA%8B%E5%85%88%E5%A3%B0%E6%98%8E%E4%B8%8D%E8%AE%B8%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E7%9A%84%E5%A4%96%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%AF%E4%B8%8D%E7%BB%8F%E8%91%97%E4%BD%9C%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%9C%A8%E6%95%99%E7%A7%91%E4%B9%A6%E4%B8%AD%E6%B1%87%E7%BC%96%E5%B7%B2%E7%BB%8F%E5%8F%91%E8%A1%A8%E7%9A%84%E4%BD%9C%E5%93%81%E7%89%87%E6%AE%B5%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E7%9F%AD%E5%B0%8F%E7%9A%84%E6%96%87%E5%AD%97%E4%BD%9C%E5%93%81%E3%80%81%E9%9F%B3%E4%B9%90%E4%BD%9C%E5%93%81%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%8D%95%E5%B9%85%E7%9A%84%E7%BE%8E%E6%9C%AF%E4%BD%9C%E5%93%81%E3%80%81%E6%91%84%E5%BD%B1%E4%BD%9C%E5%93%81%EF%BC%8C%E4%BD%86%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E6%8C%89%E7%85%A7%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E6%94%AF%E4%BB%98%E6%8A%A5%E9%85%AC%EF%BC%8C%E6%8C%87%E6%98%8E%E4%BD%9C%E8%80%85%E5%A7%93%E5%90%8D%E3%80%81%E4%BD%9C%E5%93%81%E5%90%8D%E7%A7%B0%EF%BC%8C%E5%B9%B6%E4%B8%94%E4%B8%8D%E5%BE%97%E4%BE%B5%E7%8A%AF%E8%91%97%E4%BD%9C%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E4%BE%9D%E7%85%A7%E6%9C%AC%E6%B3%95%E4%BA%AB%E6%9C%89%E7%9A%84%E5%85%B6%E4%BB%96%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">

		<outline text="290.简述著作权的法定许可❶❷" _mubu_text="290.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E8%91%97%E4%BD%9C%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E2%9D%B6%E2%9D%B7">
		<outline text="著作权的法定许可的概念" _mubu_text="%E8%91%97%E4%BD%9C%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="著作权的法定许可是指依照法律的明文规定，不经著作权人同意而有偿使用他人已经发表的作品的行为。法定许可是除了合理使用外对著作权的又一限制。" _mubu_text="%E8%91%97%E4%BD%9C%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E4%BE%9D%E7%85%A7%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E7%9A%84%E6%98%8E%E6%96%87%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E4%B8%8D%E7%BB%8F%E8%91%97%E4%BD%9C%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E5%90%8C%E6%84%8F%E8%80%8C%E6%9C%89%E5%81%BF%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E4%BB%96%E4%BA%BA%E5%B7%B2%E7%BB%8F%E5%8F%91%E8%A1%A8%E7%9A%84%E4%BD%9C%E5%93%81%E7%9A%84%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E6%98%AF%E9%99%A4%E4%BA%86%E5%90%88%E7%90%86%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E5%A4%96%E5%AF%B9%E8%91%97%E4%BD%9C%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E5%8F%88%E4%B8%80%E9%99%90%E5%88%B6%E3%80%82" _note="@必须掌握的概念" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%BF%85%E9%A1%BB%E6%8E%8C%E6%8F%A1%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>

		<outline text="著作权的法定许可的情形主要有" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E8%91%97%E4%BD%9C%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E7%9A%84%E6%83%85%E5%BD%A2%E4%B8%BB%E8%A6%81%E6%9C%89%3C/span%3E" _note="@简答题&nbsp;@题眼&nbsp;@口诀&nbsp;竹筏行数转音二放" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E9%A2%98%E7%9C%BC%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E7%AB%B9%E7%AD%8F%E8%A1%8C%E6%95%B0%E8%BD%AC%E9%9F%B3%E4%BA%8C%E6%94%BE" _heading="1" _color="#dc2d1e">
		<outline text="（1）九年义务教育和国家教育规划的教科书" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E6%95%99%E8%82%B2%E5%92%8C%E5%9B%BD%E5%AE%B6%E6%95%99%E8%82%B2%E8%A7%84%E5%88%92%E7%9A%84%E6%95%99%E7%A7%91%E4%B9%A6">
		<outline text="为实施九年义务教育和国家教育规划而编写出版教科书，除作者事先声明不许使用的外，可不经著作权人许可，在教科书中汇编已经发表的作品片段或者短小的文字作品、音乐作品或者单幅的美术作品、摄影作品，但应当按照规定支付报酬，指明作者姓名、作品名称，并且不得侵犯著作权人依照本法享有的其他权利。" _mubu_text="%E4%B8%BA%E5%AE%9E%E6%96%BD%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E6%95%99%E8%82%B2%E5%92%8C%E5%9B%BD%E5%AE%B6%E6%95%99%E8%82%B2%E8%A7%84%E5%88%92%E8%80%8C%E7%BC%96%E5%86%99%E5%87%BA%E7%89%88%E6%95%99%E7%A7%91%E4%B9%A6%EF%BC%8C%E9%99%A4%E4%BD%9C%E8%80%85%E4%BA%8B%E5%85%88%E5%A3%B0%E6%98%8E%E4%B8%8D%E8%AE%B8%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E7%9A%84%E5%A4%96%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%AF%E4%B8%8D%E7%BB%8F%E8%91%97%E4%BD%9C%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%9C%A8%E6%95%99%E7%A7%91%E4%B9%A6%E4%B8%AD%E6%B1%87%E7%BC%96%E5%B7%B2%E7%BB%8F%E5%8F%91%E8%A1%A8%E7%9A%84%E4%BD%9C%E5%93%81%E7%89%87%E6%AE%B5%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E7%9F%AD%E5%B0%8F%E7%9A%84%E6%96%87%E5%AD%97%E4%BD%9C%E5%93%81%E3%80%81%E9%9F%B3%E4%B9%90%E4%BD%9C%E5%93%81%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%8D%95%E5%B9%85%E7%9A%84%E7%BE%8E%E6%9C%AF%E4%BD%9C%E5%93%81%E3%80%81%E6%91%84%E5%BD%B1%E4%BD%9C%E5%93%81%EF%BC%8C%E4%BD%86%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E6%8C%89%E7%85%A7%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E6%94%AF%E4%BB%98%E6%8A%A5%E9%85%AC%EF%BC%8C%E6%8C%87%E6%98%8E%E4%BD%9C%E8%80%85%E5%A7%93%E5%90%8D%E3%80%81%E4%BD%9C%E5%93%81%E5%90%8D%E7%A7%B0%EF%BC%8C%E5%B9%B6%E4%B8%94%E4%B8%8D%E5%BE%97%E4%BE%B5%E7%8A%AF%E8%91%97%E4%BD%9C%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E4%BE%9D%E7%85%A7%E6%9C%AC%E6%B3%95%E4%BA%AB%E6%9C%89%E7%9A%84%E5%85%B6%E4%BB%96%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">

		<outline text="（2）刊登后的转载、摘录和资料刊登" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%E5%88%8A%E7%99%BB%E5%90%8E%E7%9A%84%E8%BD%AC%E8%BD%BD%E3%80%81%E6%91%98%E5%BD%95%E5%92%8C%E8%B5%84%E6%96%99%E5%88%8A%E7%99%BB">
		<outline text="作品刊登后，除著作权人声明不得转载、摘编的外，其他报刊可以转载或者作为文摘、资料刊登，但应当按照规定向著作权人支付报酬。" _mubu_text="%E4%BD%9C%E5%93%81%E5%88%8A%E7%99%BB%E5%90%8E%EF%BC%8C%E9%99%A4%E8%91%97%E4%BD%9C%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E5%A3%B0%E6%98%8E%E4%B8%8D%E5%BE%97%E8%BD%AC%E8%BD%BD%E3%80%81%E6%91%98%E7%BC%96%E7%9A%84%E5%A4%96%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%85%B6%E4%BB%96%E6%8A%A5%E5%88%8A%3C/span%3E%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E8%BD%AC%E8%BD%BD%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E4%BD%9C%E4%B8%BA%E6%96%87%E6%91%98%E3%80%81%E8%B5%84%E6%96%99%E5%88%8A%E7%99%BB%EF%BC%8C%E4%BD%86%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E6%8C%89%E7%85%A7%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E5%90%91%E8%91%97%E4%BD%9C%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E6%94%AF%E4%BB%98%E6%8A%A5%E9%85%AC%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="（3）录音制作者使用他人合法录制的录音制品" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%E5%BD%95%E9%9F%B3%E5%88%B6%E4%BD%9C%E8%80%85%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E4%BB%96%E4%BA%BA%E5%90%88%E6%B3%95%E5%BD%95%E5%88%B6%E7%9A%84%E5%BD%95%E9%9F%B3%E5%88%B6%E5%93%81">
		<outline text="录音制作者使用他人已经合法录制为录音制品的音乐作品制作录音作品，可以不经著作权人许可，但应当按照规定支付报酬。著作权人声明不许使用的不得使用。" _mubu_text="%E5%BD%95%E9%9F%B3%E5%88%B6%E4%BD%9C%E8%80%85%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E4%BB%96%E4%BA%BA%E5%B7%B2%E7%BB%8F%E5%90%88%E6%B3%95%E5%BD%95%E5%88%B6%E4%B8%BA%E5%BD%95%E9%9F%B3%E5%88%B6%E5%93%81%E7%9A%84%E9%9F%B3%E4%B9%90%E4%BD%9C%E5%93%81%E5%88%B6%E4%BD%9C%E5%BD%95%E9%9F%B3%E4%BD%9C%E5%93%81%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E4%B8%8D%E7%BB%8F%E8%91%97%E4%BD%9C%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%EF%BC%8C%E4%BD%86%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E6%8C%89%E7%85%A7%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E6%94%AF%E4%BB%98%E6%8A%A5%E9%85%AC%E3%80%82%E8%91%97%E4%BD%9C%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E5%A3%B0%E6%98%8E%E4%B8%8D%E8%AE%B8%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%8D%E5%BE%97%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="广播电台、电视台播放他人已经发表的作品可以不经著作权人许可，但应支付报酬。" _mubu_text="%E5%B9%BF%E6%92%AD%E7%94%B5%E5%8F%B0%E3%80%81%E7%94%B5%E8%A7%86%E5%8F%B0%E6%92%AD%E6%94%BE%E4%BB%96%E4%BA%BA%E5%B7%B2%E7%BB%8F%E5%8F%91%E8%A1%A8%E7%9A%84%E4%BD%9C%E5%93%81%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E4%B8%8D%E7%BB%8F%E8%91%97%E4%BD%9C%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%EF%BC%8C%E4%BD%86%E5%BA%94%E6%94%AF%E4%BB%98%E6%8A%A5%E9%85%AC%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="（5）广播电台、电视台播放已经出版的录音制品" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%885%EF%BC%89%E5%B9%BF%E6%92%AD%E7%94%B5%E5%8F%B0%E3%80%81%E7%94%B5%E8%A7%86%E5%8F%B0%E6%92%AD%E6%94%BE%E5%B7%B2%E7%BB%8F%E5%87%BA%E7%89%88%E7%9A%84%E5%BD%95%E9%9F%B3%E5%88%B6%E5%93%81">

		<outline text="291.简述对著作权的保护❶" _mubu_text="291.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E5%AF%B9%E8%91%97%E4%BD%9C%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E4%BF%9D%E6%8A%A4%E2%9D%B6">
		<outline text="侵犯著作权，是指他人未经著作权人许可又无法律上的依据，使用他人作品或行使著作专有权的行为。视侵权行为情节的轻重及危害后果的不同，侵权者应当承担民事责任、行政责任和刑事责任中的一种或同时承担几种法律责任。" _mubu_text="%E4%BE%B5%E7%8A%AF%E8%91%97%E4%BD%9C%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%8C%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E4%BB%96%E4%BA%BA%E6%9C%AA%E7%BB%8F%E8%91%97%E4%BD%9C%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E5%8F%88%E6%97%A0%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E4%B8%8A%E7%9A%84%E4%BE%9D%E6%8D%AE%EF%BC%8C%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E4%BB%96%E4%BA%BA%E4%BD%9C%E5%93%81%E6%88%96%E8%A1%8C%E4%BD%BF%E8%91%97%E4%BD%9C%E4%B8%93%E6%9C%89%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E3%80%82%E8%A7%86%E4%BE%B5%E6%9D%83%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E6%83%85%E8%8A%82%E7%9A%84%E8%BD%BB%E9%87%8D%E5%8F%8A%E5%8D%B1%E5%AE%B3%E5%90%8E%E6%9E%9C%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%8D%E5%90%8C%EF%BC%8C%E4%BE%B5%E6%9D%83%E8%80%85%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E6%89%BF%E6%8B%85%E6%B0%91%E4%BA%8B%E8%B4%A3%E4%BB%BB%E3%80%81%E8%A1%8C%E6%94%BF%E8%B4%A3%E4%BB%BB%E5%92%8C%E5%88%91%E4%BA%8B%E8%B4%A3%E4%BB%BB%E4%B8%AD%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%80%E7%A7%8D%E6%88%96%E5%90%8C%E6%97%B6%E6%89%BF%E6%8B%85%E5%87%A0%E7%A7%8D%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E8%B4%A3%E4%BB%BB%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="有下列侵权行为的,应当根据情况,承担停止侵害、消除影响、赔礼道歉、赔偿损失等民事责任。" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%9C%89%E4%B8%8B%E5%88%97%E4%BE%B5%E6%9D%83%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E7%9A%84,%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE%E6%83%85%E5%86%B5,%E6%89%BF%E6%8B%85%E5%81%9C%E6%AD%A2%E4%BE%B5%E5%AE%B3%E3%80%81%E6%B6%88%E9%99%A4%E5%BD%B1%E5%93%8D%E3%80%81%E8%B5%94%E7%A4%BC%E9%81%93%E6%AD%89%E3%80%81%E8%B5%94%E5%81%BF%E6%8D%9F%E5%A4%B1%E7%AD%89%E6%B0%91%E4%BA%8B%E8%B4%A3%E4%BB%BB%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E" _note="@口诀&nbsp;明泽表叔外妾改永祖，为父设计传播塔&nbsp;@考点&nbsp;@简答题" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E6%98%8E%E6%B3%BD%E8%A1%A8%E5%8F%94%E5%A4%96%E5%A6%BE%E6%94%B9%E6%B0%B8%E7%A5%96%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%BA%E7%88%B6%E8%AE%BE%E8%AE%A1%E4%BC%A0%E6%92%AD%E5%A1%94&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E8%80%83%E7%82%B9%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E" _heading="1" _color="#3da8f5">
		<outline text="1.发表、单独发表、署名、歪曲篡改、剽窃、改变他人作品，或者使用、出租他人作品类。" _mubu_text="1.%E5%8F%91%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E8%A1%A8%3C/span%3E%E3%80%81%E5%8D%95%E7%8B%AC%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%8F%91%3C/span%3E%E8%A1%A8%E3%80%81%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E7%BD%B2%3C/span%3E%E5%90%8D%E3%80%81%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%AD%AA%3C/span%3E%E6%9B%B2%E7%AF%A1%E6%94%B9%E3%80%81%E5%89%BD%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E7%AA%83%3C/span%3E%E3%80%81%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%94%B9%3C/span%3E%E5%8F%98%E4%BB%96%E4%BA%BA%E4%BD%9C%E5%93%81%EF%BC%8C%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E4%BD%BF%3C/span%3E%E7%94%A8%E3%80%81%E5%87%BA%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E7%A7%9F%3C/span%3E%E4%BB%96%E4%BA%BA%E4%BD%9C%E5%93%81%E7%B1%BB%E3%80%82" _note="@口诀&nbsp;表叔外妾改永祖" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E8%A1%A8%E5%8F%94%E5%A4%96%E5%A6%BE%E6%94%B9%E6%B0%B8%E7%A5%96">

		<outline text="（三）退职、退休或者调动工作后一年内作出的，与其在原单位承担的本职工作或者原单位分配的任务有关的发明创造。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%88%E4%B8%89%EF%BC%89%E9%80%80%E8%81%8C%E3%80%81%E9%80%80%E4%BC%91%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E8%B0%83%E5%8A%A8%E5%B7%A5%E4%BD%9C%E5%90%8E%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%86%85%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%8E%E5%85%B6%E5%9C%A8%E5%8E%9F%E5%8D%95%E4%BD%8D%E6%89%BF%E6%8B%85%E7%9A%84%E6%9C%AC%E8%81%8C%E5%B7%A5%E4%BD%9C%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%8E%9F%E5%8D%95%E4%BD%8D%E5%88%86%E9%85%8D%E7%9A%84%E4%BB%BB%E5%8A%A1%E6%9C%89%E5%85%B3%E7%9A%84%E5%8F%91%E6%98%8E%E5%88%9B%E9%80%A0%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="发明" _mubu_text="%E5%8F%91%E6%98%8E">

		<outline text="实用新型和发明相比：" _mubu_text="%E5%AE%9E%E7%94%A8%E6%96%B0%E5%9E%8B%E5%92%8C%E5%8F%91%E6%98%8E%E7%9B%B8%E6%AF%94%EF%BC%9A">
		<outline text="①范围不如发明大，不包括物品的制造方法；" _mubu_text="%E2%91%A0%E8%8C%83%E5%9B%B4%E4%B8%8D%E5%A6%82%E5%8F%91%E6%98%8E%E5%A4%A7%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%8D%E5%8C%85%E6%8B%AC%E7%89%A9%E5%93%81%E7%9A%84%E5%88%B6%E9%80%A0%E6%96%B9%E6%B3%95%EF%BC%9B" _note="伪：范围" _mubu_note="%E4%BC%AA%EF%BC%9A%E8%8C%83%E5%9B%B4">

		<outline text="专利权并非自动产生的权利，必须经过专利行政部门的授予才能取得。" _mubu_text="%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E5%B9%B6%E9%9D%9E%E8%87%AA%E5%8A%A8%E4%BA%A7%E7%94%9F%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%EF%BC%8C%E5%BF%85%E9%A1%BB%E7%BB%8F%E8%BF%87%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E8%A1%8C%E6%94%BF%E9%83%A8%E9%97%A8%E7%9A%84%E6%8E%88%E4%BA%88%E6%89%8D%E8%83%BD%E5%8F%96%E5%BE%97%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="专利权的授予条件包括实体条件和程序条件。" _mubu_text="%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E6%8E%88%E4%BA%88%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E5%8C%85%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%8B%AC%E5%AE%9E%E4%BD%93%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E5%92%8C%E7%A8%8B%E5%BA%8F%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%3C/span%3E%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="实体条件" _mubu_text="%E5%AE%9E%E4%BD%93%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6">
		<outline text="1.授予发明和实用新型专利权的实体条件" _mubu_text="1.%E6%8E%88%E4%BA%88%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%8F%91%E6%98%8E%E5%92%8C%E5%AE%9E%E7%94%A8%E6%96%B0%E5%9E%8B%3C/span%3E%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E5%AE%9E%E4%BD%93%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6">
		<outline text="（1）新颖性" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E6%96%B0%E9%A2%96%E6%80%A7">
		<outline text="我国专利法对新颖性的要求" _mubu_text="%E6%88%91%E5%9B%BD%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%B3%95%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B0%E9%A2%96%E6%80%A7%E7%9A%84%E8%A6%81%E6%B1%82" _note="我国在新颖性标准上采用的是绝对新颖性标准。" _mubu_note="%E6%88%91%E5%9B%BD%E5%9C%A8%E6%96%B0%E9%A2%96%E6%80%A7%E6%A0%87%E5%87%86%E4%B8%8A%E9%87%87%E7%94%A8%E7%9A%84%E6%98%AF%E7%BB%9D%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B0%E9%A2%96%E6%80%A7%E6%A0%87%E5%87%86%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="①该发明或者实用新型不属于现有技术。" _mubu_text="%E2%91%A0%E8%AF%A5%E5%8F%91%E6%98%8E%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%AE%9E%E7%94%A8%E6%96%B0%E5%9E%8B%E4%B8%8D%E5%B1%9E%E4%BA%8E%E7%8E%B0%E6%9C%89%E6%8A%80%E6%9C%AF%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="现有技术是指申请日以前在国内外为公众所知的技术，技术公开的方式包括，出版物公开、使用公开和其他方式的公开。" _mubu_text="%E7%8E%B0%E6%9C%89%E6%8A%80%E6%9C%AF%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E6%97%A5%E4%BB%A5%E5%89%8D%E5%9C%A8%E5%9B%BD%E5%86%85%E5%A4%96%E4%B8%BA%E5%85%AC%E4%BC%97%E6%89%80%E7%9F%A5%E7%9A%84%E6%8A%80%E6%9C%AF%EF%BC%8C%E6%8A%80%E6%9C%AF%E5%85%AC%E5%BC%80%E7%9A%84%E6%96%B9%E5%BC%8F%E5%8C%85%E6%8B%AC%EF%BC%8C%E5%87%BA%E7%89%88%E7%89%A9%E5%85%AC%E5%BC%80%E3%80%81%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E5%85%AC%E5%BC%80%E5%92%8C%E5%85%B6%E4%BB%96%E6%96%B9%E5%BC%8F%E7%9A%84%E5%85%AC%E5%BC%80%E3%80%82" _note="@法条分析" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E6%B3%95%E6%9D%A1%E5%88%86%E6%9E%90%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="②也没有任何单位或者个人就同样的发明或者实用新型在申请日以前向国务院专利行政部门提出过申请，并记载在申请日以后公布的专利申请文件或者公告的专利文件中。" _mubu_text="%E2%91%A1%E4%B9%9F%E6%B2%A1%E6%9C%89%E4%BB%BB%E4%BD%95%E5%8D%95%E4%BD%8D%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E4%B8%AA%E4%BA%BA%E5%B0%B1%E5%90%8C%E6%A0%B7%E7%9A%84%E5%8F%91%E6%98%8E%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%AE%9E%E7%94%A8%E6%96%B0%E5%9E%8B%E5%9C%A8%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E6%97%A5%E4%BB%A5%E5%89%8D%E5%90%91%E5%9B%BD%E5%8A%A1%E9%99%A2%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E8%A1%8C%E6%94%BF%E9%83%A8%E9%97%A8%E6%8F%90%E5%87%BA%E8%BF%87%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%EF%BC%8C%E5%B9%B6%E8%AE%B0%E8%BD%BD%E5%9C%A8%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E6%97%A5%E4%BB%A5%E5%90%8E%E5%85%AC%E5%B8%83%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E6%96%87%E4%BB%B6%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%85%AC%E5%91%8A%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%96%87%E4%BB%B6%E4%B8%AD%E3%80%82" _note="意思是申请人申请专利时，即使有其他的单位和个人就相同的发明或者实用新型先于申请人提出申请的，只要在先的申请最后没有获得批准，申请人仍然可能申请成功。申请专利的技术是否与他人申请的专利重合，有他人的申请是否能够得到批准为最后的决定条件，并不必然以申请时间的早晚决定谁享有该技术的专利权。" _mubu_note="%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E6%98%AF%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E4%BA%BA%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%97%B6%EF%BC%8C%E5%8D%B3%E4%BD%BF%E6%9C%89%E5%85%B6%E4%BB%96%E7%9A%84%E5%8D%95%E4%BD%8D%E5%92%8C%E4%B8%AA%E4%BA%BA%E5%B0%B1%E7%9B%B8%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E5%8F%91%E6%98%8E%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%AE%9E%E7%94%A8%E6%96%B0%E5%9E%8B%E5%85%88%E4%BA%8E%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E4%BA%BA%E6%8F%90%E5%87%BA%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%AA%E8%A6%81%E5%9C%A8%E5%85%88%E7%9A%84%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E6%9C%80%E5%90%8E%E6%B2%A1%E6%9C%89%E8%8E%B7%E5%BE%97%E6%89%B9%E5%87%86%EF%BC%8C%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E4%BA%BA%E4%BB%8D%E7%84%B6%E5%8F%AF%E8%83%BD%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E6%88%90%E5%8A%9F%E3%80%82%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E7%9A%84%E6%8A%80%E6%9C%AF%E6%98%AF%E5%90%A6%E4%B8%8E%E4%BB%96%E4%BA%BA%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E9%87%8D%E5%90%88%EF%BC%8C%E6%9C%89%E4%BB%96%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E6%98%AF%E5%90%A6%E8%83%BD%E5%A4%9F%E5%BE%97%E5%88%B0%E6%89%B9%E5%87%86%E4%B8%BA%E6%9C%80%E5%90%8E%E7%9A%84%E5%86%B3%E5%AE%9A%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%EF%BC%8C%E5%B9%B6%E4%B8%8D%E5%BF%85%E7%84%B6%E4%BB%A5%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E6%97%B6%E9%97%B4%E7%9A%84%E6%97%A9%E6%99%9A%E5%86%B3%E5%AE%9A%E8%B0%81%E4%BA%AB%E6%9C%89%E8%AF%A5%E6%8A%80%E6%9C%AF%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="申请专利的发明创造在申请日以前6个月内，有下列情形之一的，不丧失新颖性" _mubu_text="%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E7%9A%84%E5%8F%91%E6%98%8E%E5%88%9B%E9%80%A0%E5%9C%A8%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E6%97%A5%E4%BB%A5%E5%89%8D6%E4%B8%AA%E6%9C%88%E5%86%85%EF%BC%8C%E6%9C%89%E4%B8%8B%E5%88%97%E6%83%85%E5%BD%A2%E4%B9%8B%E4%B8%80%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%8D%E4%B8%A7%E5%A4%B1%E6%96%B0%E9%A2%96%E6%80%A7">

		<outline text="必须同申请日以前已有的技术相比有突出的实质性特点和显著的进步。" _mubu_text="%E5%BF%85%E9%A1%BB%E5%90%8C%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E6%97%A5%E4%BB%A5%E5%89%8D%E5%B7%B2%E6%9C%89%E7%9A%84%E6%8A%80%E6%9C%AF%E7%9B%B8%E6%AF%94%E6%9C%89%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E7%AA%81%E5%87%BA%E7%9A%84%3C/span%3E%E5%AE%9E%E8%B4%A8%E6%80%A7%E7%89%B9%E7%82%B9%E5%92%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%98%BE%E8%91%97%E7%9A%84%3C/span%3E%E8%BF%9B%E6%AD%A5%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="我国专利法对实用性的要求是，发明或者实用新型能够制造或者使用，并且能够产生积极效果。" _mubu_text="%E6%88%91%E5%9B%BD%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%B3%95%E5%AF%B9%E5%AE%9E%E7%94%A8%E6%80%A7%E7%9A%84%E8%A6%81%E6%B1%82%E6%98%AF%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%91%E6%98%8E%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%AE%9E%E7%94%A8%E6%96%B0%E5%9E%8B%E8%83%BD%E5%A4%9F%E5%88%B6%E9%80%A0%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%EF%BC%8C%E5%B9%B6%E4%B8%94%E8%83%BD%E5%A4%9F%E4%BA%A7%E7%94%9F%E7%A7%AF%E6%9E%81%E6%95%88%E6%9E%9C%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="2.授予外观设计专利权的实体条件" _mubu_text="2.%E6%8E%88%E4%BA%88%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%A4%96%E8%A7%82%E8%AE%BE%E8%AE%A1%3C/span%3E%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E5%AE%9E%E4%BD%93%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6">
		<outline text="（1）授予专利权的外观设计，应当不属于现有设计，也没有任何单位或者个人就同样的外观设计在申请日以前向国务院专利行政部门提出过申请，并记载在申请日以后公告的专利文件中。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E6%8E%88%E4%BA%88%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E5%A4%96%E8%A7%82%E8%AE%BE%E8%AE%A1%EF%BC%8C%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E4%B8%8D%E5%B1%9E%E4%BA%8E%E7%8E%B0%E6%9C%89%E8%AE%BE%E8%AE%A1%EF%BC%8C%E4%B9%9F%E6%B2%A1%E6%9C%89%E4%BB%BB%E4%BD%95%E5%8D%95%E4%BD%8D%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E4%B8%AA%E4%BA%BA%E5%B0%B1%E5%90%8C%E6%A0%B7%E7%9A%84%E5%A4%96%E8%A7%82%E8%AE%BE%E8%AE%A1%E5%9C%A8%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E6%97%A5%E4%BB%A5%E5%89%8D%E5%90%91%E5%9B%BD%E5%8A%A1%E9%99%A2%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E8%A1%8C%E6%94%BF%E9%83%A8%E9%97%A8%E6%8F%90%E5%87%BA%E8%BF%87%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%EF%BC%8C%E5%B9%B6%E8%AE%B0%E8%BD%BD%E5%9C%A8%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E6%97%A5%E4%BB%A5%E5%90%8E%E5%85%AC%E5%91%8A%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%96%87%E4%BB%B6%E4%B8%AD%E3%80%82" _note="现有设计，是指申请日以前在国内外为公众所知的设计。" _mubu_note="%E7%8E%B0%E6%9C%89%E8%AE%BE%E8%AE%A1%EF%BC%8C%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E6%97%A5%E4%BB%A5%E5%89%8D%E5%9C%A8%E5%9B%BD%E5%86%85%E5%A4%96%E4%B8%BA%E5%85%AC%E4%BC%97%E6%89%80%E7%9F%A5%E7%9A%84%E8%AE%BE%E8%AE%A1%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（2）授予专利的外观设计与现有设计或者现有设计特征的组合相比应当具有明显的区别，且不得与他人在申请日以前已经取得的合法利益相冲突。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%E6%8E%88%E4%BA%88%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E7%9A%84%E5%A4%96%E8%A7%82%E8%AE%BE%E8%AE%A1%E4%B8%8E%E7%8E%B0%E6%9C%89%E8%AE%BE%E8%AE%A1%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E7%8E%B0%E6%9C%89%E8%AE%BE%E8%AE%A1%E7%89%B9%E5%BE%81%E7%9A%84%E7%BB%84%E5%90%88%E7%9B%B8%E6%AF%94%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E5%85%B7%E6%9C%89%E6%98%8E%E6%98%BE%E7%9A%84%E5%8C%BA%E5%88%AB%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%94%E4%B8%8D%E5%BE%97%E4%B8%8E%E4%BB%96%E4%BA%BA%E5%9C%A8%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E6%97%A5%E4%BB%A5%E5%89%8D%E5%B7%B2%E7%BB%8F%E5%8F%96%E5%BE%97%E7%9A%84%E5%90%88%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E7%9B%B8%E5%86%B2%E7%AA%81%E3%80%82" _note="现有设计，是指申请日以前在国内外为公众所知的设计。" _mubu_note="%E7%8E%B0%E6%9C%89%E8%AE%BE%E8%AE%A1%EF%BC%8C%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E6%97%A5%E4%BB%A5%E5%89%8D%E5%9C%A8%E5%9B%BD%E5%86%85%E5%A4%96%E4%B8%BA%E5%85%AC%E4%BC%97%E6%89%80%E7%9F%A5%E7%9A%84%E8%AE%BE%E8%AE%A1%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>

		<outline text="程序条件" _mubu_text="%E7%A8%8B%E5%BA%8F%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6">
		<outline text="1.发明专利的申请程序条件" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E1.%E5%8F%91%E6%98%8E%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E7%9A%84%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E7%A8%8B%E5%BA%8F%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%3C/span%3E" _note="@简答题&nbsp;@题眼&nbsp;@口诀&nbsp;发力橙提出尸首" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E9%A2%98%E7%9C%BC%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E5%8F%91%E5%8A%9B%E6%A9%99%E6%8F%90%E5%87%BA%E5%B0%B8%E9%A6%96" _heading="1" _color="#dc2d1e">
		<outline text="（1）提交申请文件" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%8F%90%3C/span%3E%E4%BA%A4%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E6%96%87%E4%BB%B6">
		<outline text="根据《专利法》规定，申请专利的，应当提交请求书等申请文件。" _mubu_text="%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE%E3%80%8A%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%B3%95%E3%80%8B%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%EF%BC%8C%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E6%8F%90%E4%BA%A4%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%3E%E8%AF%B7%E6%B1%82%E4%B9%A6%3C/span%3E%E7%AD%89%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E6%96%87%E4%BB%B6%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="（2）初步审查并公布（18月或提前）" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%88%9D%3C/span%3E%E6%AD%A5%E5%AE%A1%E6%9F%A5%E5%B9%B6%E5%85%AC%E5%B8%83%EF%BC%8818%E6%9C%88%E6%88%96%E6%8F%90%E5%89%8D%EF%BC%89">
		<outline text="国务院专利行政部门收到发明专利申请后，经初步审查认为符合专利法要求的，自申请日起满18个月，即行公布，也可以根据申请人的请求早日公布。" _mubu_text="%E5%9B%BD%E5%8A%A1%E9%99%A2%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E8%A1%8C%E6%94%BF%E9%83%A8%E9%97%A8%E6%94%B6%E5%88%B0%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%8F%91%E6%98%8E%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E7%94%B3%3C/span%3E%E8%AF%B7%E5%90%8E%EF%BC%8C%E7%BB%8F%E5%88%9D%E6%AD%A5%E5%AE%A1%E6%9F%A5%E8%AE%A4%E4%B8%BA%E7%AC%A6%E5%90%88%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%B3%95%E8%A6%81%E6%B1%82%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E8%87%AA%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E6%97%A5%E8%B5%B7%E6%BB%A118%E4%B8%AA%E6%9C%88%EF%BC%8C%E5%8D%B3%E8%A1%8C%E5%85%AC%E5%B8%83%EF%BC%8C%E4%B9%9F%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E8%AF%B7%E6%B1%82%E6%97%A9%E6%97%A5%E5%85%AC%E5%B8%83%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="（3）实质审查（3年内）" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%3E%E5%AE%9E%3C/span%3E%E8%B4%A8%E5%AE%A1%E6%9F%A5%EF%BC%883%E5%B9%B4%E5%86%85%EF%BC%89">
		<outline text="发明专利申请自申请日起3年内，国务院专利行政部门可以根据申请人随时提出的请求，对其申请进行实质审查。" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%8F%91%E6%98%8E%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%3C/span%3E%E8%87%AA%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E6%97%A5%E8%B5%B73%E5%B9%B4%E5%86%85%EF%BC%8C%E5%9B%BD%E5%8A%A1%E9%99%A2%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E8%A1%8C%E6%94%BF%E9%83%A8%E9%97%A8%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E4%BA%BA%E9%9A%8F%E6%97%B6%E6%8F%90%E5%87%BA%E7%9A%84%E8%AF%B7%E6%B1%82%EF%BC%8C%E5%AF%B9%E5%85%B6%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E8%BF%9B%E8%A1%8C%E5%AE%9E%E8%B4%A8%E5%AE%A1%E6%9F%A5%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="国务院专利行政部门认为必要的时候，可以自行对发明专利申请进行实质审查。" _mubu_text="%E5%9B%BD%E5%8A%A1%E9%99%A2%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E8%A1%8C%E6%94%BF%E9%83%A8%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%A4%E4%B8%BA%E5%BF%85%E8%A6%81%E7%9A%84%E6%97%B6%E5%80%99%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E8%87%AA%E8%A1%8C%E5%AF%B9%E5%8F%91%E6%98%8E%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E8%BF%9B%E8%A1%8C%E5%AE%9E%E8%B4%A8%E5%AE%A1%E6%9F%A5%E3%80%82">
		</outline>

		<outline text="（4）授予发明专利证书并予以登记和公告" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%884%EF%BC%89%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%8E%88%3C/span%3E%E4%BA%88%E5%8F%91%E6%98%8E%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E8%AF%81%E4%B9%A6%E5%B9%B6%E4%BA%88%E4%BB%A5%E7%99%BB%E8%AE%B0%E5%92%8C%E5%85%AC%E5%91%8A">
		<outline text="专利申请经实质审查没有发现驳回理由的，由国务院专利行政部门作出授予发明专利权的决定，发给申请人发明专利证书，同时予以登记和公告。" _mubu_text="%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E7%BB%8F%E5%AE%9E%E8%B4%A8%E5%AE%A1%E6%9F%A5%E6%B2%A1%E6%9C%89%E5%8F%91%E7%8E%B0%E9%A9%B3%E5%9B%9E%E7%90%86%E7%94%B1%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E7%94%B1%E5%9B%BD%E5%8A%A1%E9%99%A2%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E8%A1%8C%E6%94%BF%E9%83%A8%E9%97%A8%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E6%8E%88%E4%BA%88%E5%8F%91%E6%98%8E%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E5%86%B3%E5%AE%9A%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%91%E7%BB%99%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%91%E6%98%8E%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E8%AF%81%E4%B9%A6%EF%BC%8C%E5%90%8C%E6%97%B6%E4%BA%88%E4%BB%A5%E7%99%BB%E8%AE%B0%E5%92%8C%E5%85%AC%E5%91%8A%E3%80%82">
		</outline>

		<outline text="（1）提交申请文件" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E6%8F%90%E4%BA%A4%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E6%96%87%E4%BB%B6">
		<outline text="根据《专利法》规定，申请专利的，应当提交请求书等申请文件。" _mubu_text="%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE%E3%80%8A%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%B3%95%E3%80%8B%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%EF%BC%8C%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E6%8F%90%E4%BA%A4%E8%AF%B7%E6%B1%82%E4%B9%A6%E7%AD%89%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E6%96%87%E4%BB%B6%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="实用新型或外观设计专利申请经初步审查没有发现驳回理由的，由国务院专利行政部门作出授予实用新型专利权或者外观设计专利权的决定，发给相应的专利证书，同时予以登记和公告。" _mubu_text="%E5%AE%9E%E7%94%A8%E6%96%B0%E5%9E%8B%E6%88%96%E5%A4%96%E8%A7%82%E8%AE%BE%E8%AE%A1%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E7%BB%8F%E5%88%9D%E6%AD%A5%E5%AE%A1%E6%9F%A5%E6%B2%A1%E6%9C%89%E5%8F%91%E7%8E%B0%E9%A9%B3%E5%9B%9E%E7%90%86%E7%94%B1%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E7%94%B1%E5%9B%BD%E5%8A%A1%E9%99%A2%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E8%A1%8C%E6%94%BF%E9%83%A8%E9%97%A8%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E6%8E%88%E4%BA%88%E5%AE%9E%E7%94%A8%E6%96%B0%E5%9E%8B%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%A4%96%E8%A7%82%E8%AE%BE%E8%AE%A1%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E5%86%B3%E5%AE%9A%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%91%E7%BB%99%E7%9B%B8%E5%BA%94%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E8%AF%81%E4%B9%A6%EF%BC%8C%E5%90%8C%E6%97%B6%E4%BA%88%E4%BB%A5%E7%99%BB%E8%AE%B0%E5%92%8C%E5%85%AC%E5%91%8A%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="针对专利的独占使用权的限制" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E9%92%88%E5%AF%B9%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E7%9A%84%E7%8B%AC%E5%8D%A0%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E9%99%90%E5%88%B6%3C/span%3E" _note="@口诀&nbsp;专线时空强步师&nbsp;@简答题" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E4%B8%93%E7%BA%BF%E6%97%B6%E7%A9%BA%E5%BC%BA%E6%AD%A5%E5%B8%88&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E" _heading="1" _color="#dc2d1e">
		<outline text="（1）时间限制" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E6%97%B6%E9%97%B4%E9%99%90%E5%88%B6">
		<outline text="专利权有法定保护期间。" _mubu_text="%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E6%9C%89%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E4%BF%9D%E6%8A%A4%E6%9C%9F%E9%97%B4%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>

		<outline text="仅在申请国内可以行使专利权。" _mubu_text="%E4%BB%85%E5%9C%A8%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E5%9B%BD%E5%86%85%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E8%A1%8C%E4%BD%BF%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E3%80%82">
		</outline>

		<outline text="（3）专利权的行使还受到公共利益的限制，具体表现为：" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E8%A1%8C%E4%BD%BF%E8%BF%98%E5%8F%97%E5%88%B0%E5%85%AC%E5%85%B1%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E7%9A%84%E9%99%90%E5%88%B6%EF%BC%8C%E5%85%B7%E4%BD%93%E8%A1%A8%E7%8E%B0%E4%B8%BA%EF%BC%9A">
		<outline text="（一）强制许可" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%88%E4%B8%80%EF%BC%89%E5%BC%BA%E5%88%B6%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF">
		<outline text="强制许可的概念" _mubu_text="%E5%BC%BA%E5%88%B6%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="强制许可是指国家专利主管机关根据具体情况不经专利权人许可，授权符合法定条件的申请人实施专利的法定制度。" _mubu_text="%E5%BC%BA%E5%88%B6%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%3E%E5%9B%BD%E5%AE%B6%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E4%B8%BB%E7%AE%A1%E6%9C%BA%E5%85%B3%3C/span%3E%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE%E5%85%B7%E4%BD%93%E6%83%85%E5%86%B5%E4%B8%8D%E7%BB%8F%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%EF%BC%8C%E6%8E%88%E6%9D%83%E7%AC%A6%E5%90%88%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E7%9A%84%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E4%BA%BA%E5%AE%9E%E6%96%BD%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E7%9A%84%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E5%88%B6%E5%BA%A6%E3%80%82" _note="@必须掌握的概念" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%BF%85%E9%A1%BB%E6%8E%8C%E6%8F%A1%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		<outline text="强制许可违反专利权人的意志，又称为非自愿许可。强制许可与保护专利权之间是相冲突的，所以对强制许可的申请条件规定十分严格。" _mubu_text="%E5%BC%BA%E5%88%B6%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E8%BF%9D%E5%8F%8D%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%84%8F%E5%BF%97%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%8F%88%E7%A7%B0%E4%B8%BA%E9%9D%9E%E8%87%AA%E6%84%BF%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E%E5%BC%BA%E5%88%B6%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E4%B8%8E%E4%BF%9D%E6%8A%A4%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E4%B9%8B%E9%97%B4%E6%98%AF%E7%9B%B8%E5%86%B2%E7%AA%81%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E6%89%80%E4%BB%A5%E5%AF%B9%E5%BC%BA%E5%88%B6%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E7%9A%84%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E5%8D%81%E5%88%86%E4%B8%A5%E6%A0%BC%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="在我国按照产生原因的不同，强制许可有三种类型：" _mubu_text="%E5%9C%A8%E6%88%91%E5%9B%BD%E6%8C%89%E7%85%A7%E4%BA%A7%E7%94%9F%E5%8E%9F%E5%9B%A0%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%8D%E5%90%8C%EF%BC%8C%E5%BC%BA%E5%88%B6%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E6%9C%89%E4%B8%89%E7%A7%8D%E7%B1%BB%E5%9E%8B%EF%BC%9A">
		<outline text="①普通强制许可" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E2%91%A0%E6%99%AE%E9%80%9A%E5%BC%BA%E5%88%B6%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%3C/span%3E" _note="@口诀&nbsp;普强垄断收伞深思不使用&nbsp;@简答题" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E6%99%AE%E5%BC%BA%E5%9E%84%E6%96%AD%E6%94%B6%E4%BC%9E%E6%B7%B1%E6%80%9D%E4%B8%8D%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E" _heading="1" _color="#3da8f5">
		<outline text="实施普通强制许可的原因" _mubu_text="%E5%AE%9E%E6%96%BD%E6%99%AE%E9%80%9A%E5%BC%BA%E5%88%B6%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E7%9A%84%E5%8E%9F%E5%9B%A0" _note="@关键词追求利益最大化，专利权滥用" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%85%B3%E9%94%AE%E8%AF%8D%3C/span%3E%E8%BF%BD%E6%B1%82%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E6%9C%80%E5%A4%A7%E5%8C%96%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E6%BB%A5%E7%94%A8">
		<outline text="专利权是独占权，专利权人可以自由决定是否许可他人实施专利，但在有些情况下专利权人在追求自身利益最大化时，可能会滥用这种独占权，普通强制许可是为防止专利权人滥用其专利权，法律规定可以对符合条件的专利实施的强制许可。" _mubu_text="%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E6%98%AF%E7%8B%AC%E5%8D%A0%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E8%87%AA%E7%94%B1%E5%86%B3%E5%AE%9A%E6%98%AF%E5%90%A6%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%96%E4%BA%BA%E5%AE%9E%E6%96%BD%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E4%BD%86%E5%9C%A8%E6%9C%89%E4%BA%9B%E6%83%85%E5%86%B5%E4%B8%8B%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E5%9C%A8%E8%BF%BD%E6%B1%82%E8%87%AA%E8%BA%AB%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E6%9C%80%E5%A4%A7%E5%8C%96%E6%97%B6%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%AF%E8%83%BD%E4%BC%9A%E6%BB%A5%E7%94%A8%E8%BF%99%E7%A7%8D%E7%8B%AC%E5%8D%A0%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%8C%E6%99%AE%E9%80%9A%E5%BC%BA%E5%88%B6%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E6%98%AF%E4%B8%BA%E9%98%B2%E6%AD%A2%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E6%BB%A5%E7%94%A8%E5%85%B6%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%8C%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E5%AF%B9%E7%AC%A6%E5%90%88%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E5%AE%9E%E6%96%BD%E7%9A%84%E5%BC%BA%E5%88%B6%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="专利法第48条规定有下列情形之一的，国务院专利行政部门根据具备实施条件的单位或者个人的申请，可以给予实施发明专利或者实用新型专利的强制许可。" _mubu_text="%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%B3%95%E7%AC%AC48%E6%9D%A1%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E6%9C%89%E4%B8%8B%E5%88%97%E6%83%85%E5%BD%A2%E4%B9%8B%E4%B8%80%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E5%9B%BD%E5%8A%A1%E9%99%A2%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E8%A1%8C%E6%94%BF%E9%83%A8%E9%97%A8%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE%E5%85%B7%E5%A4%87%E5%AE%9E%E6%96%BD%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E7%9A%84%E5%8D%95%E4%BD%8D%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E4%B8%AA%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E7%BB%99%E4%BA%88%E5%AE%9E%E6%96%BD%E5%8F%91%E6%98%8E%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%AE%9E%E7%94%A8%E6%96%B0%E5%9E%8B%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E7%9A%84%E5%BC%BA%E5%88%B6%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="1）专利权人自专利权被授予之日起满三年，且自提出专利申请之日起满四年，无正当理由未实施或者未充分实施其专利的。" _mubu_text="1%EF%BC%89%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E8%87%AA%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E8%A2%AB%E6%8E%88%E4%BA%88%E4%B9%8B%E6%97%A5%E8%B5%B7%E6%BB%A1%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%94%E8%87%AA%E6%8F%90%E5%87%BA%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E4%B9%8B%E6%97%A5%E8%B5%B7%E6%BB%A1%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4%EF%BC%8C%E6%97%A0%E6%AD%A3%E5%BD%93%E7%90%86%E7%94%B1%E6%9C%AA%E5%AE%9E%E6%96%BD%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E6%9C%AA%E5%85%85%E5%88%86%E5%AE%9E%E6%96%BD%E5%85%B6%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E7%9A%84%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="未充分实施是指专利权人及其被许可人实施其专利的方式或者规模不能满足国内对专利产品或专利方法的需求" _mubu_text="%E6%9C%AA%E5%85%85%E5%88%86%E5%AE%9E%E6%96%BD%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%8A%E5%85%B6%E8%A2%AB%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E4%BA%BA%E5%AE%9E%E6%96%BD%E5%85%B6%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E7%9A%84%E6%96%B9%E5%BC%8F%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E8%A7%84%E6%A8%A1%E4%B8%8D%E8%83%BD%E6%BB%A1%E8%B6%B3%E5%9B%BD%E5%86%85%E5%AF%B9%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E4%BA%A7%E5%93%81%E6%88%96%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%96%B9%E6%B3%95%E7%9A%84%E9%9C%80%E6%B1%82" _note="@法条分析" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E6%B3%95%E6%9D%A1%E5%88%86%E6%9E%90%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="2）专利权人行使专利权的行为被依法认定为垄断行为，为消除或者减少该行为对竞争产生的不利影响，而实施的强制许可。" _mubu_text="2%EF%BC%89%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E8%A1%8C%E4%BD%BF%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E8%A2%AB%E4%BE%9D%E6%B3%95%E8%AE%A4%E5%AE%9A%E4%B8%BA%E5%9E%84%E6%96%AD%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%BA%E6%B6%88%E9%99%A4%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%87%8F%E5%B0%91%E8%AF%A5%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E5%AF%B9%E7%AB%9E%E4%BA%89%E4%BA%A7%E7%94%9F%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%8D%E5%88%A9%E5%BD%B1%E5%93%8D%EF%BC%8C%E8%80%8C%E5%AE%9E%E6%96%BD%E7%9A%84%E5%BC%BA%E5%88%B6%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="②交叉强制许可（的情形）" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E2%91%A1%E4%BA%A4%E5%8F%89%E5%BC%BA%E5%88%B6%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%EF%BC%88%E7%9A%84%E6%83%85%E5%BD%A2%EF%BC%89%3C/span%3E" _note="@口诀&nbsp;胶墙厚显重大&nbsp;@简答题" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E8%83%B6%E5%A2%99%E5%8E%9A%E6%98%BE%E9%87%8D%E5%A4%A7&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E" _heading="1" _color="#3da8f5">
		<outline text="该制度的设计主要是为了“依存专利”的实施。" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E8%AF%A5%E5%88%B6%E5%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E8%AE%BE%E8%AE%A1%E4%B8%BB%E8%A6%81%E6%98%AF%E4%B8%BA%E4%BA%86%E2%80%9C%E4%BE%9D%E5%AD%98%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E2%80%9D%E7%9A%84%E5%AE%9E%E6%96%BD%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		<outline text="所谓“依存专利”是指后​一专利的实施以前一专利的实施为前提，如不实施前一专利，则后一专利也无法实施。" _mubu_text="%E6%89%80%E8%B0%93%E2%80%9C%E4%BE%9D%E5%AD%98%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E2%80%9D%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%90%8E%E2%80%8B%E4%B8%80%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E7%9A%84%E5%AE%9E%E6%96%BD%E4%BB%A5%E5%89%8D%E4%B8%80%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E7%9A%84%E5%AE%9E%E6%96%BD%E4%B8%BA%E5%89%8D%E6%8F%90%EF%BC%8C%E5%A6%82%E4%B8%8D%E5%AE%9E%E6%96%BD%E5%89%8D%E4%B8%80%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%EF%BC%8C%E5%88%99%E5%90%8E%E4%B8%80%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E4%B9%9F%E6%97%A0%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9E%E6%96%BD%E3%80%82" _note="@必须掌握的概念" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%BF%85%E9%A1%BB%E6%8E%8C%E6%8F%A1%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="一项取得专利权的发明或者实用新型比前已取得专利权的发明或者实用新型具有显著经济意义的重大技术进步，其实施又有赖于前一发明或者实用新型实施的，国务院专利行政部门根据后一专利权人的申请，可以给予实施前一发明或者实用新型的强制许可。此类型强制许可的申请一般由后一专利的专利权人提出，而前一专利的专利权人在自己的专利技术被强制许可给后一专利权人之后，还可以申请使用后一专利技术的强制许可。" 		</outline>
		<outline text="③以公共利益为目的的强制许可（的情形）" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E2%91%A2%E4%BB%A5%E5%85%AC%E5%85%B1%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E4%B8%BA%E7%9B%AE%E7%9A%84%E7%9A%84%E5%BC%BA%E5%88%B6%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%EF%BC%88%E7%9A%84%E6%83%85%E5%BD%A2%EF%BC%89%3C/span%3E" _note="这种强制许可没有时间限制，也不需要申请。&nbsp;@口诀&nbsp;攻强国金工件&nbsp;@简答题" _mubu_note="%E8%BF%99%E7%A7%8D%E5%BC%BA%E5%88%B6%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E6%B2%A1%E6%9C%89%E6%97%B6%E9%97%B4%E9%99%90%E5%88%B6%EF%BC%8C%E4%B9%9F%E4%B8%8D%E9%9C%80%E8%A6%81%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E3%80%82&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E6%94%BB%E5%BC%BA%E5%9B%BD%E9%87%91%E5%B7%A5%E4%BB%B6&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E" _heading="1" _color="#3da8f5">
		<outline text="1）在国家出现紧急状态或者非常情况时，为了公共利益的目的，国务院专利行政部门可以给予实施发明专利或者实用新型专利的强制许可。" _mubu_text="1%EF%BC%89%E5%9C%A8%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%9B%BD%3C/span%3E%E5%AE%B6%E5%87%BA%E7%8E%B0%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E7%B4%A7%3C/span%3E%E6%80%A5%E7%8A%B6%E6%80%81%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E9%9D%9E%E5%B8%B8%E6%83%85%E5%86%B5%E6%97%B6%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%BA%E4%BA%86%E5%85%AC%E5%85%B1%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E7%9A%84%E7%9B%AE%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E5%9B%BD%E5%8A%A1%E9%99%A2%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E8%A1%8C%E6%94%BF%E9%83%A8%E9%97%A8%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E7%BB%99%E4%BA%88%E5%AE%9E%E6%96%BD%E5%8F%91%E6%98%8E%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%AE%9E%E7%94%A8%E6%96%B0%E5%9E%8B%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E7%9A%84%E5%BC%BA%E5%88%B6%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E3%80%82" _note="国金：国家出现紧急状态或者非常状态" _mubu_note="%E5%9B%BD%E9%87%91%EF%BC%9A%E5%9B%BD%E5%AE%B6%E5%87%BA%E7%8E%B0%E7%B4%A7%E6%80%A5%E7%8A%B6%E6%80%81%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E9%9D%9E%E5%B8%B8%E7%8A%B6%E6%80%81">

		<outline text="2）为了公共健康目的，对取得专利权的药品，国务院专利行政部门可以给予制造并将其出口到符合我国参加的有关国际条约规定的国家或者地区的强制许可。" _mubu_text="2%EF%BC%89%E4%B8%BA%E4%BA%86%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%85%AC%3C/span%3E%E5%85%B1%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%81%A5%3C/span%3E%E5%BA%B7%E7%9B%AE%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E5%AF%B9%E5%8F%96%E5%BE%97%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E8%8D%AF%E5%93%81%EF%BC%8C%E5%9B%BD%E5%8A%A1%E9%99%A2%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E8%A1%8C%E6%94%BF%E9%83%A8%E9%97%A8%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E7%BB%99%E4%BA%88%E5%88%B6%E9%80%A0%E5%B9%B6%E5%B0%86%E5%85%B6%E5%87%BA%E5%8F%A3%E5%88%B0%E7%AC%A6%E5%90%88%E6%88%91%E5%9B%BD%E5%8F%82%E5%8A%A0%E7%9A%84%E6%9C%89%E5%85%B3%E5%9B%BD%E9%99%85%E6%9D%A1%E7%BA%A6%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E5%9B%BD%E5%AE%B6%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%9C%B0%E5%8C%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%BC%BA%E5%88%B6%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E3%80%82" _note="工件：为了公共健康的目的" _mubu_note="%E5%B7%A5%E4%BB%B6%EF%BC%9A%E4%B8%BA%E4%BA%86%E5%85%AC%E5%85%B1%E5%81%A5%E5%BA%B7%E7%9A%84%E7%9B%AE%E7%9A%84">

		<outline text="强制许可的实施" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%BC%BA%E5%88%B6%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E7%9A%84%E5%AE%9E%E6%96%BD%3C/span%3E" _note="@口诀&nbsp;强势身正示范灯不沾付费@简答题&nbsp;3＋1" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E5%BC%BA%E5%8A%BF%E8%BA%AB%E6%AD%A3%E7%A4%BA%E8%8C%83%E7%81%AF%E4%B8%8D%E6%B2%BE%E4%BB%98%E8%B4%B9@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98&amp;nbsp;3%EF%BC%8B1" _heading="1" _color="#3da8f5">
		<outline text="（1）申请普通强制许可中的第一类（长期无理由未实施其专利）和交叉强制许可的单位或者个人，必须提交书面申请书以及必要的证据，证明其以合理的条件请求专利权人许可其实施专利，但未能在合理的时间内获得许可。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E6%99%AE%E9%80%9A%E5%BC%BA%E5%88%B6%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E4%B8%AD%E7%9A%84%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%80%E7%B1%BB%EF%BC%88%E9%95%BF%E6%9C%9F%E6%97%A0%E7%90%86%E7%94%B1%E6%9C%AA%E5%AE%9E%E6%96%BD%E5%85%B6%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%EF%BC%89%E5%92%8C%E4%BA%A4%E5%8F%89%E5%BC%BA%E5%88%B6%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E7%9A%84%E5%8D%95%E4%BD%8D%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E4%B8%AA%E4%BA%BA%EF%BC%8C%E5%BF%85%E9%A1%BB%E6%8F%90%E4%BA%A4%E4%B9%A6%E9%9D%A2%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E4%B9%A6%E4%BB%A5%E5%8F%8A%E5%BF%85%E8%A6%81%E7%9A%84%E8%AF%81%E6%8D%AE%EF%BC%8C%E8%AF%81%E6%98%8E%E5%85%B6%E4%BB%A5%E5%90%88%E7%90%86%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E8%AF%B7%E6%B1%82%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E5%85%B6%E5%AE%9E%E6%96%BD%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%EF%BC%8C%E4%BD%86%E6%9C%AA%E8%83%BD%E5%9C%A8%E5%90%88%E7%90%86%E7%9A%84%E6%97%B6%E9%97%B4%E5%86%85%E8%8E%B7%E5%BE%97%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E3%80%82" _note="身正：书面申请书、必要的证据" _mubu_note="%E8%BA%AB%E6%AD%A3%EF%BC%9A%E4%B9%A6%E9%9D%A2%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E4%B9%A6%E3%80%81%E5%BF%85%E8%A6%81%E7%9A%84%E8%AF%81%E6%8D%AE">

		<outline text="（3）取得实施强制许可的单位或者个人不享有独占实施权，且无权允许他人实施，同时还应该付给专利权人合理的使用费。" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%E5%8F%96%E5%BE%97%E5%AE%9E%E6%96%BD%E5%BC%BA%E5%88%B6%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E7%9A%84%E5%8D%95%E4%BD%8D%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E4%B8%AA%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%8D%E4%BA%AB%E6%9C%89%E7%8B%AC%E5%8D%A0%E5%AE%9E%E6%96%BD%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%94%E6%97%A0%E6%9D%83%E5%85%81%E8%AE%B8%E4%BB%96%E4%BA%BA%E5%AE%9E%E6%96%BD%3C/span%3E%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%90%8C%E6%97%B6%E8%BF%98%E5%BA%94%E8%AF%A5%E4%BB%98%E7%BB%99%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E5%90%88%E7%90%86%E7%9A%84%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E8%B4%B9%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E" _note="不沾付费：不享有独占实施权，付给专利权人合理的费用。" _mubu_note="%E4%B8%8D%E6%B2%BE%E4%BB%98%E8%B4%B9%EF%BC%9A%E4%B8%8D%E4%BA%AB%E6%9C%89%E7%8B%AC%E5%8D%A0%E5%AE%9E%E6%96%BD%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%8C%E4%BB%98%E7%BB%99%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E5%90%88%E7%90%86%E7%9A%84%E8%B4%B9%E7%94%A8%E3%80%82">

		</outline>
		<outline text="（3）临时过境的外国运输工具的使用。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%E4%B8%B4%E6%97%B6%E8%BF%87%E5%A2%83%E7%9A%84%E5%A4%96%E5%9B%BD%E8%BF%90%E8%BE%93%E5%B7%A5%E5%85%B7%E7%9A%84%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E3%80%82" _note="林：临事过境" _mubu_note="%E6%9E%97%EF%BC%9A%E4%B8%B4%E4%BA%8B%E8%BF%87%E5%A2%83">
		<outline text="临时通过中国领陆、领水、领空的外国运输工具，依照其所属国同中国签订的协议或者共同参加的国际条约，或者依照互惠原则，为运输工具自身需要，而在其装置和设备中使用有关专利的行为，不视为侵犯专利权。" _mubu_text="%E4%B8%B4%E6%97%B6%E9%80%9A%E8%BF%87%E4%B8%AD%E5%9B%BD%E9%A2%86%E9%99%86%E3%80%81%E9%A2%86%E6%B0%B4%E3%80%81%E9%A2%86%E7%A9%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%A4%96%E5%9B%BD%E8%BF%90%E8%BE%93%E5%B7%A5%E5%85%B7%EF%BC%8C%E4%BE%9D%E7%85%A7%E5%85%B6%E6%89%80%E5%B1%9E%E5%9B%BD%E5%90%8C%E4%B8%AD%E5%9B%BD%E7%AD%BE%E8%AE%A2%E7%9A%84%E5%8D%8F%E8%AE%AE%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%85%B1%E5%90%8C%E5%8F%82%E5%8A%A0%E7%9A%84%E5%9B%BD%E9%99%85%E6%9D%A1%E7%BA%A6%EF%BC%8C%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E4%BE%9D%E7%85%A7%E4%BA%92%E6%83%A0%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%BA%E8%BF%90%E8%BE%93%E5%B7%A5%E5%85%B7%E8%87%AA%E8%BA%AB%E9%9C%80%E8%A6%81%EF%BC%8C%E8%80%8C%E5%9C%A8%E5%85%B6%E8%A3%85%E7%BD%AE%E5%92%8C%E8%AE%BE%E5%A4%87%E4%B8%AD%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E6%9C%89%E5%85%B3%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E7%9A%84%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%8D%E8%A7%86%E4%B8%BA%E4%BE%B5%E7%8A%AF%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="（4）以科学研究为目的的使用。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%884%EF%BC%89%E4%BB%A5%E7%A7%91%E5%AD%A6%E7%A0%94%E7%A9%B6%E4%B8%BA%E7%9B%AE%E7%9A%84%E7%9A%84%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E3%80%82" _note="可：科学研究" _mubu_note="%E5%8F%AF%EF%BC%9A%E7%A7%91%E5%AD%A6%E7%A0%94%E7%A9%B6">
		<outline text="专为科学研究和实验，而使用有关专利的行为，不视为侵犯专利权。" _mubu_text="%E4%B8%93%E4%B8%BA%E7%A7%91%E5%AD%A6%E7%A0%94%E7%A9%B6%E5%92%8C%E5%AE%9E%E9%AA%8C%EF%BC%8C%E8%80%8C%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E6%9C%89%E5%85%B3%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E7%9A%84%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%8D%E8%A7%86%E4%B8%BA%E4%BE%B5%E7%8A%AF%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E3%80%82">
		</outline>

		<outline text="（5）以医药与医疗器械的行政审批为目的的使用。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%885%EF%BC%89%E4%BB%A5%E5%8C%BB%E8%8D%AF%E4%B8%8E%E5%8C%BB%E7%96%97%E5%99%A8%E6%A2%B0%E7%9A%84%E8%A1%8C%E6%94%BF%E5%AE%A1%E6%89%B9%E4%B8%BA%E7%9B%AE%E7%9A%84%E7%9A%84%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E3%80%82" _note="以：医药、医疗器械" _mubu_note="%E4%BB%A5%EF%BC%9A%E5%8C%BB%E8%8D%AF%E3%80%81%E5%8C%BB%E7%96%97%E5%99%A8%E6%A2%B0">
		<outline text="为提供行政审批所需要的信息，制造、使用、进口专利药品或者专利医疗器械的，以及专门为其制造进口专利药品或专利医疗器械的行为，不视为侵犯专利权。" _mubu_text="%E4%B8%BA%E6%8F%90%E4%BE%9B%E8%A1%8C%E6%94%BF%E5%AE%A1%E6%89%B9%E6%89%80%E9%9C%80%E8%A6%81%E7%9A%84%E4%BF%A1%E6%81%AF%EF%BC%8C%E5%88%B6%E9%80%A0%E3%80%81%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E3%80%81%E8%BF%9B%E5%8F%A3%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E8%8D%AF%E5%93%81%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E5%8C%BB%E7%96%97%E5%99%A8%E6%A2%B0%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E4%BB%A5%E5%8F%8A%E4%B8%93%E9%97%A8%E4%B8%BA%E5%85%B6%E5%88%B6%E9%80%A0%E8%BF%9B%E5%8F%A3%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E8%8D%AF%E5%93%81%E6%88%96%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E5%8C%BB%E7%96%97%E5%99%A8%E6%A2%B0%E7%9A%84%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%8D%E8%A7%86%E4%B8%BA%E4%BE%B5%E7%8A%AF%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="5月10日" _mubu_text="5%E6%9C%8810%E6%97%A5">
		<outline text="301.简述对专利权的保护❶" _mubu_text="301.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E5%AF%B9%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E4%BF%9D%E6%8A%A4%E2%9D%B6">
		<outline text="专利权的保护范围" _mubu_text="%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E4%BF%9D%E6%8A%A4%E8%8C%83%E5%9B%B4">
		<outline text="（1）发明或者实用新型专利权的保护范围，以其权利要求的内容为准，说明书及附图可以用于解释权利要求。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E5%8F%91%E6%98%8E%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%AE%9E%E7%94%A8%E6%96%B0%E5%9E%8B%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E4%BF%9D%E6%8A%A4%E8%8C%83%E5%9B%B4%EF%BC%8C%E4%BB%A5%E5%85%B6%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%3E%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E8%A6%81%E6%B1%82%E7%9A%84%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%3C/span%3E%E4%B8%BA%E5%87%86%EF%BC%8C%E8%AF%B4%E6%98%8E%E4%B9%A6%E5%8F%8A%E9%99%84%E5%9B%BE%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E7%94%A8%E4%BA%8E%E8%A7%A3%E9%87%8A%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E8%A6%81%E6%B1%82%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（2）外观设计专利权的保护范围，以表示在图片或者照片中的该外观设计专利产品为准，简要说明可以用于解释图片或者照片所表示的该产品的外观设计。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%E5%A4%96%E8%A7%82%E8%AE%BE%E8%AE%A1%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E4%BF%9D%E6%8A%A4%E8%8C%83%E5%9B%B4%EF%BC%8C%E4%BB%A5%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E5%9C%A8%E5%9B%BE%E7%89%87%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E7%85%A7%E7%89%87%E4%B8%AD%E7%9A%84%E8%AF%A5%E5%A4%96%E8%A7%82%E8%AE%BE%E8%AE%A1%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E4%BA%A7%E5%93%81%E4%B8%BA%E5%87%86%EF%BC%8C%E7%AE%80%E8%A6%81%E8%AF%B4%E6%98%8E%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E7%94%A8%E4%BA%8E%E8%A7%A3%E9%87%8A%E5%9B%BE%E7%89%87%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E7%85%A7%E7%89%87%E6%89%80%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E7%9A%84%E8%AF%A5%E4%BA%A7%E5%93%81%E7%9A%84%E5%A4%96%E8%A7%82%E8%AE%BE%E8%AE%A1%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="侵犯专利权的情形及专利权的保护方式" _mubu_text="%E4%BE%B5%E7%8A%AF%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E6%83%85%E5%BD%A2%E5%8F%8A%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E4%BF%9D%E6%8A%A4%E6%96%B9%E5%BC%8F">
		<outline text="侵犯专利权的情形" _mubu_text="%E4%BE%B5%E7%8A%AF%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E6%83%85%E5%BD%A2">
		<outline text="（1）根据《专利法》的规定，发明和实用新型专利权被授予后，除另有规定的以外，他人未经专利权人许可，为生产经营目的制造、使用、许诺销售、销售、进口其专利产品，或者使用其专利方法以及使用、许诺销售、销售、进口依照该专利方法直接获得的产品，均构成侵权;（针对专利产品和专利方法两个方面）" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE%E3%80%8A%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%B3%95%E3%80%8B%E7%9A%84%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%8F%91%E6%98%8E%E5%92%8C%E5%AE%9E%E7%94%A8%E6%96%B0%E5%9E%8B%3C/span%3E%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E8%A2%AB%E6%8E%88%E4%BA%88%E5%90%8E%EF%BC%8C%E9%99%A4%E5%8F%A6%E6%9C%89%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E4%BB%A5%E5%A4%96%EF%BC%8C%E4%BB%96%E4%BA%BA%E6%9C%AA%E7%BB%8F%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E4%B8%BA%E7%94%9F%E4%BA%A7%E7%BB%8F%E8%90%A5%E7%9B%AE%E7%9A%84%3C/span%3E%E5%88%B6%E9%80%A0%E3%80%81%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E3%80%81%E8%AE%B8%E8%AF%BA%E9%94%80%E5%94%AE%E3%80%81%E9%94%80%E5%94%AE%E3%80%81%E8%BF%9B%E5%8F%A3%E5%85%B6%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E4%BA%A7%E5%93%81%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E5%85%B6%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%96%B9%E6%B3%95%E4%BB%A5%E5%8F%8A%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E3%80%81%E8%AE%B8%E8%AF%BA%E9%94%80%E5%94%AE%E3%80%81%E9%94%80%E5%94%AE%E3%80%81%E8%BF%9B%E5%8F%A3%E4%BE%9D%E7%85%A7%E8%AF%A5%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%96%B9%E6%B3%95%E7%9B%B4%E6%8E%A5%E8%8E%B7%E5%BE%97%E7%9A%84%E4%BA%A7%E5%93%81%EF%BC%8C%E5%9D%87%E6%9E%84%E6%88%90%E4%BE%B5%E6%9D%83;%EF%BC%88%E9%92%88%E5%AF%B9%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E4%BA%A7%E5%93%81%E5%92%8C%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%96%B9%E6%B3%95%E4%B8%A4%E4%B8%AA%E6%96%B9%E9%9D%A2%EF%BC%89%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（2）外观设计专利权被授予后，他人未经专利权人许可，为生产经营目的制造、许诺销售、销售、进口其外观设计专利产品，同样构成侵权。（只针对专利产品）" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%A4%96%E8%A7%82%E8%AE%BE%E8%AE%A1%3C/span%3E%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E8%A2%AB%E6%8E%88%E4%BA%88%E5%90%8E%EF%BC%8C%E4%BB%96%E4%BA%BA%E6%9C%AA%E7%BB%8F%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E4%B8%BA%E7%94%9F%E4%BA%A7%E7%BB%8F%E8%90%A5%E7%9B%AE%E7%9A%84%3C/span%3E%E5%88%B6%E9%80%A0%E3%80%81%E8%AE%B8%E8%AF%BA%E9%94%80%E5%94%AE%E3%80%81%E9%94%80%E5%94%AE%E3%80%81%E8%BF%9B%E5%8F%A3%E5%85%B6%E5%A4%96%E8%A7%82%E8%AE%BE%E8%AE%A1%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E4%BA%A7%E5%93%81%EF%BC%8C%E5%90%8C%E6%A0%B7%E6%9E%84%E6%88%90%E4%BE%B5%E6%9D%83%E3%80%82%EF%BC%88%E5%8F%AA%E9%92%88%E5%AF%B9%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E4%BA%A7%E5%93%81%EF%BC%89">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="专利权的保护方式" _mubu_text="%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E4%BF%9D%E6%8A%A4%E6%96%B9%E5%BC%8F">
		<outline text="专利权人或者利害关系人在专利权受到不法侵害时，可以请求专利管理机关进行处理，也可以直接向人民法院提起诉讼。" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%3E%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%88%A9%E5%AE%B3%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E4%BA%BA%3C/span%3E%E5%9C%A8%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E6%9D%83%E5%8F%97%E5%88%B0%E4%B8%8D%E6%B3%95%E4%BE%B5%E5%AE%B3%E6%97%B6%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E8%AF%B7%E6%B1%82%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%3E%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E6%9C%BA%E5%85%B3%3C/span%3E%E8%BF%9B%E8%A1%8C%E5%A4%84%E7%90%86%EF%BC%8C%E4%B9%9F%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E7%9B%B4%E6%8E%A5%E5%90%91%E4%BA%BA%E6%B0%91%E6%B3%95%E9%99%A2%E6%8F%90%E8%B5%B7%E8%AF%89%E8%AE%BC%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="（1）专利管理机关处理时，认定侵权行为成立的，可以责令侵权人立即停止侵权行为。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E4%B8%93%E5%88%A9%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E6%9C%BA%E5%85%B3%E5%A4%84%E7%90%86%E6%97%B6%EF%BC%8C%E8%AE%A4%E5%AE%9A%E4%BE%B5%E6%9D%83%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E8%B4%A3%E4%BB%A4%E4%BE%B5%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E7%AB%8B%E5%8D%B3%E5%81%9C%E6%AD%A2%E4%BE%B5%E6%9D%83%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="（1）同中华人民共和国的国家名称、国旗、国徽、国歌、军旗、军徽、军歌、军勋章等相同或者近似的以及同中央国家机关的名称、标志、所在地特定地点的名称或者标志性建筑物的名称、图形相同的。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E5%90%8C%E4%B8%AD%E5%8D%8E%E4%BA%BA%E6%B0%91%E5%85%B1%E5%92%8C%E5%9B%BD%E7%9A%84%E5%9B%BD%E5%AE%B6%E5%90%8D%E7%A7%B0%E3%80%81%E5%9B%BD%E6%97%97%E3%80%81%E5%9B%BD%E5%BE%BD%E3%80%81%E5%9B%BD%E6%AD%8C%E3%80%81%E5%86%9B%E6%97%97%E3%80%81%E5%86%9B%E5%BE%BD%E3%80%81%E5%86%9B%E6%AD%8C%E3%80%81%E5%86%9B%E5%8B%8B%E7%AB%A0%E7%AD%89%E7%9B%B8%E5%90%8C%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E8%BF%91%E4%BC%BC%E7%9A%84%E4%BB%A5%E5%8F%8A%E5%90%8C%E4%B8%AD%E5%A4%AE%E5%9B%BD%E5%AE%B6%E6%9C%BA%E5%85%B3%E7%9A%84%E5%90%8D%E7%A7%B0%E3%80%81%E6%A0%87%E5%BF%97%E3%80%81%E6%89%80%E5%9C%A8%E5%9C%B0%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E5%9C%B0%E7%82%B9%E7%9A%84%E5%90%8D%E7%A7%B0%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E6%A0%87%E5%BF%97%E6%80%A7%E5%BB%BA%E7%AD%91%E7%89%A9%E7%9A%84%E5%90%8D%E7%A7%B0%E3%80%81%E5%9B%BE%E5%BD%A2%E7%9B%B8%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E3%80%82" _note="中：中华人民共和国、中央国家机关" _mubu_note="%E4%B8%AD%EF%BC%9A%E4%B8%AD%E5%8D%8E%E4%BA%BA%E6%B0%91%E5%85%B1%E5%92%8C%E5%9B%BD%E3%80%81%E4%B8%AD%E5%A4%AE%E5%9B%BD%E5%AE%B6%E6%9C%BA%E5%85%B3">

		<outline text="（2）同外国的国家名称、国旗、国徽、军旗等相同或者近似的，但经该国政府同意的除外。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%E5%90%8C%E5%A4%96%E5%9B%BD%E7%9A%84%E5%9B%BD%E5%AE%B6%E5%90%8D%E7%A7%B0%E3%80%81%E5%9B%BD%E6%97%97%E3%80%81%E5%9B%BD%E5%BE%BD%E3%80%81%E5%86%9B%E6%97%97%E7%AD%89%E7%9B%B8%E5%90%8C%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E8%BF%91%E4%BC%BC%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E4%BD%86%E7%BB%8F%E8%AF%A5%E5%9B%BD%E6%94%BF%E5%BA%9C%E5%90%8C%E6%84%8F%E7%9A%84%E9%99%A4%E5%A4%96%E3%80%82" _note="外：外国" _mubu_note="%E5%A4%96%EF%BC%9A%E5%A4%96%E5%9B%BD">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（3）同政府间的国际组织的名称、旗帜、徽记等相同或者近似的，但经该组织同意或者不易误导公众的除外。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%E5%90%8C%E6%94%BF%E5%BA%9C%E9%97%B4%E7%9A%84%E5%9B%BD%E9%99%85%E7%BB%84%E7%BB%87%E7%9A%84%E5%90%8D%E7%A7%B0%E3%80%81%E6%97%97%E5%B8%9C%E3%80%81%E5%BE%BD%E8%AE%B0%E7%AD%89%E7%9B%B8%E5%90%8C%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E8%BF%91%E4%BC%BC%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E4%BD%86%E7%BB%8F%E8%AF%A5%E7%BB%84%E7%BB%87%E5%90%8C%E6%84%8F%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%3E%E4%B8%8D%E6%98%93%E8%AF%AF%E5%AF%BC%E5%85%AC%E4%BC%97%E7%9A%84%E9%99%A4%E5%A4%96%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E" _note="足：政府间国际组织" _mubu_note="%E8%B6%B3%EF%BC%9A%E6%94%BF%E5%BA%9C%E9%97%B4%E5%9B%BD%E9%99%85%E7%BB%84%E7%BB%87">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（4）与表明实施控制、予以保证的官方标志、检验印记相同或者近似的，但经授权的除外。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%884%EF%BC%89%E4%B8%8E%E8%A1%A8%E6%98%8E%E5%AE%9E%E6%96%BD%E6%8E%A7%E5%88%B6%E3%80%81%E4%BA%88%E4%BB%A5%E4%BF%9D%E8%AF%81%E7%9A%84%E5%AE%98%E6%96%B9%E6%A0%87%E5%BF%97%E3%80%81%E6%A3%80%E9%AA%8C%E5%8D%B0%E8%AE%B0%E7%9B%B8%E5%90%8C%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E8%BF%91%E4%BC%BC%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E4%BD%86%E7%BB%8F%E6%8E%88%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E9%99%A4%E5%A4%96%E3%80%82" _note="控：实施控制、予以保证" _mubu_note="%E6%8E%A7%EF%BC%9A%E5%AE%9E%E6%96%BD%E6%8E%A7%E5%88%B6%E3%80%81%E4%BA%88%E4%BB%A5%E4%BF%9D%E8%AF%81">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（5）同“红十字”、“红新月”的名称、标志相同或者近似的。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%885%EF%BC%89%E5%90%8C%E2%80%9C%E7%BA%A2%E5%8D%81%E5%AD%97%E2%80%9D%E3%80%81%E2%80%9C%E7%BA%A2%E6%96%B0%E6%9C%88%E2%80%9D%E7%9A%84%E5%90%8D%E7%A7%B0%E3%80%81%E6%A0%87%E5%BF%97%E7%9B%B8%E5%90%8C%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E8%BF%91%E4%BC%BC%E7%9A%84%E3%80%82" _note="红：红十字、红新月" _mubu_note="%E7%BA%A2%EF%BC%9A%E7%BA%A2%E5%8D%81%E5%AD%97%E3%80%81%E7%BA%A2%E6%96%B0%E6%9C%88">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（6）带有民族歧视性的。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%886%EF%BC%89%E5%B8%A6%E6%9C%89%E6%B0%91%E6%97%8F%E6%AD%A7%E8%A7%86%E6%80%A7%E7%9A%84%E3%80%82" _note="旗：民族歧视性" _mubu_note="%E6%97%97%EF%BC%9A%E6%B0%91%E6%97%8F%E6%AD%A7%E8%A7%86%E6%80%A7">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（7）带有欺骗性，容易使公众对商品的质量等特点或者产地产生误认的。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%887%EF%BC%89%E5%B8%A6%E6%9C%89%E6%AC%BA%E9%AA%97%E6%80%A7%EF%BC%8C%E5%AE%B9%E6%98%93%E4%BD%BF%E5%85%AC%E4%BC%97%E5%AF%B9%E5%95%86%E5%93%81%E7%9A%84%E8%B4%A8%E9%87%8F%E7%AD%89%E7%89%B9%E7%82%B9%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E4%BA%A7%E5%9C%B0%E4%BA%A7%E7%94%9F%E8%AF%AF%E8%AE%A4%E7%9A%84%E3%80%82" _note="骗：带有欺骗性" _mubu_note="%E9%AA%97%EF%BC%9A%E5%B8%A6%E6%9C%89%E6%AC%BA%E9%AA%97%E6%80%A7">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（8）有害于社会主义道德风尚或者有其他不良影响的。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%888%EF%BC%89%E6%9C%89%E5%AE%B3%E4%BA%8E%E7%A4%BE%E4%BC%9A%E4%B8%BB%E4%B9%89%E9%81%93%E5%BE%B7%E9%A3%8E%E5%B0%9A%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E6%9C%89%E5%85%B6%E4%BB%96%E4%B8%8D%E8%89%AF%E5%BD%B1%E5%93%8D%E7%9A%84%E3%80%82" _note="到：社会主义道德风尚" _mubu_note="%E5%88%B0%EF%BC%9A%E7%A4%BE%E4%BC%9A%E4%B8%BB%E4%B9%89%E9%81%93%E5%BE%B7%E9%A3%8E%E5%B0%9A">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（9）县级以上行政区域的地名或者公众知晓的外国地名，不得作为商标。但是地名具有其他含义或者作为集体商标、证明商标组成部分的除外。已经注册的使用地名的商标继续有效。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%889%EF%BC%89%E5%8E%BF%E7%BA%A7%E4%BB%A5%E4%B8%8A%E8%A1%8C%E6%94%BF%E5%8C%BA%E5%9F%9F%E7%9A%84%E5%9C%B0%E5%90%8D%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%85%AC%E4%BC%97%E7%9F%A5%E6%99%93%E7%9A%84%E5%A4%96%E5%9B%BD%E5%9C%B0%E5%90%8D%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%8D%E5%BE%97%E4%BD%9C%E4%B8%BA%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E3%80%82%E4%BD%86%E6%98%AF%E5%9C%B0%E5%90%8D%E5%85%B7%E6%9C%89%E5%85%B6%E4%BB%96%E5%90%AB%E4%B9%89%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E4%BD%9C%E4%B8%BA%E9%9B%86%E4%BD%93%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E3%80%81%E8%AF%81%E6%98%8E%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E7%BB%84%E6%88%90%E9%83%A8%E5%88%86%E7%9A%84%E9%99%A4%E5%A4%96%E3%80%82%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%B7%B2%E7%BB%8F%E6%B3%A8%E5%86%8C%E7%9A%84%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E5%9C%B0%E5%90%8D%E7%9A%84%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E7%BB%A7%E7%BB%AD%E6%9C%89%E6%95%88%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E" _note="底：县级以上行政区域的地名或者公众知晓的外国地名    
​注意：继续有效的只能是已经注册的商标，未经注册的使如上所述的地名的商标的无效" _mubu_note="%E5%BA%95%EF%BC%9A%E5%8E%BF%E7%BA%A7%E4%BB%A5%E4%B8%8A%E8%A1%8C%E6%94%BF%E5%8C%BA%E5%9F%9F%E7%9A%84%E5%9C%B0%E5%90%8D%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%85%AC%E4%BC%97%E7%9F%A5%E6%99%93%E7%9A%84%E5%A4%96%E5%9B%BD%E5%9C%B0%E5%90%8D%20%20%20%20%0A%E2%80%8B%E6%B3%A8%E6%84%8F%EF%BC%9A%E7%BB%A7%E7%BB%AD%E6%9C%89%E6%95%88%E7%9A%84%E5%8F%AA%E8%83%BD%E6%98%AF%E5%B7%B2%E7%BB%8F%E6%B3%A8%E5%86%8C%E7%9A%84%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%EF%BC%8C%E6%9C%AA%E7%BB%8F%E6%B3%A8%E5%86%8C%E7%9A%84%E4%BD%BF%E5%A6%82%E4%B8%8A%E6%89%80%E8%BF%B0%E7%9A%84%E5%9C%B0%E5%90%8D%E7%9A%84%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E6%97%A0%E6%95%88">

		<outline text="304.简述商标权的内容（权利）❶" _mubu_text="304.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%EF%BC%88%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%EF%BC%89%E2%9D%B6">
		<outline text="1.独占使用权。" _mubu_text="1.%E7%8B%AC%E5%8D%A0%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E6%9D%83%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="商标一经注册，商标权人即对注册商标在法定范围内享有专有使用的权利，他人未经许可不得使用。否则，就构成侵权。" _mubu_text="%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E4%B8%80%E7%BB%8F%E6%B3%A8%E5%86%8C%EF%BC%8C%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E5%8D%B3%E5%AF%B9%E6%B3%A8%E5%86%8C%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E5%9C%A8%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E8%8C%83%E5%9B%B4%E5%86%85%E4%BA%AB%E6%9C%89%E4%B8%93%E6%9C%89%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%EF%BC%8C%E4%BB%96%E4%BA%BA%E6%9C%AA%E7%BB%8F%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E4%B8%8D%E5%BE%97%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E3%80%82%E5%90%A6%E5%88%99%EF%BC%8C%E5%B0%B1%E6%9E%84%E6%88%90%E4%BE%B5%E6%9D%83%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="2.转让权。" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E2.%E8%BD%AC%E8%AE%A9%E6%9D%83%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E" _note="@口诀&nbsp;标转取丧协申质量一并公告@简答题   " _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E6%A0%87%E8%BD%AC%E5%8F%96%E4%B8%A7%E5%8D%8F%E7%94%B3%E8%B4%A8%E9%87%8F%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B6%E5%85%AC%E5%91%8A@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%20%20%20" _heading="1" _color="#75c940">
		<outline text="（1）商标权人有权依照法律规定，将商标权转让给他人。商标转让后，原商标权人的权利丧失，受让人取得商标权。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E6%9C%89%E6%9D%83%E4%BE%9D%E7%85%A7%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%EF%BC%8C%E5%B0%86%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%9D%83%E8%BD%AC%E8%AE%A9%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%96%E4%BA%BA%E3%80%82%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E8%BD%AC%E8%AE%A9%E5%90%8E%EF%BC%8C%E5%8E%9F%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E4%B8%A7%E5%A4%B1%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%97%E8%AE%A9%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%96%E5%BE%97%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%9D%83%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（2）转让注册商标的，转让人和受让人应当签订转让协议，并共同向商标局提出申请。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%E8%BD%AC%E8%AE%A9%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%3E%E6%B3%A8%E5%86%8C%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%3C/span%3E%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E8%BD%AC%E8%AE%A9%E4%BA%BA%E5%92%8C%E5%8F%97%E8%AE%A9%E4%BA%BA%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E7%AD%BE%E8%AE%A2%E8%BD%AC%E8%AE%A9%E5%8D%8F%E8%AE%AE%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%3E%E5%B9%B6%E5%85%B1%E5%90%8C%E5%90%91%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E5%B1%80%E6%8F%90%E5%87%BA%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（3）受让人应当保证使用该注册商标的商品质量。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%E5%8F%97%E8%AE%A9%E4%BA%BA%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E4%BF%9D%E8%AF%81%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E8%AF%A5%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%3E%E6%B3%A8%E5%86%8C%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%3C/span%3E%E7%9A%84%E5%95%86%E5%93%81%E8%B4%A8%E9%87%8F%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（4）转让注册商标的，商标注册人对其在同一种商品上注册的近似的商标，或者在类似商品上注册的相同或者近似的商标，应当一并转让。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%884%EF%BC%89%E8%BD%AC%E8%AE%A9%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%3E%E6%B3%A8%E5%86%8C%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%3C/span%3E%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%B3%A8%E5%86%8C%E4%BA%BA%E5%AF%B9%E5%85%B6%E5%9C%A8%E5%90%8C%E4%B8%80%E7%A7%8D%E5%95%86%E5%93%81%E4%B8%8A%E6%B3%A8%E5%86%8C%E7%9A%84%E8%BF%91%E4%BC%BC%E7%9A%84%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%EF%BC%8C%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%9C%A8%E7%B1%BB%E4%BC%BC%E5%95%86%E5%93%81%E4%B8%8A%E6%B3%A8%E5%86%8C%E7%9A%84%E7%9B%B8%E5%90%8C%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E8%BF%91%E4%BC%BC%E7%9A%84%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%EF%BC%8C%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B6%E8%BD%AC%E8%AE%A9%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（5）转让注册商标经核准后，予以公告。受让人自公告之日起享有商标专用权。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%885%EF%BC%89%E8%BD%AC%E8%AE%A9%E6%B3%A8%E5%86%8C%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E7%BB%8F%E6%A0%B8%E5%87%86%E5%90%8E%EF%BC%8C%E4%BA%88%E4%BB%A5%E5%85%AC%E5%91%8A%E3%80%82%E5%8F%97%E8%AE%A9%E4%BA%BA%E8%87%AA%E5%85%AC%E5%91%8A%E4%B9%8B%E6%97%A5%E8%B5%B7%E4%BA%AB%E6%9C%89%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E4%B8%93%E7%94%A8%E6%9D%83%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="3.使用许可权。" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E3.%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E6%9D%83%3C/span%3E%E3%80%82" _note="@口诀&nbsp;表叔（许）唯一监督标明备案 （表叔是唯一的商标许可使用权监督者，他身上已经标明了备案字样）      &nbsp;@简答题" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E8%A1%A8%E5%8F%94%EF%BC%88%E8%AE%B8%EF%BC%89%E5%94%AF%E4%B8%80%E7%9B%91%E7%9D%A3%E6%A0%87%E6%98%8E%E5%A4%87%E6%A1%88%20%EF%BC%88%E8%A1%A8%E5%8F%94%E6%98%AF%E5%94%AF%E4%B8%80%E7%9A%84%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E6%9D%83%E7%9B%91%E7%9D%A3%E8%80%85%EF%BC%8C%E4%BB%96%E8%BA%AB%E4%B8%8A%E5%B7%B2%E7%BB%8F%E6%A0%87%E6%98%8E%E4%BA%86%E5%A4%87%E6%A1%88%E5%AD%97%E6%A0%B7%EF%BC%89%20%20%20%20%20%20&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E" _heading="1" _color="#75c940">
		<outline text="（1）商标权人有权通过签订商标使用许可合同，许可他人使用自己的注册商标。在此种情形下，商标权人可以保留自己的使用权，也可以放弃使用权，但无论哪种情况，商标权并未发生转移，仍属于许可人。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E6%9C%89%E6%9D%83%E9%80%9A%E8%BF%87%E7%AD%BE%E8%AE%A2%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%EF%BC%8C%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%96%E4%BA%BA%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E8%87%AA%E5%B7%B1%E7%9A%84%E6%B3%A8%E5%86%8C%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E3%80%82%E5%9C%A8%E6%AD%A4%E7%A7%8D%E6%83%85%E5%BD%A2%E4%B8%8B%EF%BC%8C%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E4%BF%9D%E7%95%99%E8%87%AA%E5%B7%B1%E7%9A%84%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%8C%E4%B9%9F%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E6%94%BE%E5%BC%83%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%8C%E4%BD%86%E6%97%A0%E8%AE%BA%E5%93%AA%E7%A7%8D%E6%83%85%E5%86%B5%EF%BC%8C%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%9D%83%E5%B9%B6%E6%9C%AA%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E8%BD%AC%E7%A7%BB%EF%BC%8C%E4%BB%8D%E5%B1%9E%E4%BA%8E%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E4%BA%BA%E3%80%82" _note="唯一：商标权并未发生转移，仍然属于许可人。" _mubu_note="%E5%94%AF%E4%B8%80%EF%BC%9A%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%9D%83%E5%B9%B6%E6%9C%AA%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E8%BD%AC%E7%A7%BB%EF%BC%8C%E4%BB%8D%E7%84%B6%E5%B1%9E%E4%BA%8E%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E4%BA%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（2）许可人应当监督被许可人使用其注册商标的商品质量。被许可人应当保证使用该注册商标的商品质量。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E4%BA%BA%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E7%9B%91%E7%9D%A3%E8%A2%AB%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E4%BA%BA%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E5%85%B6%E6%B3%A8%E5%86%8C%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E5%95%86%E5%93%81%E8%B4%A8%E9%87%8F%E3%80%82%E8%A2%AB%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E4%BA%BA%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E4%BF%9D%E8%AF%81%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E8%AF%A5%E6%B3%A8%E5%86%8C%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E5%95%86%E5%93%81%E8%B4%A8%E9%87%8F%E3%80%82" _note="监督" _mubu_note="%E7%9B%91%E7%9D%A3">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（3）经许可使用他人注册商标的，必须在使用该注册商标的商品上标明被许可人的名称和商品产地。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%E7%BB%8F%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E4%BB%96%E4%BA%BA%E6%B3%A8%E5%86%8C%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E5%BF%85%E9%A1%BB%E5%9C%A8%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E8%AF%A5%E6%B3%A8%E5%86%8C%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E5%95%86%E5%93%81%E4%B8%8A%E6%A0%87%E6%98%8E%E8%A2%AB%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%90%8D%E7%A7%B0%E5%92%8C%E5%95%86%E5%93%81%E4%BA%A7%E5%9C%B0%E3%80%82" _note="标明" _mubu_note="%E6%A0%87%E6%98%8E">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（4）商标使用许可合同应当报商标局备案，未经备案不得对抗善意第三人。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%884%EF%BC%89%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E6%8A%A5%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E5%B1%80%E5%A4%87%E6%A1%88%EF%BC%8C%E6%9C%AA%E7%BB%8F%E5%A4%87%E6%A1%88%E4%B8%8D%E5%BE%97%E5%AF%B9%E6%8A%97%E5%96%84%E6%84%8F%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%E3%80%82" _note="备案" _mubu_note="%E5%A4%87%E6%A1%88">

		<outline text="305.简述商标权终止的原因❶" _mubu_text="305.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%9D%83%E7%BB%88%E6%AD%A2%E7%9A%84%E5%8E%9F%E5%9B%A0%E2%9D%B6">
		<outline text="商标权的终止原因包括" _mubu_text="%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E7%BB%88%E6%AD%A2%E5%8E%9F%E5%9B%A0%E5%8C%85%E6%8B%AC">
		<outline text="1.注销。" _mubu_text="1.%E6%B3%A8%E9%94%80%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="商标注销的概念" _mubu_text="%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%B3%A8%E9%94%80%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="注销是指因商标权人自动放弃商标权或无人承继商标权而由商标主管部门注销商标。" _mubu_text="%E6%B3%A8%E9%94%80%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%9B%A0%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E8%87%AA%E5%8A%A8%E6%94%BE%E5%BC%83%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%9D%83%E6%88%96%E6%97%A0%E4%BA%BA%E6%89%BF%E7%BB%A7%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%9D%83%E8%80%8C%E7%94%B1%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E4%B8%BB%E7%AE%A1%E9%83%A8%E9%97%A8%E6%B3%A8%E9%94%80%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="自动放弃商标权" _mubu_text="%E8%87%AA%E5%8A%A8%E6%94%BE%E5%BC%83%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%9D%83">
		<outline text="商标权人的自动放弃行为可以是明示的，也可以是默示的，如商标权期满未申请续展。" _mubu_text="%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E8%87%AA%E5%8A%A8%E6%94%BE%E5%BC%83%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E6%98%AF%E6%98%8E%E7%A4%BA%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E4%B9%9F%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E6%98%AF%E9%BB%98%E7%A4%BA%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%A6%82%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%9D%83%E6%9C%9F%E6%BB%A1%E6%9C%AA%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E7%BB%AD%E5%B1%95%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="无人承继商标权" _mubu_text="%E6%97%A0%E4%BA%BA%E6%89%BF%E7%BB%A7%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%9D%83">
		<outline text="无人承继商标权是指商标权人死亡或者终止，自死亡或者终止之日起1年期满，该注册商标没有办理移转手续。在此种情况下，任何人都可以向商标局申请注销该注册商标。" _mubu_text="%E6%97%A0%E4%BA%BA%E6%89%BF%E7%BB%A7%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%9D%83%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E6%AD%BB%E4%BA%A1%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E7%BB%88%E6%AD%A2%EF%BC%8C%E8%87%AA%E6%AD%BB%E4%BA%A1%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E7%BB%88%E6%AD%A2%E4%B9%8B%E6%97%A5%E8%B5%B7%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E1%E5%B9%B4%E6%9C%9F%E6%BB%A1%EF%BC%8C%3C/span%3E%E8%AF%A5%E6%B3%A8%E5%86%8C%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%B2%A1%E6%9C%89%E5%8A%9E%E7%90%86%E7%A7%BB%E8%BD%AC%E6%89%8B%E7%BB%AD%E3%80%82%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%9C%A8%E6%AD%A4%E7%A7%8D%E6%83%85%E5%86%B5%E4%B8%8B%EF%BC%8C%E4%BB%BB%E4%BD%95%E4%BA%BA%E9%83%BD%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E5%90%91%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E5%B1%80%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E6%B3%A8%E9%94%80%E8%AF%A5%E6%B3%A8%E5%86%8C%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E" _note="@考点" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E8%80%83%E7%82%B9%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="2.撤销。" _mubu_text="2.%E6%92%A4%E9%94%80%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="商标权的撤销的概念" _mubu_text="%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E6%92%A4%E9%94%80%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="商标权的撤销是指因商标权人违反法律规定而被商标主管部门强制终止商标权。" _mubu_text="%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E6%92%A4%E9%94%80%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%9B%A0%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E8%BF%9D%E5%8F%8D%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E8%80%8C%E8%A2%AB%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E4%B8%BB%E7%AE%A1%E9%83%A8%E9%97%A8%E5%BC%BA%E5%88%B6%E7%BB%88%E6%AD%A2%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%9D%83%E3%80%82" _color="#333333">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="商标权的撤销事由" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E6%92%A4%E9%94%80%E4%BA%8B%E7%94%B1%3C/span%3E" _note="@口诀&nbsp;上车自行同命三年&nbsp;@考点&nbsp;@简答题" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E4%B8%8A%E8%BD%A6%E8%87%AA%E8%A1%8C%E5%90%8C%E5%91%BD%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E8%80%83%E7%82%B9%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E" _heading="1" _color="#75c940">
		<outline text="（1）根据《商标法》的规定，商标注册人在使用注册商标的过程中，自行改变注册商标、注册人名义、地址或者其他注册事项的，由地方工商行政管理部门责令限期改正；期满不改正的，由商标局撤销其注册商标。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE%E3%80%8A%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%B3%95%E3%80%8B%E7%9A%84%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%EF%BC%8C%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%B3%A8%E5%86%8C%E4%BA%BA%E5%9C%A8%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E6%B3%A8%E5%86%8C%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E8%BF%87%E7%A8%8B%E4%B8%AD%EF%BC%8C%E8%87%AA%E8%A1%8C%E6%94%B9%E5%8F%98%E6%B3%A8%E5%86%8C%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E3%80%81%E6%B3%A8%E5%86%8C%E4%BA%BA%E5%90%8D%E4%B9%89%E3%80%81%E5%9C%B0%E5%9D%80%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%85%B6%E4%BB%96%E6%B3%A8%E5%86%8C%E4%BA%8B%E9%A1%B9%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E7%94%B1%E5%9C%B0%E6%96%B9%E5%B7%A5%E5%95%86%E8%A1%8C%E6%94%BF%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E9%83%A8%E9%97%A8%E8%B4%A3%E4%BB%A4%E9%99%90%E6%9C%9F%E6%94%B9%E6%AD%A3%EF%BC%9B%E6%9C%9F%E6%BB%A1%E4%B8%8D%E6%94%B9%E6%AD%A3%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E7%94%B1%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E5%B1%80%E6%92%A4%E9%94%80%E5%85%B6%E6%B3%A8%E5%86%8C%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E3%80%82" _color="#333333">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（2）注册商标成为其核定使用的商品的通用名称或者没有正当理由连续3年不使用的，任何单位或者个人可以向商标局申请撤销该注册商标。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%B3%A8%E5%86%8C%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%88%90%E4%B8%BA%E5%85%B6%E6%A0%B8%E5%AE%9A%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E7%9A%84%E5%95%86%E5%93%81%E7%9A%84%E9%80%9A%E7%94%A8%E5%90%8D%E7%A7%B0%3C/span%3E%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E6%B2%A1%E6%9C%89%E6%AD%A3%E5%BD%93%E7%90%86%E7%94%B1%E8%BF%9E%E7%BB%AD3%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%8D%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E4%BB%BB%E4%BD%95%E5%8D%95%E4%BD%8D%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E4%B8%AA%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E5%90%91%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E5%B1%80%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E6%92%A4%E9%94%80%E8%AF%A5%E6%B3%A8%E5%86%8C%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E3%80%82" _color="#333333">

		<outline text="撤销商标权的后果" _mubu_text="%E6%92%A4%E9%94%80%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E5%90%8E%E6%9E%9C" _color="#333333">
		<outline text="被撤销的注册商标，由商标局予以公告，该注册商标专用权自公告之日起终止。" _mubu_text="%E8%A2%AB%E6%92%A4%E9%94%80%E7%9A%84%E6%B3%A8%E5%86%8C%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%EF%BC%8C%E7%94%B1%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E5%B1%80%E4%BA%88%E4%BB%A5%E5%85%AC%E5%91%8A%EF%BC%8C%E8%AF%A5%E6%B3%A8%E5%86%8C%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E4%B8%93%E7%94%A8%E6%9D%83%E8%87%AA%E5%85%AC%E5%91%8A%E4%B9%8B%E6%97%A5%E8%B5%B7%E7%BB%88%E6%AD%A2%E3%80%82" _color="#333333">

		<outline text="注册商标被撤销的或者期满不再续展的，自撤销或者注销之日起1年内，商标局对与该商标相同或者近似的商标注册申请，不予核准。" _mubu_text="%E6%B3%A8%E5%86%8C%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E8%A2%AB%E6%92%A4%E9%94%80%E7%9A%84%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E6%9C%9F%E6%BB%A1%E4%B8%8D%E5%86%8D%E7%BB%AD%E5%B1%95%3C/span%3E%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E8%87%AA%E6%92%A4%E9%94%80%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E6%B3%A8%E9%94%80%E4%B9%8B%E6%97%A5%E8%B5%B71%E5%B9%B4%E5%86%85%EF%BC%8C%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E5%B1%80%E5%AF%B9%E4%B8%8E%E8%AF%A5%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E7%9B%B8%E5%90%8C%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E8%BF%91%E4%BC%BC%E7%9A%84%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%B3%A8%E5%86%8C%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%8D%E4%BA%88%E6%A0%B8%E5%87%86%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E" _note="@考点" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E8%80%83%E7%82%B9%3C/span%3E">

		<outline text="306.简述商标权的保护方式❶" _mubu_text="306.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E4%BF%9D%E6%8A%A4%E6%96%B9%E5%BC%8F%E2%9D%B6">
		<outline text="商标权侵权的处理方式" _mubu_text="%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%9D%83%E4%BE%B5%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E5%A4%84%E7%90%86%E6%96%B9%E5%BC%8F">
		<outline text="善意侵权" _mubu_text="%E5%96%84%E6%84%8F%E4%BE%B5%E6%9D%83">
		<outline text="善意侵权的概念" _mubu_text="%E5%96%84%E6%84%8F%E4%BE%B5%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="侵犯商标权给权利人造成损害的,应当承担赔偿损失的民事责任,但销售不知道是侵犯注册商标专用权的商品，能说明该商品是自己合法取得并说明提供者的，不承担赔偿责任。此种情形在学理上被称为善意侵权。" _mubu_text="%E4%BE%B5%E7%8A%AF%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%9D%83%E7%BB%99%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E4%BA%BA%E9%80%A0%E6%88%90%E6%8D%9F%E5%AE%B3%E7%9A%84,%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E6%89%BF%E6%8B%85%E8%B5%94%E5%81%BF%E6%8D%9F%E5%A4%B1%E7%9A%84%E6%B0%91%E4%BA%8B%E8%B4%A3%E4%BB%BB,%E4%BD%86%E9%94%80%E5%94%AE%E4%B8%8D%E7%9F%A5%E9%81%93%E6%98%AF%E4%BE%B5%E7%8A%AF%E6%B3%A8%E5%86%8C%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E4%B8%93%E7%94%A8%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E5%95%86%E5%93%81%EF%BC%8C%E8%83%BD%E8%AF%B4%E6%98%8E%E8%AF%A5%E5%95%86%E5%93%81%E6%98%AF%E8%87%AA%E5%B7%B1%E5%90%88%E6%B3%95%E5%8F%96%E5%BE%97%E5%B9%B6%E8%AF%B4%E6%98%8E%E6%8F%90%E4%BE%9B%E8%80%85%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E4%B8%8D%E6%89%BF%E6%8B%85%E8%B5%94%E5%81%BF%E8%B4%A3%E4%BB%BB%3C/span%3E%E3%80%82%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%AD%A4%E7%A7%8D%E6%83%85%E5%BD%A2%E5%9C%A8%E5%AD%A6%E7%90%86%E4%B8%8A%E8%A2%AB%E7%A7%B0%E4%B8%BA%E5%96%84%E6%84%8F%E4%BE%B5%E6%9D%83%3C/span%3E%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="侵权人虽然不承担赔偿责任，但应当承担停止侵权的责任。" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E4%BE%B5%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E8%99%BD%E7%84%B6%E4%B8%8D%E6%89%BF%E6%8B%85%E8%B5%94%E5%81%BF%E8%B4%A3%E4%BB%BB%EF%BC%8C%E4%BD%86%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E6%89%BF%E6%8B%85%E5%81%9C%E6%AD%A2%E4%BE%B5%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E8%B4%A3%E4%BB%BB%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
