		<outline text="权利人可以直接向侵权人请求承担侵权责任。" _mubu_text="%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E7%9B%B4%E6%8E%A5%E5%90%91%E4%BE%B5%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E8%AF%B7%E6%B1%82%E6%89%BF%E6%8B%85%E4%BE%B5%E6%9D%83%E8%B4%A3%E4%BB%BB%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="(1) 向侵权人所在地县级以上工商行政管理部门要求处理。" _mubu_text="(1)%20%E5%90%91%E4%BE%B5%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E6%89%80%E5%9C%A8%E5%9C%B0%E5%8E%BF%E7%BA%A7%E4%BB%A5%E4%B8%8A%E5%B7%A5%E5%95%86%E8%A1%8C%E6%94%BF%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E9%83%A8%E9%97%A8%E8%A6%81%E6%B1%82%E5%A4%84%E7%90%86%E3%80%82" _note="注意：是向侵权人所在地的工商行政部门要求处理，不是商标权所在地工商行政管理部门。" _mubu_note="%E6%B3%A8%E6%84%8F%EF%BC%9A%E6%98%AF%E5%90%91%E4%BE%B5%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E6%89%80%E5%9C%A8%E5%9C%B0%E7%9A%84%E5%B7%A5%E5%95%86%E8%A1%8C%E6%94%BF%E9%83%A8%E9%97%A8%E8%A6%81%E6%B1%82%E5%A4%84%E7%90%86%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%8D%E6%98%AF%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%9D%83%E6%89%80%E5%9C%A8%E5%9C%B0%E5%B7%A5%E5%95%86%E8%A1%8C%E6%94%BF%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E9%83%A8%E9%97%A8%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="工商行政管理部门认定侵权行为成立的，有权责令侵权人立即停止侵权行为，没收、销毁侵权商品和专门用于制造侵权商品、伪造注册商标标识的工具，并可处以罚款。" _mubu_text="%E5%B7%A5%E5%95%86%E8%A1%8C%E6%94%BF%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E9%83%A8%E9%97%A8%E8%AE%A4%E5%AE%9A%E4%BE%B5%E6%9D%83%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E6%9C%89%E6%9D%83%E8%B4%A3%E4%BB%A4%E4%BE%B5%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E7%AB%8B%E5%8D%B3%E5%81%9C%E6%AD%A2%E4%BE%B5%E6%9D%83%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%EF%BC%8C%E6%B2%A1%E6%94%B6%E3%80%81%E9%94%80%E6%AF%81%E4%BE%B5%E6%9D%83%E5%95%86%E5%93%81%E5%92%8C%E4%B8%93%E9%97%A8%E7%94%A8%E4%BA%8E%E5%88%B6%E9%80%A0%E4%BE%B5%E6%9D%83%E5%95%86%E5%93%81%E3%80%81%E4%BC%AA%E9%80%A0%E6%B3%A8%E5%86%8C%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E6%A0%87%E8%AF%86%E7%9A%84%E5%B7%A5%E5%85%B7%EF%BC%8C%E5%B9%B6%E5%8F%AF%E5%A4%84%E4%BB%A5%E7%BD%9A%E6%AC%BE%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="根据当事人的请求，进行处理的工商行政管理部门可以就侵犯商标专用权的赔偿数额进行调解。调解不成的，当事人可以依法向人民法院起诉。" _mubu_text="%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E8%AF%B7%E6%B1%82%EF%BC%8C%E8%BF%9B%E8%A1%8C%E5%A4%84%E7%90%86%E7%9A%84%E5%B7%A5%E5%95%86%E8%A1%8C%E6%94%BF%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E9%83%A8%E9%97%A8%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E5%B0%B1%E4%BE%B5%E7%8A%AF%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E4%B8%93%E7%94%A8%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E8%B5%94%E5%81%BF%E6%95%B0%E9%A2%9D%E8%BF%9B%E8%A1%8C%E8%B0%83%E8%A7%A3%E3%80%82%E8%B0%83%E8%A7%A3%E4%B8%8D%E6%88%90%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E4%BE%9D%E6%B3%95%E5%90%91%E4%BA%BA%E6%B0%91%E6%B3%95%E9%99%A2%E8%B5%B7%E8%AF%89%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(2)向人民法院提起民事诉讼，要求人民法院依法责令侵权人停止侵害，消除影响，赔偿损失。" _mubu_text="(2)%E5%90%91%E4%BA%BA%E6%B0%91%E6%B3%95%E9%99%A2%E6%8F%90%E8%B5%B7%E6%B0%91%E4%BA%8B%E8%AF%89%E8%AE%BC%EF%BC%8C%E8%A6%81%E6%B1%82%E4%BA%BA%E6%B0%91%E6%B3%95%E9%99%A2%E4%BE%9D%E6%B3%95%E8%B4%A3%E4%BB%A4%E4%BE%B5%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E5%81%9C%E6%AD%A2%E4%BE%B5%E5%AE%B3%EF%BC%8C%E6%B6%88%E9%99%A4%E5%BD%B1%E5%93%8D%EF%BC%8C%E8%B5%94%E5%81%BF%E6%8D%9F%E5%A4%B1%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="赔偿数额按照权利人因被侵权所受到的实际损失确定；" _mubu_text="%E8%B5%94%E5%81%BF%E6%95%B0%E9%A2%9D%E6%8C%89%E7%85%A7%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E4%BA%BA%E5%9B%A0%E8%A2%AB%E4%BE%B5%E6%9D%83%E6%89%80%E5%8F%97%E5%88%B0%E7%9A%84%E5%AE%9E%E9%99%85%E6%8D%9F%E5%A4%B1%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%EF%BC%9B">
		</outline>
		<outline text="实际损失难以确定的，可以按照侵权人因侵权所获得的利益确定；" _mubu_text="%E5%AE%9E%E9%99%85%E6%8D%9F%E5%A4%B1%E9%9A%BE%E4%BB%A5%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E6%8C%89%E7%85%A7%E4%BE%B5%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E5%9B%A0%E4%BE%B5%E6%9D%83%E6%89%80%E8%8E%B7%E5%BE%97%E7%9A%84%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%EF%BC%9B">
		</outline>
		<outline text="以上均难以确定的，参照该商标许可使用费的倍数合理确定。赔偿数额应当包括权利人为制止侵权行为所支付的合理开支。" _mubu_text="%E4%BB%A5%E4%B8%8A%E5%9D%87%E9%9A%BE%E4%BB%A5%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%82%E7%85%A7%E8%AF%A5%E5%95%86%E6%A0%87%E8%AE%B8%E5%8F%AF%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E8%B4%B9%E7%9A%84%E5%80%8D%E6%95%B0%E5%90%88%E7%90%86%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%E3%80%82%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E8%B5%94%E5%81%BF%E6%95%B0%E9%A2%9D%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E5%8C%85%E6%8B%AC%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%BA%E5%88%B6%E6%AD%A2%E4%BE%B5%E6%9D%83%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E6%89%80%E6%94%AF%E4%BB%98%E7%9A%84%E5%90%88%E7%90%86%E5%BC%80%E6%94%AF%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="307.简述债的概念和特征❶" _mubu_text="307.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5%E5%92%8C%E7%89%B9%E5%BE%81%E2%9D%B6">
		<outline text="债的概念" _mubu_text="%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="民法上的债，是指特定的当事人之间可以请求为特定行为的民事法律关系。" _mubu_text="%E6%B0%91%E6%B3%95%E4%B8%8A%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%EF%BC%8C%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%B9%8B%E9%97%B4%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E8%AF%B7%E6%B1%82%E4%B8%BA%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%B0%91%E4%BA%8B%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="债的特征" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E7%89%B9%E5%BE%81%3C/span%3E" _note="@简答题&nbsp;@题眼&nbsp;@口诀&nbsp;宅正特请笔法满" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E9%A2%98%E7%9C%BC%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E5%AE%85%E6%AD%A3%E7%89%B9%E8%AF%B7%E7%AC%94%E6%B3%95%E6%BB%A1" _heading="1" _color="#dc2d1e">
		<outline text="（1）债是存在于特定当事人之间的法律关系。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E5%80%BA%E6%98%AF%E5%AD%98%E5%9C%A8%E4%BA%8E%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%B9%8B%E9%97%B4%E7%9A%84%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（2）债是特定当事人之间请求为特定行为的法律关系。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%E5%80%BA%E6%98%AF%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%B9%8B%E9%97%B4%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E8%AF%B7%E6%B1%82%E4%B8%BA%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%3C/span%3E%E7%9A%84%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（3）债是能够以货币衡量评价的财产法律关系。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%E5%80%BA%E6%98%AF%E8%83%BD%E5%A4%9F%E4%BB%A5%E8%B4%A7%E5%B8%81%E8%A1%A1%E9%87%8F%E8%AF%84%E4%BB%B7%E7%9A%84%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E8%B4%A2%E4%BA%A7%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（4）债是按照法律规定或者法律行为而产生的法律关系。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%884%EF%BC%89%E5%80%BA%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%89%E7%85%A7%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%3C/span%3E%E8%80%8C%E4%BA%A7%E7%94%9F%E7%9A%84%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（5）债的存在表明债权人的利益还没有得到满足，在债权人的利益得到满足时,债的关系即消灭，故在本质上债体现的是债权人实现自身特定利益的法律手段。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%885%EF%BC%89%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%AD%98%E5%9C%A8%E8%A1%A8%E6%98%8E%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E8%BF%98%E6%B2%A1%E6%9C%89%E5%BE%97%E5%88%B0%E6%BB%A1%E8%B6%B3%EF%BC%8C%E5%9C%A8%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E5%BE%97%E5%88%B0%E6%BB%A1%E8%B6%B3%E6%97%B6,%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E5%8D%B3%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%EF%BC%8C%E6%95%85%E5%9C%A8%E6%9C%AC%E8%B4%A8%E4%B8%8A%E5%80%BA%E4%BD%93%E7%8E%B0%E7%9A%84%E6%98%AF%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E5%AE%9E%E7%8E%B0%E8%87%AA%E8%BA%AB%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E7%9A%84%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E6%89%8B%E6%AE%B5%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="308.简述债权的特征❶" _mubu_text="308.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E7%89%B9%E5%BE%81%E2%9D%B6">
		<outline text="债权的特征" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E7%89%B9%E5%BE%81%3C/span%3E" _note="@简答题&nbsp;@题眼&nbsp;@口诀&nbsp;翟泉正请降认费派平" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E9%A2%98%E7%9C%BC%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E7%BF%9F%E6%B3%89%E6%AD%A3%E8%AF%B7%E9%99%8D%E8%AE%A4%E8%B4%B9%E6%B4%BE%E5%B9%B3" _heading="1" _color="#dc2d1e">
		<outline text="债权的概念" _mubu_text="%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="债权是指债权人享有的以请求债务人为一定以给付为内容的行为的权利。" _mubu_text="%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E4%BA%AB%E6%9C%89%E7%9A%84%E4%BB%A5%E8%AF%B7%E6%B1%82%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%BA%E4%B8%80%E5%AE%9A%E4%BB%A5%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E4%B8%BA%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E7%9A%84%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(1)债权为请求权。" _mubu_text="(1)%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%B8%BA%E8%AF%B7%E6%B1%82%E6%9D%83%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="债权是债权人的请求债务人为特定行为的权利，在债务人作出给付前，债权人不能直接支配债务人应给付的标的物，也不能以支配债务人的人身来强制债务人作出给付，只能请求债务人履行债务来实现利益。" _mubu_text="%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E6%98%AF%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E8%AF%B7%E6%B1%82%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%BA%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%EF%BC%8C%E5%9C%A8%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E5%89%8D%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%8D%E8%83%BD%E7%9B%B4%E6%8E%A5%E6%94%AF%E9%85%8D%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E5%BA%94%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E7%9A%84%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E7%89%A9%EF%BC%8C%E4%B9%9F%E4%B8%8D%E8%83%BD%E4%BB%A5%E6%94%AF%E9%85%8D%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E4%BA%BA%E8%BA%AB%E6%9D%A5%E5%BC%BA%E5%88%B6%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%AA%E8%83%BD%E8%AF%B7%E6%B1%82%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E6%9D%A5%E5%AE%9E%E7%8E%B0%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(2)债权为相对权。" _mubu_text="(2)%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%B8%BA%E7%9B%B8%E5%AF%B9%E6%9D%83%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="债权人只能向债务人主张权利，请求债务人履行债务，除法律有明确规定外，即使因第三人的原因致使债权不能实现，债权人也只能以债之关系为基础向债务人主张权利。" _mubu_text="%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%AA%E8%83%BD%E5%90%91%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%BB%E5%BC%A0%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%EF%BC%8C%E8%AF%B7%E6%B1%82%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%EF%BC%8C%E9%99%A4%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E6%9C%89%E6%98%8E%E7%A1%AE%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E5%A4%96%EF%BC%8C%E5%8D%B3%E4%BD%BF%E5%9B%A0%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%8E%9F%E5%9B%A0%E8%87%B4%E4%BD%BF%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%B8%8D%E8%83%BD%E5%AE%9E%E7%8E%B0%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E4%B9%9F%E5%8F%AA%E8%83%BD%E4%BB%A5%E5%80%BA%E4%B9%8B%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E4%B8%BA%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80%E5%90%91%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%BB%E5%BC%A0%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(3)债权具有任意性。" _mubu_text="(3)%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E5%85%B7%E6%9C%89%E4%BB%BB%E6%84%8F%E6%80%A7%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="当事人在不违反强行法规定的情况下可以任意设定债的关系，法律并不加以限制；即使是法定之债，当事人也可以通过协商确定债的内容。" _mubu_text="%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E5%9C%A8%E4%B8%8D%E8%BF%9D%E5%8F%8D%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%3E%E5%BC%BA%E8%A1%8C%E6%B3%95%3C/span%3E%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E6%83%85%E5%86%B5%E4%B8%8B%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E4%BB%BB%E6%84%8F%E8%AE%BE%E5%AE%9A%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%EF%BC%8C%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E5%B9%B6%E4%B8%8D%E5%8A%A0%E4%BB%A5%E9%99%90%E5%88%B6%EF%BC%9B%E5%8D%B3%E4%BD%BF%E6%98%AF%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E4%B9%8B%E5%80%BA%EF%BC%8C%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%B9%9F%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E9%80%9A%E8%BF%87%E5%8D%8F%E5%95%86%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(4)债权具有非排他性。" _mubu_text="(4)%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E5%85%B7%E6%9C%89%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E9%9D%9E%E6%8E%92%E4%BB%96%E6%80%A7%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		<outline text="债权人仅能够向债务人提出给付的请求，不能对债务人应交付的标的物或者债务人的行为予以直接支配，而且，以同一给付为标的而成立的数个内容相同的债权相互之间不发生权利上的冲突，尽管此种情形下可能只有一个债权最终得以实现，但其他债权仍然有效，债权人可以债务不履行为由向债务人主张违约责任。" _mubu_text="%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E4%BB%85%E8%83%BD%E5%A4%9F%E5%90%91%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E6%8F%90%E5%87%BA%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E7%9A%84%E8%AF%B7%E6%B1%82%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%8D%E8%83%BD%E5%AF%B9%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E5%BA%94%E4%BA%A4%E4%BB%98%E7%9A%84%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E7%89%A9%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E4%BA%88%E4%BB%A5%E7%9B%B4%E6%8E%A5%E6%94%AF%E9%85%8D%EF%BC%8C%E8%80%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%3E%E4%B8%94%EF%BC%8C%E4%BB%A5%E5%90%8C%E4%B8%80%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E4%B8%BA%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E8%80%8C%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E7%9A%84%E6%95%B0%E4%B8%AA%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E7%9B%B8%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E7%9B%B8%E4%BA%92%E4%B9%8B%E9%97%B4%E4%B8%8D%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E4%B8%8A%E7%9A%84%E5%86%B2%E7%AA%81%EF%BC%8C%E5%B0%BD%E7%AE%A1%E6%AD%A4%E7%A7%8D%E6%83%85%E5%BD%A2%E4%B8%8B%E5%8F%AF%E8%83%BD%E5%8F%AA%E6%9C%89%E4%B8%80%E4%B8%AA%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E6%9C%80%E7%BB%88%E5%BE%97%E4%BB%A5%E5%AE%9E%E7%8E%B0%EF%BC%8C%E4%BD%86%E5%85%B6%E4%BB%96%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BB%8D%E7%84%B6%E6%9C%89%E6%95%88%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%B8%8D%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E7%94%B1%E5%90%91%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%BB%E5%BC%A0%E8%BF%9D%E7%BA%A6%E8%B4%A3%E4%BB%BB%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E" _color="#dc2d1e">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(5)债权具有平等性。" _mubu_text="(5)%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E5%85%B7%E6%9C%89%E5%B9%B3%E7%AD%89%E6%80%A7%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="对于同一债务人先后成立的数个债权，效力一律平等。" _mubu_text="%E5%AF%B9%E4%BA%8E%E5%90%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E5%85%88%E5%90%8E%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E7%9A%84%E6%95%B0%E4%B8%AA%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%8C%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%E4%B8%80%E5%BE%8B%E5%B9%B3%E7%AD%89%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="在该债务人陷入破产时，数个债权人则根据债权数额的比例接受清偿。" _mubu_text="%E5%9C%A8%E8%AF%A5%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E9%99%B7%E5%85%A5%E7%A0%B4%E4%BA%A7%E6%97%B6%EF%BC%8C%E6%95%B0%E4%B8%AA%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E5%88%99%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E6%95%B0%E9%A2%9D%E7%9A%84%E6%AF%94%E4%BE%8B%E6%8E%A5%E5%8F%97%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="309.简述债权的权能❶" _mubu_text="309.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%83%E8%83%BD%E2%9D%B6">
		<outline text="债权的权能" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%83%E8%83%BD%3C/span%3E" _note="@简答题&nbsp;@题眼&nbsp;@口诀&nbsp;翟泉能请爆兽全出" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E9%A2%98%E7%9C%BC%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E7%BF%9F%E6%B3%89%E8%83%BD%E8%AF%B7%E7%88%86%E5%85%BD%E5%85%A8%E5%87%BA" _heading="1" _color="#dc2d1e">
		<outline text="(1)请求权能。" _mubu_text="(1)%E8%AF%B7%E6%B1%82%E6%9D%83%E8%83%BD%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="作为一种请求权，债权人可以直接请求债务人履行债务，也可以通过诉讼方式以国家强制力来实现其请求。" _mubu_text="%E4%BD%9C%E4%B8%BA%E4%B8%80%E7%A7%8D%E8%AF%B7%E6%B1%82%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E7%9B%B4%E6%8E%A5%E8%AF%B7%E6%B1%82%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%EF%BC%8C%E4%B9%9F%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E9%80%9A%E8%BF%87%E8%AF%89%E8%AE%BC%E6%96%B9%E5%BC%8F%E4%BB%A5%E5%9B%BD%E5%AE%B6%E5%BC%BA%E5%88%B6%E5%8A%9B%E6%9D%A5%E5%AE%9E%E7%8E%B0%E5%85%B6%E8%AF%B7%E6%B1%82%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(2)保持受领权能。" _mubu_text="(2)%E4%BF%9D%E6%8C%81%E5%8F%97%E9%A2%86%E6%9D%83%E8%83%BD%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="债权的存在是债权人受领债务人给付的合法原因。债务人履行债务或受强制执行提出给付时，债权人有接受给付的权利并有权保持因此获得的利益。" _mubu_text="%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E5%AD%98%E5%9C%A8%E6%98%AF%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%97%E9%A2%86%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E7%9A%84%E5%90%88%E6%B3%95%E5%8E%9F%E5%9B%A0%E3%80%82%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E6%88%96%E5%8F%97%E5%BC%BA%E5%88%B6%E6%89%A7%E8%A1%8C%E6%8F%90%E5%87%BA%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E6%97%B6%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E6%9C%89%E6%8E%A5%E5%8F%97%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E5%B9%B6%E6%9C%89%E6%9D%83%E4%BF%9D%E6%8C%81%E5%9B%A0%E6%AD%A4%E8%8E%B7%E5%BE%97%E7%9A%84%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(3)保全权能。" _mubu_text="(3)%E4%BF%9D%E5%85%A8%E6%9D%83%E8%83%BD%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="当债务人的某些行为对债权人造成损害时,债权人可以向人民法院请求以自己的名义代位行使债务人的债权，或者请求人民法院撤销债务人的行为。债权人享有的债权保全权能是对债的相对性原理的突破。" _mubu_text="%E5%BD%93%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%9F%90%E4%BA%9B%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E5%AF%B9%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E9%80%A0%E6%88%90%E6%8D%9F%E5%AE%B3%E6%97%B6,%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E5%90%91%E4%BA%BA%E6%B0%91%E6%B3%95%E9%99%A2%E8%AF%B7%E6%B1%82%E4%BB%A5%E8%87%AA%E5%B7%B1%E7%9A%84%E5%90%8D%E4%B9%89%E4%BB%A3%E4%BD%8D%E8%A1%8C%E4%BD%BF%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%8C%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E8%AF%B7%E6%B1%82%E4%BA%BA%E6%B0%91%E6%B3%95%E9%99%A2%E6%92%A4%E9%94%80%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E3%80%82%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E4%BA%AB%E6%9C%89%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BF%9D%E5%85%A8%E6%9D%83%E8%83%BD%E6%98%AF%E5%AF%B9%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E7%9B%B8%E5%AF%B9%E6%80%A7%E5%8E%9F%E7%90%86%E7%9A%84%E7%AA%81%E7%A0%B4%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(4)处分权能。" _mubu_text="(4)%E5%A4%84%E5%88%86%E6%9D%83%E8%83%BD%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="债权人可通过抵销、免除、让与债权和设定债权质权等方式对享有的债权予以处分。" _mubu_text="%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%AF%E9%80%9A%E8%BF%87%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E3%80%81%E5%85%8D%E9%99%A4%E3%80%81%E8%AE%A9%E4%B8%8E%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E5%92%8C%E8%AE%BE%E5%AE%9A%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E8%B4%A8%E6%9D%83%E7%AD%89%E6%96%B9%E5%BC%8F%E5%AF%B9%E4%BA%AB%E6%9C%89%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%88%E4%BB%A5%E5%A4%84%E5%88%86%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="上述权能齐备的债权为完全债权，否则为不完全债权，但欠缺保持受领权能的债权不再是债权。" _mubu_text="%E4%B8%8A%E8%BF%B0%E6%9D%83%E8%83%BD%E9%BD%90%E5%A4%87%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%B8%BA%E5%AE%8C%E5%85%A8%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%8C%E5%90%A6%E5%88%99%E4%B8%BA%E4%B8%8D%E5%AE%8C%E5%85%A8%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%8C%E4%BD%86%E6%AC%A0%E7%BC%BA%E4%BF%9D%E6%8C%81%E5%8F%97%E9%A2%86%E6%9D%83%E8%83%BD%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%B8%8D%E5%86%8D%E6%98%AF%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="310.简述债务的特征❶" _mubu_text="310.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E7%9A%84%E7%89%B9%E5%BE%81%E2%9D%B6">
		<outline text="债务的特征" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E7%9A%84%E7%89%B9%E5%BE%81%3C/span%3E" _note="@简答题&nbsp;@口诀&nbsp;宅吴峥特泣墙" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E5%AE%85%E5%90%B4%E5%B3%A5%E7%89%B9%E6%B3%A3%E5%A2%99" _heading="1" _color="#3da8f5">
		<outline text="债务的概念" _mubu_text="%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="债务是指债务人依照约定或法律规定向债权人作出给付的义务。" _mubu_text="%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E4%BE%9D%E7%85%A7%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E6%88%96%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E5%90%91%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E7%9A%84%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(1)债务具有特定性。" _mubu_text="(1)%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E5%85%B7%E6%9C%89%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E6%80%A7%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="在任何债之关系中，债务人均是特定的，且债务的内容也是特定的。" _mubu_text="%E5%9C%A8%E4%BB%BB%E4%BD%95%E5%80%BA%E4%B9%8B%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E4%B8%AD%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E5%9D%87%E6%98%AF%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%94%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%3E%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E7%9A%84%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%3C/span%3E%E4%B9%9F%E6%98%AF%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="依法成立的债务非依法律规定或经当事人协商不得变更。" _mubu_text="%E4%BE%9D%E6%B3%95%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E9%9D%9E%E4%BE%9D%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E6%88%96%E7%BB%8F%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E5%8D%8F%E5%95%86%E4%B8%8D%E5%BE%97%E5%8F%98%E6%9B%B4%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(2)债务具有期限性。" _mubu_text="(2)%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E5%85%B7%E6%9C%89%E6%9C%9F%E9%99%90%E6%80%A7%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="任何债务都有确定或可确定的期限。" _mubu_text="%E4%BB%BB%E4%BD%95%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E9%83%BD%E6%9C%89%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%E6%88%96%E5%8F%AF%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E6%9C%9F%E9%99%90%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(3)债务履行具有强制性。" _mubu_text="(3)%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E5%85%B7%E6%9C%89%E5%BC%BA%E5%88%B6%E6%80%A7%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="债务在本质上是债务人应承担的负担，当债务人不履行债务时，债权人有权追究债务人的民事责任以满足其利益。" _mubu_text="%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E5%9C%A8%E6%9C%AC%E8%B4%A8%E4%B8%8A%E6%98%AF%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E5%BA%94%E6%89%BF%E6%8B%85%E7%9A%84%E8%B4%9F%E6%8B%85%EF%BC%8C%E5%BD%93%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%8D%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E6%97%B6%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E6%9C%89%E6%9D%83%E8%BF%BD%E7%A9%B6%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%B0%91%E4%BA%8B%E8%B4%A3%E4%BB%BB%E4%BB%A5%E6%BB%A1%E8%B6%B3%E5%85%B6%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="责任是债务人履行债务的一种担保，无责任的债务无法律约束力。" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E8%B4%A3%E4%BB%BB%E6%98%AF%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%80%E7%A7%8D%E6%8B%85%E4%BF%9D%EF%BC%8C%E6%97%A0%E8%B4%A3%E4%BB%BB%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E6%97%A0%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E7%BA%A6%E6%9D%9F%E5%8A%9B%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="311.简述选择之债特定化的方式" _mubu_text="311.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E9%80%89%E6%8B%A9%E4%B9%8B%E5%80%BA%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E5%8C%96%E7%9A%84%E6%96%B9%E5%BC%8F">
		<outline text="选择之债的特定化方式有三种:" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E9%80%89%E6%8B%A9%E4%B9%8B%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E5%8C%96%E6%96%B9%E5%BC%8F%E6%9C%89%E4%B8%89%E7%A7%8D:%3C/span%3E" _note="@简答题&nbsp;@口诀&nbsp;炫宅定河全省" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E7%82%AB%E5%AE%85%E5%AE%9A%E6%B2%B3%E5%85%A8%E7%9C%81" _heading="1" _color="#3da8f5">
		<outline text="一是在履行时由当事人合意选定给付标的；" _mubu_text="%E4%B8%80%E6%98%AF%E5%9C%A8%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%97%B6%E7%94%B1%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%3E%E5%90%88%3C/span%3E%E6%84%8F%E9%80%89%E5%AE%9A%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%9B">
		</outline>
		<outline text="二是有选择权的当事人行使选择权予以特定；" _mubu_text="%E4%BA%8C%E6%98%AF%E6%9C%89%E9%80%89%E6%8B%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E8%A1%8C%E4%BD%BF%E9%80%89%E6%8B%A9%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%88%E4%BB%A5%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%EF%BC%9B">
		<outline text="其中，当事人行使选择权使选择之债的给付标的特定是最常见方式，该选择权在性质上为形成权，选择权行使后不得撤回，效力溯及到债之发生时。" _mubu_text="%E5%85%B6%E4%B8%AD%EF%BC%8C%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E8%A1%8C%E4%BD%BF%E9%80%89%E6%8B%A9%E6%9D%83%E4%BD%BF%E9%80%89%E6%8B%A9%E4%B9%8B%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E6%98%AF%E6%9C%80%E5%B8%B8%E8%A7%81%E6%96%B9%E5%BC%8F%EF%BC%8C%E8%AF%A5%E9%80%89%E6%8B%A9%E6%9D%83%E5%9C%A8%E6%80%A7%E8%B4%A8%E4%B8%8A%E4%B8%BA%E5%BD%A2%E6%88%90%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%8C%E9%80%89%E6%8B%A9%E6%9D%83%E8%A1%8C%E4%BD%BF%E5%90%8E%E4%B8%8D%E5%BE%97%E6%92%A4%E5%9B%9E%EF%BC%8C%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%E6%BA%AF%E5%8F%8A%E5%88%B0%E5%80%BA%E4%B9%8B%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E6%97%B6%E3%80%82" _note="@考点" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E8%80%83%E7%82%B9%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		<outline text="确定选择权归属的原则是" _mubu_text="%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%E9%80%89%E6%8B%A9%E6%9D%83%E5%BD%92%E5%B1%9E%E7%9A%84%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99%E6%98%AF">
		<outline text="依法律直接规定发生的选择之债，选择权的归属由法律直接规定；" _mubu_text="%E4%BE%9D%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E7%9B%B4%E6%8E%A5%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E7%9A%84%E9%80%89%E6%8B%A9%E4%B9%8B%E5%80%BA%EF%BC%8C%E9%80%89%E6%8B%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E5%BD%92%E5%B1%9E%E7%94%B1%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E7%9B%B4%E6%8E%A5%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%EF%BC%9B">
		</outline>
		<outline text="依合同发生的选择之债，由当事人约定选择权的归属。" _mubu_text="%E4%BE%9D%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E7%9A%84%E9%80%89%E6%8B%A9%E4%B9%8B%E5%80%BA%EF%BC%8C%E7%94%B1%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E9%80%89%E6%8B%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E5%BD%92%E5%B1%9E%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="既无法律规定又无约定的，选择权应当属于债务人。" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%97%A2%E6%97%A0%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E5%8F%88%E6%97%A0%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E9%80%89%E6%8B%A9%E6%9D%83%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E5%B1%9E%E4%BA%8E%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E" _note="@考点" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E8%80%83%E7%82%B9%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="三是因其他标的发生履行不能而只剩下一种可给付的标的。" _mubu_text="%E4%B8%89%E6%98%AF%E5%9B%A0%E5%85%B6%E4%BB%96%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%8D%E8%83%BD%E8%80%8C%E5%8F%AA%E5%89%A9%E4%B8%8B%E4%B8%80%E7%A7%8D%E5%8F%AF%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E7%9A%84%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="312.简述区分简单之债与选择之债的意义" _mubu_text="312.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E5%8C%BA%E5%88%86%E7%AE%80%E5%8D%95%E4%B9%8B%E5%80%BA%E4%B8%8E%E9%80%89%E6%8B%A9%E4%B9%8B%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%84%8F%E4%B9%89">
		<outline text="区分简单之债与选择之债的意义" _mubu_text="%E5%8C%BA%E5%88%86%E7%AE%80%E5%8D%95%E4%B9%8B%E5%80%BA%E4%B8%8E%E9%80%89%E6%8B%A9%E4%B9%8B%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%84%8F%E4%B9%89">
		<outline text="其一，简单之债中当事人只能给付约定的标的，不能以其他标的替代；选择之债中的给付标的须以一定方法特定使之转化为简单之债后才能履行。" _mubu_text="%E5%85%B6%E4%B8%80%EF%BC%8C%E7%AE%80%E5%8D%95%E4%B9%8B%E5%80%BA%E4%B8%AD%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%AA%E8%83%BD%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%8D%E8%83%BD%E4%BB%A5%E5%85%B6%E4%BB%96%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E6%9B%BF%E4%BB%A3%EF%BC%9B%E9%80%89%E6%8B%A9%E4%B9%8B%E5%80%BA%E4%B8%AD%E7%9A%84%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E9%A1%BB%E4%BB%A5%E4%B8%80%E5%AE%9A%E6%96%B9%E6%B3%95%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E4%BD%BF%E4%B9%8B%E8%BD%AC%E5%8C%96%E4%B8%BA%E7%AE%80%E5%8D%95%E4%B9%8B%E5%80%BA%E5%90%8E%E6%89%8D%E8%83%BD%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="其二，简单之债的给付标的无法履行时发生履行不能；选择之债的给付标的全部无法履行时才发生履行不能。" _mubu_text="%E5%85%B6%E4%BA%8C%EF%BC%8C%E7%AE%80%E5%8D%95%E4%B9%8B%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E6%97%A0%E6%B3%95%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%97%B6%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%8D%E8%83%BD%EF%BC%9B%E9%80%89%E6%8B%A9%E4%B9%8B%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E5%85%A8%E9%83%A8%E6%97%A0%E6%B3%95%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%97%B6%E6%89%8D%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%8D%E8%83%BD%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="313.简述特定物之债与种类物之债的区别" _mubu_text="313.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E7%89%A9%E4%B9%8B%E5%80%BA%E4%B8%8E%E7%A7%8D%E7%B1%BB%E7%89%A9%E4%B9%8B%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%8C%BA%E5%88%AB">
		<outline text="两者的区别主要有:" _mubu_text="%E4%B8%A4%E8%80%85%E7%9A%84%E5%8C%BA%E5%88%AB%E4%B8%BB%E8%A6%81%E6%9C%89:" _note="@考点" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E8%80%83%E7%82%B9%3C/span%3E">
		<outline text="第一，特定物之债中的债务人必须交付特定物。如果该特定物在交付前毀损、灭失，则发生债的履行不能，债务人免除继续履行的责任；而在种类物之债中，除该类型的种类物全部灭失外，不存在履行不能的问题。" _mubu_text="%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%80%EF%BC%8C%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E7%89%A9%E4%B9%8B%E5%80%BA%E4%B8%AD%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E5%BF%85%E9%A1%BB%E4%BA%A4%E4%BB%98%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E7%89%A9%E3%80%82%E5%A6%82%E6%9E%9C%E8%AF%A5%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E7%89%A9%E5%9C%A8%E4%BA%A4%E4%BB%98%E5%89%8D%E6%AF%80%E6%8D%9F%E3%80%81%E7%81%AD%E5%A4%B1%EF%BC%8C%E5%88%99%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%8D%E8%83%BD%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E5%85%8D%E9%99%A4%E7%BB%A7%E7%BB%AD%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E7%9A%84%E8%B4%A3%E4%BB%BB%EF%BC%9B%E8%80%8C%E5%9C%A8%E7%A7%8D%E7%B1%BB%E7%89%A9%E4%B9%8B%E5%80%BA%E4%B8%AD%EF%BC%8C%E9%99%A4%E8%AF%A5%E7%B1%BB%E5%9E%8B%E7%9A%84%E7%A7%8D%E7%B1%BB%E7%89%A9%E5%85%A8%E9%83%A8%E7%81%AD%E5%A4%B1%E5%A4%96%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%8D%E5%AD%98%E5%9C%A8%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%8D%E8%83%BD%E7%9A%84%E9%97%AE%E9%A2%98%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="第二，在特定物之债中，标的物的所有权转移时间和风险负担的转移时间可以由当事人约定或由法律规定；在种类物之债中，标的物的所有权转移时间和风险负担的转移时间只能是标的物交付之时。" _mubu_text="%E7%AC%AC%E4%BA%8C%EF%BC%8C%E5%9C%A8%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E7%89%A9%E4%B9%8B%E5%80%BA%E4%B8%AD%EF%BC%8C%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E7%89%A9%E7%9A%84%E6%89%80%E6%9C%89%E6%9D%83%E8%BD%AC%E7%A7%BB%E6%97%B6%E9%97%B4%E5%92%8C%E9%A3%8E%E9%99%A9%E8%B4%9F%E6%8B%85%E7%9A%84%E8%BD%AC%E7%A7%BB%E6%97%B6%E9%97%B4%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E7%94%B1%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E6%88%96%E7%94%B1%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%EF%BC%9B%E5%9C%A8%E7%A7%8D%E7%B1%BB%E7%89%A9%E4%B9%8B%E5%80%BA%E4%B8%AD%EF%BC%8C%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E7%89%A9%E7%9A%84%E6%89%80%E6%9C%89%E6%9D%83%E8%BD%AC%E7%A7%BB%E6%97%B6%E9%97%B4%E5%92%8C%E9%A3%8E%E9%99%A9%E8%B4%9F%E6%8B%85%E7%9A%84%E8%BD%AC%E7%A7%BB%E6%97%B6%E9%97%B4%E5%8F%AA%E8%83%BD%E6%98%AF%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E7%89%A9%E4%BA%A4%E4%BB%98%E4%B9%8B%E6%97%B6%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="314.简述债的发生根据" _mubu_text="314.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE">
		<outline text="债的发生根据的概念" _mubu_text="%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="债的发生根据，是指能够在特定当事人之间引起债之关系产生的法律事实，引起债之关系发生的法律事实既可以是行为也可以是事件，其中行为包括表示行为和事实行为。" _mubu_text="%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE%EF%BC%8C%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E8%83%BD%E5%A4%9F%E5%9C%A8%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%B9%8B%E9%97%B4%E5%BC%95%E8%B5%B7%E5%80%BA%E4%B9%8B%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E4%BA%A7%E7%94%9F%E7%9A%84%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E4%BA%8B%E5%AE%9E%EF%BC%8C%E5%BC%95%E8%B5%B7%E5%80%BA%E4%B9%8B%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E7%9A%84%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E4%BA%8B%E5%AE%9E%E6%97%A2%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E6%98%AF%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E4%B9%9F%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E6%98%AF%E4%BA%8B%E4%BB%B6%EF%BC%8C%E5%85%B6%E4%B8%AD%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E5%8C%85%E6%8B%AC%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E5%92%8C%E4%BA%8B%E5%AE%9E%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%3C/span%3E%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="债的发生根据包括" _mubu_text="%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE%E5%8C%85%E6%8B%AC">
		<outline text="（1）合同" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C">
		<outline text="合同依法成立后，当事人之间即产生债权债务关系，故合同是债的发生原因之一。" _mubu_text="%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E4%BE%9D%E6%B3%95%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E5%90%8E%EF%BC%8C%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%B9%8B%E9%97%B4%E5%8D%B3%E4%BA%A7%E7%94%9F%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%EF%BC%8C%E6%95%85%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%98%AF%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E5%8E%9F%E5%9B%A0%E4%B9%8B%E4%B8%80%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="（2）侵权行为" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%E4%BE%B5%E6%9D%83%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA">
		<outline text="侵权行为发生后，侵权人与受害人之间即产生债权债务关系，故侵权行为也是债的发生原因之一。" _mubu_text="%E4%BE%B5%E6%9D%83%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E5%90%8E%EF%BC%8C%E4%BE%B5%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%8E%E5%8F%97%E5%AE%B3%E4%BA%BA%E4%B9%8B%E9%97%B4%E5%8D%B3%E4%BA%A7%E7%94%9F%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%EF%BC%8C%E6%95%85%E4%BE%B5%E6%9D%83%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E4%B9%9F%E6%98%AF%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E5%8E%9F%E5%9B%A0%E4%B9%8B%E4%B8%80%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="（3）无因管理" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%E6%97%A0%E5%9B%A0%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86">
		<outline text="无因管理能够依法在管理人与受益人之间引起债的关系，故无因管理是债发生的法定原因之一。" _mubu_text="%E6%97%A0%E5%9B%A0%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E8%83%BD%E5%A4%9F%E4%BE%9D%E6%B3%95%E5%9C%A8%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%8E%E5%8F%97%E7%9B%8A%E4%BA%BA%E4%B9%8B%E9%97%B4%E5%BC%95%E8%B5%B7%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%EF%BC%8C%E6%95%85%E6%97%A0%E5%9B%A0%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E6%98%AF%E5%80%BA%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E7%9A%84%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E5%8E%9F%E5%9B%A0%E4%B9%8B%E4%B8%80%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="（4）不当得利" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%884%EF%BC%89%E4%B8%8D%E5%BD%93%E5%BE%97%E5%88%A9">
		<outline text="不当得利是可以引起债发生的法律事实之一，因不当得利所产生的债称为不当得利之债。" _mubu_text="%E4%B8%8D%E5%BD%93%E5%BE%97%E5%88%A9%E6%98%AF%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E5%BC%95%E8%B5%B7%E5%80%BA%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E7%9A%84%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E4%BA%8B%E5%AE%9E%E4%B9%8B%E4%B8%80%EF%BC%8C%E5%9B%A0%E4%B8%8D%E5%BD%93%E5%BE%97%E5%88%A9%E6%89%80%E4%BA%A7%E7%94%9F%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E7%A7%B0%E4%B8%BA%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E4%B8%8D%E5%BD%93%E5%BE%97%E5%88%A9%E4%B9%8B%E5%80%BA%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="（5）其他事实" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%885%EF%BC%89%E5%85%B6%E4%BB%96%E4%BA%8B%E5%AE%9E">
		<outline text="除上述债发生的主要原因外，根据各国或地区规定，单方允诺、缔约过失、遗赠等也可以成为债的发生根据。" _mubu_text="%E9%99%A4%E4%B8%8A%E8%BF%B0%E5%80%BA%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%BB%E8%A6%81%E5%8E%9F%E5%9B%A0%E5%A4%96%EF%BC%8C%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE%E5%90%84%E5%9B%BD%E6%88%96%E5%9C%B0%E5%8C%BA%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%8D%95%E6%96%B9%E5%85%81%E8%AF%BA%E3%80%81%E7%BC%94%E7%BA%A6%E8%BF%87%E5%A4%B1%E3%80%81%E9%81%97%E8%B5%A0%E7%AD%89%E4%B9%9F%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E6%88%90%E4%B8%BA%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>

		<outline text="315.简述债的内容变更的特征" _mubu_text="315.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E5%8F%98%E6%9B%B4%E7%9A%84%E7%89%B9%E5%BE%81">
		<outline text="债的内容变更的概念" _mubu_text="%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E5%8F%98%E6%9B%B4%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="债的内容变更是指在不改变债的主体的情况下对债的内容予以改变，如改变标的物、改变履行条件、改变所附条件、改变担保等。" _mubu_text="%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E5%8F%98%E6%9B%B4%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%9C%A8%E4%B8%8D%E6%94%B9%E5%8F%98%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%BB%E4%BD%93%E7%9A%84%E6%83%85%E5%86%B5%E4%B8%8B%E5%AF%B9%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E4%BA%88%E4%BB%A5%E6%94%B9%E5%8F%98%EF%BC%8C%E5%A6%82%E6%94%B9%E5%8F%98%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E7%89%A9%E3%80%81%E6%94%B9%E5%8F%98%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E3%80%81%E6%94%B9%E5%8F%98%E6%89%80%E9%99%84%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E3%80%81%E6%94%B9%E5%8F%98%E6%8B%85%E4%BF%9D%E7%AD%89%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="债的内容改变的特征" _mubu_text="%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E6%94%B9%E5%8F%98%E7%9A%84%E7%89%B9%E5%BE%81">
		<outline text="（1）变更以原债有效为前提;" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E5%8F%98%E6%9B%B4%E4%BB%A5%E5%8E%9F%E5%80%BA%E6%9C%89%E6%95%88%E4%B8%BA%E5%89%8D%E6%8F%90;">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（2）变更的是债的内容而非债的主体;" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%E5%8F%98%E6%9B%B4%E7%9A%84%E6%98%AF%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E8%80%8C%E9%9D%9E%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%BB%E4%BD%93;">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（3）变更之后，债的关系仍然有效。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%E5%8F%98%E6%9B%B4%E4%B9%8B%E5%90%8E%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E4%BB%8D%E7%84%B6%E6%9C%89%E6%95%88%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（4）如系合同内容变更，须经当事人协商一致，如果当事人对合同变更的内容约定不明确的，推定为合同未变更。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%884%EF%BC%89%E5%A6%82%E7%B3%BB%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E5%8F%98%E6%9B%B4%EF%BC%8C%E9%A1%BB%E7%BB%8F%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E5%8D%8F%E5%95%86%E4%B8%80%E8%87%B4%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%A6%82%E6%9E%9C%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E5%AF%B9%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E5%8F%98%E6%9B%B4%E7%9A%84%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E4%B8%8D%E6%98%8E%E7%A1%AE%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E6%8E%A8%E5%AE%9A%E4%B8%BA%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%9C%AA%E5%8F%98%E6%9B%B4%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（5）法律、行政法规规定应当办理批准、登记等手续的，依照其规定。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%885%EF%BC%89%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E3%80%81%E8%A1%8C%E6%94%BF%E6%B3%95%E8%A7%84%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E5%8A%9E%E7%90%86%E6%89%B9%E5%87%86%E3%80%81%E7%99%BB%E8%AE%B0%E7%AD%89%E6%89%8B%E7%BB%AD%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E4%BE%9D%E7%85%A7%E5%85%B6%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（6）合同变更后，当事人应当按照变更后的合同履行，但合同变更对已按原合同所作的履行没有追及力。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%886%EF%BC%89%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E5%8F%98%E6%9B%B4%E5%90%8E%EF%BC%8C%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E6%8C%89%E7%85%A7%E5%8F%98%E6%9B%B4%E5%90%8E%E7%9A%84%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%EF%BC%8C%E4%BD%86%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E5%8F%98%E6%9B%B4%E5%AF%B9%E5%B7%B2%E6%8C%89%E5%8E%9F%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%89%80%E4%BD%9C%E7%9A%84%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%B2%A1%E6%9C%89%E8%BF%BD%E5%8F%8A%E5%8A%9B%E3%80%82" _note="意思是原合同已经履行的部分继续有效" _mubu_note="%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E6%98%AF%E5%8E%9F%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E5%B7%B2%E7%BB%8F%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E7%9A%84%E9%83%A8%E5%88%86%E7%BB%A7%E7%BB%AD%E6%9C%89%E6%95%88">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（7）同时，合同的变更也不影响当事人要求赔偿损失的权利。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%887%EF%BC%89%E5%90%8C%E6%97%B6%EF%BC%8C%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E5%8F%98%E6%9B%B4%E4%B9%9F%E4%B8%8D%E5%BD%B1%E5%93%8D%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E8%A6%81%E6%B1%82%E8%B5%94%E5%81%BF%E6%8D%9F%E5%A4%B1%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>

		<outline text="5月11日" _mubu_text="5%E6%9C%8811%E6%97%A5">
		<outline text="316.简述债权让与的条件、效力、不得转让的债权" _mubu_text="316.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E8%AE%A9%E4%B8%8E%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E3%80%81%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%E3%80%81%E4%B8%8D%E5%BE%97%E8%BD%AC%E8%AE%A9%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83">
		<outline text="债权让与的概念" _mubu_text="%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E8%AE%A9%E4%B8%8E%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="债权让与，是指在不改变债的内容的前提下，债权人与第三人订立合同将其债权移转给第三人享有。其中债权人称为让与人，第三人称为受让人。" _mubu_text="%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E8%AE%A9%E4%B8%8E%EF%BC%8C%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%9C%A8%E4%B8%8D%E6%94%B9%E5%8F%98%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E7%9A%84%E5%89%8D%E6%8F%90%E4%B8%8B%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%8E%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%E8%AE%A2%E7%AB%8B%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E5%B0%86%E5%85%B6%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E7%A7%BB%E8%BD%AC%E7%BB%99%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%E4%BA%AB%E6%9C%89%E3%80%82%E5%85%B6%E4%B8%AD%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E7%A7%B0%E4%B8%BA%E8%AE%A9%E4%B8%8E%E4%BA%BA%EF%BC%8C%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%E7%A7%B0%E4%B8%BA%E5%8F%97%E8%AE%A9%E4%BA%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="债权让与的分类" _mubu_text="%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E8%AE%A9%E4%B8%8E%E7%9A%84%E5%88%86%E7%B1%BB">
		<outline text="全部让与" _mubu_text="%E5%85%A8%E9%83%A8%E8%AE%A9%E4%B8%8E">
		<outline text="是指债权人将其债权全部转让给第三人享有,并在转让协议生效后退出该债之关系,使受让入成为债权人。" _mubu_text="%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E5%B0%86%E5%85%B6%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E5%85%A8%E9%83%A8%E8%BD%AC%E8%AE%A9%E7%BB%99%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%E4%BA%AB%E6%9C%89,%E5%B9%B6%E5%9C%A8%E8%BD%AC%E8%AE%A9%E5%8D%8F%E8%AE%AE%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E5%90%8E%E9%80%80%E5%87%BA%E8%AF%A5%E5%80%BA%E4%B9%8B%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB,%E4%BD%BF%E5%8F%97%E8%AE%A9%E5%85%A5%E6%88%90%E4%B8%BA%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="部分让与。" _mubu_text="%E9%83%A8%E5%88%86%E8%AE%A9%E4%B8%8E%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="是指债权人将其债权部分转让给第三人享有,但其在转让协议生效后并不退出债之关系,而是与受让人共同成为债权人。" _mubu_text="%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E5%B0%86%E5%85%B6%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E9%83%A8%E5%88%86%E8%BD%AC%E8%AE%A9%E7%BB%99%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%E4%BA%AB%E6%9C%89,%E4%BD%86%E5%85%B6%E5%9C%A8%E8%BD%AC%E8%AE%A9%E5%8D%8F%E8%AE%AE%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E5%90%8E%E5%B9%B6%E4%B8%8D%E9%80%80%E5%87%BA%E5%80%BA%E4%B9%8B%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB,%E8%80%8C%E6%98%AF%E4%B8%8E%E5%8F%97%E8%AE%A9%E4%BA%BA%E5%85%B1%E5%90%8C%E6%88%90%E4%B8%BA%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="转让协议对转让的债权份额有约定时，在让与人与受让人之间成立按份债权;" _mubu_text="%E8%BD%AC%E8%AE%A9%E5%8D%8F%E8%AE%AE%E5%AF%B9%E8%BD%AC%E8%AE%A9%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BB%BD%E9%A2%9D%E6%9C%89%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E6%97%B6%EF%BC%8C%E5%9C%A8%E8%AE%A9%E4%B8%8E%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%8E%E5%8F%97%E8%AE%A9%E4%BA%BA%E4%B9%8B%E9%97%B4%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E6%8C%89%E4%BB%BD%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83;">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="成立连带债权" _mubu_text="%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E8%BF%9E%E5%B8%A6%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83">
		<outline text="如果双方对转让的债权份额没有约定的，则在让与人与受让人之间成立连带债权。" _mubu_text="%E5%A6%82%E6%9E%9C%E5%8F%8C%E6%96%B9%E5%AF%B9%E8%BD%AC%E8%AE%A9%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BB%BD%E9%A2%9D%E6%B2%A1%E6%9C%89%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E5%88%99%E5%9C%A8%E8%AE%A9%E4%B8%8E%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%8E%E5%8F%97%E8%AE%A9%E4%BA%BA%E4%B9%8B%E9%97%B4%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E8%BF%9E%E5%B8%A6%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E3%80%82" _note="@考点" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E8%80%83%E7%82%B9%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		</outline>

		<outline text="通过合同方式让与债权的条件" _mubu_text="%E9%80%9A%E8%BF%87%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%96%B9%E5%BC%8F%E8%AE%A9%E4%B8%8E%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6">
		<outline text="(1)存在有效的债权。" _mubu_text="(1)%E5%AD%98%E5%9C%A8%E6%9C%89%E6%95%88%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="此处有效的债权包括:" _mubu_text="%E6%AD%A4%E5%A4%84%E6%9C%89%E6%95%88%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E5%8C%85%E6%8B%AC:" _note="@考点" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E8%80%83%E7%82%B9%3C/span%3E">
		<outline text="诉讼时效已经完成的债权;" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E8%AF%89%E8%AE%BC%E6%97%B6%E6%95%88%E5%B7%B2%E7%BB%8F%E5%AE%8C%E6%88%90%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83;%3C/span%3E">
		<outline text="我国适用诉讼时效抗辩发生主义，法院不得主动适用诉讼时效。当事人未提出诉讼时效抗辩的，属于自动放弃有关的权利。所以此种债权也被归为有效债权。" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%88%91%E5%9B%BD%E9%80%82%E7%94%A8%E8%AF%89%E8%AE%BC%E6%97%B6%E6%95%88%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E4%B8%BB%E4%B9%89%EF%BC%8C%E6%B3%95%E9%99%A2%E4%B8%8D%E5%BE%97%E4%B8%BB%E5%8A%A8%E9%80%82%E7%94%A8%E8%AF%89%E8%AE%BC%E6%97%B6%E6%95%88%E3%80%82%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E6%9C%AA%E6%8F%90%E5%87%BA%E8%AF%89%E8%AE%BC%E6%97%B6%E6%95%88%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E5%B1%9E%E4%BA%8E%E8%87%AA%E5%8A%A8%E6%94%BE%E5%BC%83%E6%9C%89%E5%85%B3%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E3%80%82%E6%89%80%E4%BB%A5%E6%AD%A4%E7%A7%8D%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%B9%9F%E8%A2%AB%E5%BD%92%E4%B8%BA%E6%9C%89%E6%95%88%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="可撤销但尚未撤销的债权;" _mubu_text="%E5%8F%AF%E6%92%A4%E9%94%80%E4%BD%86%E5%B0%9A%E6%9C%AA%E6%92%A4%E9%94%80%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83;">
		</outline>
		<outline text="附解除或期限的债权。" _mubu_text="%E9%99%84%E8%A7%A3%E9%99%A4%E6%88%96%E6%9C%9F%E9%99%90%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="(2)原债权人与第三人达成合意且不违反法律规定。" _mubu_text="(2)%E5%8E%9F%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%8E%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%E8%BE%BE%E6%88%90%E5%90%88%E6%84%8F%E4%B8%94%E4%B8%8D%E8%BF%9D%E5%8F%8D%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="(3)债权具有可让与性。" _mubu_text="(3)%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E5%85%B7%E6%9C%89%E5%8F%AF%E8%AE%A9%E4%B8%8E%E6%80%A7%E3%80%82" _note="在现代社会，作为财产权的债权有自由流通的要求。设立债权让与的目的在于尊重债权人对于其债权的自由处分权,并增强债权的利用价值。但各国或地区法律从保护债务人出发,对债权让与作出了一定的限制。" _mubu_note="%E5%9C%A8%E7%8E%B0%E4%BB%A3%E7%A4%BE%E4%BC%9A%EF%BC%8C%E4%BD%9C%E4%B8%BA%E8%B4%A2%E4%BA%A7%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E6%9C%89%E8%87%AA%E7%94%B1%E6%B5%81%E9%80%9A%E7%9A%84%E8%A6%81%E6%B1%82%E3%80%82%E8%AE%BE%E7%AB%8B%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E8%AE%A9%E4%B8%8E%E7%9A%84%E7%9B%AE%E7%9A%84%E5%9C%A8%E4%BA%8E%E5%B0%8A%E9%87%8D%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E5%AF%B9%E4%BA%8E%E5%85%B6%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E8%87%AA%E7%94%B1%E5%A4%84%E5%88%86%E6%9D%83,%E5%B9%B6%E5%A2%9E%E5%BC%BA%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E5%88%A9%E7%94%A8%E4%BB%B7%E5%80%BC%E3%80%82%E4%BD%86%E5%90%84%E5%9B%BD%E6%88%96%E5%9C%B0%E5%8C%BA%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E4%BB%8E%E4%BF%9D%E6%8A%A4%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E5%87%BA%E5%8F%91,%E5%AF%B9%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E8%AE%A9%E4%B8%8E%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E4%BA%86%E4%B8%80%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E9%99%90%E5%88%B6%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="下列债权不得转让:" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E4%B8%8B%E5%88%97%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%B8%8D%E5%BE%97%E8%BD%AC%E8%AE%A9:%3C/span%3E" _note="@简答题&nbsp;@口诀&nbsp;不转债权性约（欲）发" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E4%B8%8D%E8%BD%AC%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E6%80%A7%E7%BA%A6%EF%BC%88%E6%AC%B2%EF%BC%89%E5%8F%91" _heading="1" _color="#3da8f5">
		<outline text="(1)根据性质不得转让的债权。" _mubu_text="(1)%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE%E6%80%A7%E8%B4%A8%E4%B8%8D%E5%BE%97%E8%BD%AC%E8%AE%A9%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E3%80%82" _color="#333333">
		<outline text="①基于当事人之间的特定身份关系发生的债权，如抚养费、赡养费之请求权;" _mubu_text="%E2%91%A0%E5%9F%BA%E4%BA%8E%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%B9%8B%E9%97%B4%E7%9A%84%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E8%BA%AB%E4%BB%BD%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%8C%E5%A6%82%E6%8A%9A%E5%85%BB%E8%B4%B9%E3%80%81%E8%B5%A1%E5%85%BB%E8%B4%B9%E4%B9%8B%E8%AF%B7%E6%B1%82%E6%9D%83;">
		</outline>
		<outline text="②基于当事人之间的信赖关系而发生的债权，如定作人对于承揽人之债权、委托人对于受托人之债权等。" _mubu_text="%E2%91%A1%E5%9F%BA%E4%BA%8E%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%B9%8B%E9%97%B4%E7%9A%84%E4%BF%A1%E8%B5%96%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E8%80%8C%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%8C%E5%A6%82%E5%AE%9A%E4%BD%9C%E4%BA%BA%E5%AF%B9%E4%BA%8E%E6%89%BF%E6%8F%BD%E4%BA%BA%E4%B9%8B%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E3%80%81%E5%A7%94%E6%89%98%E4%BA%BA%E5%AF%B9%E4%BA%8E%E5%8F%97%E6%89%98%E4%BA%BA%E4%B9%8B%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E7%AD%89%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(2)按照当事人约定不得转让的债权。" _mubu_text="(2)%E6%8C%89%E7%85%A7%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E4%B8%8D%E5%BE%97%E8%BD%AC%E8%AE%A9%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="根据债权的性质，一些债权具有可让与性，但如债权人与债务人特别约定该债权不得转让，则债权人不得将该债权让与他人。" _mubu_text="%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E6%80%A7%E8%B4%A8%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%80%E4%BA%9B%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E5%85%B7%E6%9C%89%E5%8F%AF%E8%AE%A9%E4%B8%8E%E6%80%A7%EF%BC%8C%E4%BD%86%E5%A6%82%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%8E%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E7%89%B9%E5%88%AB%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E8%AF%A5%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%B8%8D%E5%BE%97%E8%BD%AC%E8%AE%A9%EF%BC%8C%E5%88%99%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%8D%E5%BE%97%E5%B0%86%E8%AF%A5%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E8%AE%A9%E4%B8%8E%E4%BB%96%E4%BA%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(3)依法律规定不得转让的债权。" _mubu_text="(3)%E4%BE%9D%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E4%B8%8D%E5%BE%97%E8%BD%AC%E8%AE%A9%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="有的债权与社会公共利益有关，因而法律禁止该类债权转让或规定该类债权转让必须经有关部门批准。" _mubu_text="%E6%9C%89%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%B8%8E%E7%A4%BE%E4%BC%9A%E5%85%AC%E5%85%B1%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E6%9C%89%E5%85%B3%EF%BC%8C%E5%9B%A0%E8%80%8C%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E7%A6%81%E6%AD%A2%E8%AF%A5%E7%B1%BB%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E8%BD%AC%E8%AE%A9%E6%88%96%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E8%AF%A5%E7%B1%BB%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E8%BD%AC%E8%AE%A9%E5%BF%85%E9%A1%BB%E7%BB%8F%E6%9C%89%E5%85%B3%E9%83%A8%E9%97%A8%E6%89%B9%E5%87%86%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="债权让与的具体规定" _mubu_text="%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E8%AE%A9%E4%B8%8E%E7%9A%84%E5%85%B7%E4%BD%93%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A" _note="@考点" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E8%80%83%E7%82%B9%3C/span%3E">
		<outline text="（1）债权人让与债权应当通知债务人，未经通知的对债务人不发生效力。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E8%AE%A9%E4%B8%8E%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E9%80%9A%E7%9F%A5%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%EF%BC%8C%E6%9C%AA%E7%BB%8F%E9%80%9A%E7%9F%A5%E7%9A%84%E5%AF%B9%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%8D%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（2）除经受让人同意外，债权转让的通知不得撤销。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%E9%99%A4%E7%BB%8F%E5%8F%97%E8%AE%A9%E4%BA%BA%E5%90%8C%E6%84%8F%E5%A4%96%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E8%BD%AC%E8%AE%A9%E7%9A%84%E9%80%9A%E7%9F%A5%E4%B8%8D%E5%BE%97%E6%92%A4%E9%94%80%E3%80%82">
		</outline>

		<outline text="即让与协议对于债务人的效力" _mubu_text="%E5%8D%B3%E8%AE%A9%E4%B8%8E%E5%8D%8F%E8%AE%AE%E5%AF%B9%E4%BA%8E%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B">

		<outline text="（1）债务人应向受让人履行债务，如债务人向让与人履行债务的，则该履行无效，且不能对抗受让人。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E5%BA%94%E5%90%91%E5%8F%97%E8%AE%A9%E4%BA%BA%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%EF%BC%8C%E5%A6%82%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E5%90%91%E8%AE%A9%E4%B8%8E%E4%BA%BA%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%88%99%E8%AF%A5%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%97%A0%E6%95%88%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%94%E4%B8%8D%E8%83%BD%E5%AF%B9%E6%8A%97%E5%8F%97%E8%AE%A9%E4%BA%BA%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>

		<outline text="免责的债务转移（债务承担）" _mubu_text="%E5%85%8D%E8%B4%A3%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E8%BD%AC%E7%A7%BB%EF%BC%88%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E6%89%BF%E6%8B%85%EF%BC%89">

		<outline text="免责的债务转移，是指原债务人将全部债务移转给第三人承担而脱离债的关系。" _mubu_text="%E5%85%8D%E8%B4%A3%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E8%BD%AC%E7%A7%BB%EF%BC%8C%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%8E%9F%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E5%B0%86%E5%85%A8%E9%83%A8%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E7%A7%BB%E8%BD%AC%E7%BB%99%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%E6%89%BF%E6%8B%85%E8%80%8C%E8%84%B1%E7%A6%BB%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="免责的债务移转的要件" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%85%8D%E8%B4%A3%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E7%A7%BB%E8%BD%AC%E7%9A%84%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6%3C/span%3E" _note="@口诀&nbsp;免责寨主（转）小蟹壳捅他&nbsp;@简答题&nbsp;@题眼" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E5%85%8D%E8%B4%A3%E5%AF%A8%E4%B8%BB%EF%BC%88%E8%BD%AC%EF%BC%89%E5%B0%8F%E8%9F%B9%E5%A3%B3%E6%8D%85%E4%BB%96&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E9%A2%98%E7%9C%BC%3C/span%3E" _heading="1" _color="#dc2d1e">
		<outline text="（1）须存在有效的债务。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E9%A1%BB%E5%AD%98%E5%9C%A8%E6%9C%89%E6%95%88%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（2）须有以债务移转为内容的协议。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%E9%A1%BB%E6%9C%89%E4%BB%A5%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E7%A7%BB%E8%BD%AC%E4%B8%BA%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E7%9A%84%E5%8D%8F%E8%AE%AE%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="该协议可以是第三人与债权人签订的，也可以是第三人与债务人签订的，还可以是债务人、债权人与第三人三方签订的。" _mubu_text="%E8%AF%A5%E5%8D%8F%E8%AE%AE%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E6%98%AF%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%8E%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E7%AD%BE%E8%AE%A2%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E4%B9%9F%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E6%98%AF%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%8E%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E7%AD%BE%E8%AE%A2%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E8%BF%98%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E6%98%AF%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E3%80%81%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%8E%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%89%E6%96%B9%E7%AD%BE%E8%AE%A2%E7%9A%84%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="（3）须债务具有可移转性。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%E9%A1%BB%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E5%85%B7%E6%9C%89%E5%8F%AF%E7%A7%BB%E8%BD%AC%E6%80%A7%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="凡性质上不可移转的债务以及当事人约定不得移转的债务,均不具有可移转性。" _mubu_text="%E5%87%A1%E6%80%A7%E8%B4%A8%E4%B8%8A%E4%B8%8D%E5%8F%AF%E7%A7%BB%E8%BD%AC%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BB%A5%E5%8F%8A%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E4%B8%8D%E5%BE%97%E7%A7%BB%E8%BD%AC%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1,%E5%9D%87%E4%B8%8D%E5%85%B7%E6%9C%89%E5%8F%AF%E7%A7%BB%E8%BD%AC%E6%80%A7%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="（4）须经债权人同意。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%884%EF%BC%89%E9%A1%BB%E7%BB%8F%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E5%90%8C%E6%84%8F%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="在债务移转协议是第三人与债务人签订时，债务移转须经债权人同意。" _mubu_text="%E5%9C%A8%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E7%A7%BB%E8%BD%AC%E5%8D%8F%E8%AE%AE%E6%98%AF%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%8E%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E7%AD%BE%E8%AE%A2%E6%97%B6%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E7%A7%BB%E8%BD%AC%E9%A1%BB%E7%BB%8F%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E5%90%8C%E6%84%8F%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="（5）法律有其他规定的应该依照其规定" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%885%EF%BC%89%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E6%9C%89%E5%85%B6%E4%BB%96%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E5%BA%94%E8%AF%A5%E4%BE%9D%E7%85%A7%E5%85%B6%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A">
		<outline text="此外，法律、行政法规规定债务移转应当办理批准、登记等手续的，依照其规定。" _mubu_text="%E6%AD%A4%E5%A4%96%EF%BC%8C%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E3%80%81%E8%A1%8C%E6%94%BF%E6%B3%95%E8%A7%84%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E7%A7%BB%E8%BD%AC%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E5%8A%9E%E7%90%86%E6%89%B9%E5%87%86%E3%80%81%E7%99%BB%E8%AE%B0%E7%AD%89%E6%89%8B%E7%BB%AD%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E4%BE%9D%E7%85%A7%E5%85%B6%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="合同承受与法定承受的区别" _mubu_text="%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%89%BF%E5%8F%97%E4%B8%8E%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E6%89%BF%E5%8F%97%E7%9A%84%E5%8C%BA%E5%88%AB">
		<outline text="(1)合同承受中的承受人可为任意第三人；法定承受中的承受人只能是法定第三人。" _mubu_text="(1)%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%89%BF%E5%8F%97%E4%B8%AD%E7%9A%84%E6%89%BF%E5%8F%97%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%AF%E4%B8%BA%E4%BB%BB%E6%84%8F%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%EF%BC%9B%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E6%89%BF%E5%8F%97%E4%B8%AD%E7%9A%84%E6%89%BF%E5%8F%97%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%AA%E8%83%BD%E6%98%AF%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%E3%80%82">
