		<outline text="320.简述合同承受应该具备的条件" _mubu_text="320.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%89%BF%E5%8F%97%E5%BA%94%E8%AF%A5%E5%85%B7%E5%A4%87%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6">
		<outline text="合同承受的概念" _mubu_text="%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%89%BF%E5%8F%97%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="合同承受，是指合同的一方当事人经对方当事人同意，与第三人订立合同将其在合同中的债权债务全部或者部分移转给第三人。" _mubu_text="%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%89%BF%E5%8F%97%EF%BC%8C%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E7%BB%8F%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E5%90%8C%E6%84%8F%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%8E%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%E8%AE%A2%E7%AB%8B%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E5%B0%86%E5%85%B6%E5%9C%A8%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E4%B8%AD%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E5%85%A8%E9%83%A8%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E9%83%A8%E5%88%86%E7%A7%BB%E8%BD%AC%E7%BB%99%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="合同承受应具备的条件有" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%89%BF%E5%8F%97%E5%BA%94%E5%85%B7%E5%A4%87%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E6%9C%89%3C/span%3E" _note="@考点&nbsp;@简答题" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E8%80%83%E7%82%B9%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E" _heading="1" _color="#75c940">
		<outline text="(1)合同承受须经合同一方当事人与第三人达成移转协议，并取得合同的对方当事人同意。" _mubu_text="(1)%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%89%BF%E5%8F%97%E9%A1%BB%E7%BB%8F%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%8E%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%E8%BE%BE%E6%88%90%E7%A7%BB%E8%BD%AC%E5%8D%8F%E8%AE%AE%EF%BC%8C%E5%B9%B6%E5%8F%96%E5%BE%97%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E5%90%8C%E6%84%8F%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="(2)被移转的合同须为双务合同。" _mubu_text="(2)%E8%A2%AB%E7%A7%BB%E8%BD%AC%E7%9A%84%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E9%A1%BB%E4%B8%BA%E5%8F%8C%E5%8A%A1%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="(3)法律、行政法规规定必须采取特定形式的，合同承受应遵循法律、行政法规的规定。" _mubu_text="(3)%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E3%80%81%E8%A1%8C%E6%94%BF%E6%B3%95%E8%A7%84%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E5%BF%85%E9%A1%BB%E9%87%87%E5%8F%96%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E5%BD%A2%E5%BC%8F%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%89%BF%E5%8F%97%E5%BA%94%E9%81%B5%E5%BE%AA%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E3%80%81%E8%A1%8C%E6%94%BF%E6%B3%95%E8%A7%84%E7%9A%84%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="321.简述债的消灭原因" _mubu_text="321.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%E5%8E%9F%E5%9B%A0">
		<outline text="债的消灭的概念" _mubu_text="%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="债的消灭，是指因一定的法律事实致使债的关系在客观上不复存在。" _mubu_text="%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%EF%BC%8C%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%9B%A0%E4%B8%80%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E4%BA%8B%E5%AE%9E%E8%87%B4%E4%BD%BF%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E5%9C%A8%E5%AE%A2%E8%A7%82%E4%B8%8A%E4%B8%8D%E5%A4%8D%E5%AD%98%E5%9C%A8%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="债的消灭的特征" _mubu_text="%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%E7%9A%84%E7%89%B9%E5%BE%81">
		<outline text="（1）债权人是为了取得一定的利益才设立债之关系，只有债消灭了债权人才能实现其目的。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E6%98%AF%E4%B8%BA%E4%BA%86%E5%8F%96%E5%BE%97%E4%B8%80%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E6%89%8D%E8%AE%BE%E7%AB%8B%E5%80%BA%E4%B9%8B%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%AA%E6%9C%89%E5%80%BA%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%E4%BA%86%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E6%89%8D%E8%83%BD%E5%AE%9E%E7%8E%B0%E5%85%B6%E7%9B%AE%E7%9A%84%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（2）债的消灭不仅使主债终止，亦使从债一并终止，但债的消灭不影响合同中结算和清理条款的效力。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%E4%B8%8D%E4%BB%85%E4%BD%BF%E4%B8%BB%E5%80%BA%E7%BB%88%E6%AD%A2%EF%BC%8C%E4%BA%A6%E4%BD%BF%E4%BB%8E%E5%80%BA%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B6%E7%BB%88%E6%AD%A2%EF%BC%8C%E4%BD%86%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%E4%B8%8D%E5%BD%B1%E5%93%8D%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E4%B8%AD%E7%BB%93%E7%AE%97%E5%92%8C%E6%B8%85%E7%90%86%E6%9D%A1%E6%AC%BE%E7%9A%84%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（3）债消灭后，当事人之间的权利义务关系终止，债权的担保及从属的权利随之消灭，债权人应将负债字据返还给债务人。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%E5%80%BA%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%E5%90%8E%EF%BC%8C%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%B9%8B%E9%97%B4%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E7%BB%88%E6%AD%A2%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E6%8B%85%E4%BF%9D%E5%8F%8A%E4%BB%8E%E5%B1%9E%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E9%9A%8F%E4%B9%8B%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E5%BA%94%E5%B0%86%E8%B4%9F%E5%80%BA%E5%AD%97%E6%8D%AE%E8%BF%94%E8%BF%98%E7%BB%99%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E3%80%82" _note="@考点" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E8%80%83%E7%82%B9%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（4）同时，当事人应该遵守诚实信用原则，根据交易习惯，履行通知、协助、保密等义务，此种义务在法理学上称之为后合同义务。违反此义务致对方损害的，应承担损害赔偿责任。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%884%EF%BC%89%E5%90%8C%E6%97%B6%EF%BC%8C%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E5%BA%94%E8%AF%A5%E9%81%B5%E5%AE%88%E8%AF%9A%E5%AE%9E%E4%BF%A1%E7%94%A8%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99%EF%BC%8C%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE%E4%BA%A4%E6%98%93%E4%B9%A0%E6%83%AF%EF%BC%8C%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E9%80%9A%E7%9F%A5%E3%80%81%E5%8D%8F%E5%8A%A9%E3%80%81%E4%BF%9D%E5%AF%86%E7%AD%89%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%EF%BC%8C%E6%AD%A4%E7%A7%8D%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E5%9C%A8%E6%B3%95%E7%90%86%E5%AD%A6%E4%B8%8A%E7%A7%B0%E4%B9%8B%E4%B8%BA%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%90%8E%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E%E8%BF%9D%E5%8F%8D%E6%AD%A4%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E8%87%B4%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E6%8D%9F%E5%AE%B3%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E5%BA%94%E6%89%BF%E6%8B%85%E6%8D%9F%E5%AE%B3%E8%B5%94%E5%81%BF%E8%B4%A3%E4%BB%BB%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="债的消灭原因主要有" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%E5%8E%9F%E5%9B%A0%E4%B8%BB%E8%A6%81%E6%9C%89%3C/span%3E" _note="@简答题&nbsp;@题眼&nbsp;@口诀&nbsp;宅灭畅姐地替冕婚" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E9%A2%98%E7%9C%BC%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E5%AE%85%E7%81%AD%E7%95%85%E5%A7%90%E5%9C%B0%E6%9B%BF%E5%86%95%E5%A9%9A" _heading="1" _color="#dc2d1e">
		<outline text="1.清偿。" _mubu_text="1.%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="清偿的概念" _mubu_text="%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="是指债务人依法律规定或合同约定完成义务的行为。" _mubu_text="%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E4%BE%9D%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E6%88%96%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E5%AE%8C%E6%88%90%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E7%9A%84%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="清偿与履行同义，只是清偿是从债的消灭的角度而言，而履行是从债的效力出发强调债务的实现过程。清偿是债消灭的常见原因。" _mubu_text="%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF%E4%B8%8E%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E5%90%8C%E4%B9%89%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%AA%E6%98%AF%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF%E6%98%AF%E4%BB%8E%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%E7%9A%84%E8%A7%92%E5%BA%A6%E8%80%8C%E8%A8%80%EF%BC%8C%E8%80%8C%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%98%AF%E4%BB%8E%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%E5%87%BA%E5%8F%91%E5%BC%BA%E8%B0%83%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E7%9A%84%E5%AE%9E%E7%8E%B0%E8%BF%87%E7%A8%8B%E3%80%82%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF%E6%98%AF%E5%80%BA%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%E7%9A%84%E5%B8%B8%E8%A7%81%E5%8E%9F%E5%9B%A0%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="在清偿中应注意代物清偿与清偿抵充两种特殊情形。" _mubu_text="%E5%9C%A8%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF%E4%B8%AD%E5%BA%94%E6%B3%A8%E6%84%8F%E4%BB%A3%E7%89%A9%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF%E4%B8%8E%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF%E6%8A%B5%E5%85%85%E4%B8%A4%E7%A7%8D%E7%89%B9%E6%AE%8A%E6%83%85%E5%BD%A2%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="代物清偿" _mubu_text="%E4%BB%A3%E7%89%A9%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF">
		<outline text="代物清偿须具备以下要件：" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E4%BB%A3%E7%89%A9%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF%E9%A1%BB%E5%85%B7%E5%A4%87%E4%BB%A5%E4%B8%8B%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6%EF%BC%9A%3C/span%3E" _note="@简答题&nbsp;@题眼@口诀&nbsp;代偿村月河守" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E9%A2%98%E7%9C%BC%3C/span%3E%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E4%BB%A3%E5%81%BF%E6%9D%91%E6%9C%88%E6%B2%B3%E5%AE%88" _heading="1" _color="#dc2d1e">
		<outline text="代物清偿的概念" _mubu_text="%E4%BB%A3%E7%89%A9%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="是指在债的履行过程中，债权人受领他种给付以代替原定给付而使债的关系消灭。" _mubu_text="%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%9C%A8%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E8%BF%87%E7%A8%8B%E4%B8%AD%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%97%E9%A2%86%E4%BB%96%E7%A7%8D%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E4%BB%A5%E4%BB%A3%E6%9B%BF%E5%8E%9F%E5%AE%9A%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E8%80%8C%E4%BD%BF%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(1)有原债务存在；" _mubu_text="(1)%E6%9C%89%E5%8E%9F%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%AD%98%3C/span%3E%E5%9C%A8%EF%BC%9B">
		</outline>
		<outline text="(2)经双方当事人约定，以他种给付代替原定给付；" _mubu_text="(2)%E7%BB%8F%E5%8F%8C%E6%96%B9%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%EF%BC%8C%E4%BB%A5%E4%BB%96%E7%A7%8D%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E4%BB%A3%E6%9B%BF%E5%8E%9F%E5%AE%9A%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%EF%BC%9B">
		</outline>
		<outline text="(3)有双方当事人关于代物清偿的合意；" _mubu_text="(3)%E6%9C%89%E5%8F%8C%E6%96%B9%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E5%85%B3%E4%BA%8E%E4%BB%A3%E7%89%A9%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF%E7%9A%84%E5%90%88%E6%84%8F%EF%BC%9B">
		</outline>
		<outline text="(4)债权人或其他有履行受领权的人现实地受领给付。" _mubu_text="(4)%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E6%88%96%E5%85%B6%E4%BB%96%E6%9C%89%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E5%8F%97%E9%A2%86%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E4%BA%BA%E7%8E%B0%E5%AE%9E%E5%9C%B0%E5%8F%97%E9%A2%86%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="清偿抵充" _mubu_text="%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF%E6%8A%B5%E5%85%85">
		<outline text="清偿抵充的概念" _mubu_text="%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF%E6%8A%B5%E5%85%85%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="是指在债务人对于同一债权人负担数宗同种类的债务而清偿人提供的给付不足以清偿全部债务时，决定以该给付抵充何宗债务的规则。" _mubu_text="%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%9C%A8%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E5%AF%B9%E4%BA%8E%E5%90%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E8%B4%9F%E6%8B%85%E6%95%B0%E5%AE%97%E5%90%8C%E7%A7%8D%E7%B1%BB%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E8%80%8C%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF%E4%BA%BA%E6%8F%90%E4%BE%9B%E7%9A%84%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E4%B8%8D%E8%B6%B3%E4%BB%A5%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF%E5%85%A8%E9%83%A8%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E6%97%B6%EF%BC%8C%E5%86%B3%E5%AE%9A%E4%BB%A5%E8%AF%A5%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E6%8A%B5%E5%85%85%E4%BD%95%E5%AE%97%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E7%9A%84%E8%A7%84%E5%88%99%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="清偿扺充的顺序" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF%E6%89%BA%E5%85%85%E7%9A%84%E9%A1%BA%E5%BA%8F%3C/span%3E" _note="@口诀&nbsp;情敌顺序乐器稍重順避&nbsp;@题眼&nbsp;@简答题" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E6%83%85%E6%95%8C%E9%A1%BA%E5%BA%8F%E4%B9%90%E5%99%A8%E7%A8%8D%E9%87%8D%E9%A0%86%E9%81%BF&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E9%A2%98%E7%9C%BC%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E" _heading="1" _color="#dc2d1e">
		<outline text="1.债权人与债务人对清偿的债务或清偿抵充顺序有约定的依约定进行抵充。" _mubu_text="1.%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%8E%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E5%AF%B9%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E6%88%96%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF%E6%8A%B5%E5%85%85%E9%A1%BA%E5%BA%8F%E6%9C%89%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E4%BE%9D%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E8%BF%9B%E8%A1%8C%E6%8A%B5%E5%85%85%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="2.当事人之间没有约定的，应当优先抵充已到期的债务；" _mubu_text="2.%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%B9%8B%E9%97%B4%E6%B2%A1%E6%9C%89%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E4%BC%98%E5%85%88%E6%8A%B5%E5%85%85%E5%B7%B2%E5%88%B0%E6%9C%9F%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%EF%BC%9B">
		</outline>
		<outline text="3.几项债务均到期的，优先抵充对债权人缺乏担保或者担保数额最少的债务；" _mubu_text="3.%E5%87%A0%E9%A1%B9%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E5%9D%87%E5%88%B0%E6%9C%9F%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E4%BC%98%E5%85%88%E6%8A%B5%E5%85%85%E5%AF%B9%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E7%BC%BA%E4%B9%8F%E6%8B%85%E4%BF%9D%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E6%8B%85%E4%BF%9D%E6%95%B0%E9%A2%9D%E6%9C%80%E5%B0%91%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%EF%BC%9B">
		</outline>
		<outline text="4.担保数额相同的，优先抵充债务负担较重的债务；" _mubu_text="4.%E6%8B%85%E4%BF%9D%E6%95%B0%E9%A2%9D%E7%9B%B8%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E4%BC%98%E5%85%88%E6%8A%B5%E5%85%85%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E8%B4%9F%E6%8B%85%E8%BE%83%E9%87%8D%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%EF%BC%9B">
		</outline>
		<outline text="5.负担相同的，按照债务到期的先后顺序抵充；" _mubu_text="5.%E8%B4%9F%E6%8B%85%E7%9B%B8%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E6%8C%89%E7%85%A7%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E5%88%B0%E6%9C%9F%E7%9A%84%E5%85%88%E5%90%8E%E9%A1%BA%E5%BA%8F%E6%8A%B5%E5%85%85%EF%BC%9B">
		</outline>
		<outline text="6.到期时间相同的，按比例抵充。" _mubu_text="6.%E5%88%B0%E6%9C%9F%E6%97%B6%E9%97%B4%E7%9B%B8%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E6%8C%89%E6%AF%94%E4%BE%8B%E6%8A%B5%E5%85%85%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="债务人除主债务之外还应当支付利息和费用，当其给付不足以清偿全部债务，并且当事人没有约定时，应当按照下列顺序抵充：" _mubu_text="%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E9%99%A4%E4%B8%BB%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%B9%8B%E5%A4%96%E8%BF%98%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E6%94%AF%E4%BB%98%E5%88%A9%E6%81%AF%E5%92%8C%E8%B4%B9%E7%94%A8%EF%BC%8C%E5%BD%93%E5%85%B6%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E4%B8%8D%E8%B6%B3%E4%BB%A5%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF%E5%85%A8%E9%83%A8%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%EF%BC%8C%E5%B9%B6%E4%B8%94%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E6%B2%A1%E6%9C%89%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E6%97%B6%EF%BC%8C%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E6%8C%89%E7%85%A7%E4%B8%8B%E5%88%97%E9%A1%BA%E5%BA%8F%E6%8A%B5%E5%85%85%EF%BC%9A" _note="@考点" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E8%80%83%E7%82%B9%3C/span%3E">
		<outline text="(1)实现债权的有关费用；" _mubu_text="(1)%E5%AE%9E%E7%8E%B0%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E6%9C%89%E5%85%B3%E8%B4%B9%E7%94%A8%EF%BC%9B">
		</outline>
		<outline text="(2)利息；" _mubu_text="(2)%E5%88%A9%E6%81%AF%EF%BC%9B">
		</outline>
		<outline text="(3)主债务。" _mubu_text="(3)%E4%B8%BB%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="2.解除。" _mubu_text="2.%E8%A7%A3%E9%99%A4%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="解除是指因当事人一方行使解除权，或者经双方协议使债的关系归于消灭的行为。在我国，解除的对象限于合同。" _mubu_text="%E8%A7%A3%E9%99%A4%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%9B%A0%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E8%A1%8C%E4%BD%BF%E8%A7%A3%E9%99%A4%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%8C%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E7%BB%8F%E5%8F%8C%E6%96%B9%E5%8D%8F%E8%AE%AE%E4%BD%BF%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E5%BD%92%E4%BA%8E%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%E7%9A%84%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E3%80%82%E5%9C%A8%E6%88%91%E5%9B%BD%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E8%A7%A3%E9%99%A4%E7%9A%84%E5%AF%B9%E8%B1%A1%E9%99%90%E4%BA%8E%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="3.抵销。" _mubu_text="3.%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="抵销的概念" _mubu_text="%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="抵销是指互负债务的双方当事人将两项债务相互充抵，以使双方债务在对等数额内消灭的行为。" _mubu_text="%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E4%BA%92%E8%B4%9F%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E7%9A%84%E5%8F%8C%E6%96%B9%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E5%B0%86%E4%B8%A4%E9%A1%B9%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E7%9B%B8%E4%BA%92%E5%85%85%E6%8A%B5%EF%BC%8C%E4%BB%A5%E4%BD%BF%E5%8F%8C%E6%96%B9%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E5%9C%A8%E5%AF%B9%E7%AD%89%E6%95%B0%E9%A2%9D%E5%86%85%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%E7%9A%84%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="法定抵销" _mubu_text="%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80">
		<outline text="法定抵销的构成要件包括：" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E7%9A%84%E6%9E%84%E6%88%90%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6%E5%8C%85%E6%8B%AC%EF%BC%9A%3C/span%3E" _note="@简答题&nbsp;@题眼@口诀&nbsp;罚地虎劫镖部" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E9%A2%98%E7%9C%BC%3C/span%3E%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E7%BD%9A%E5%9C%B0%E8%99%8E%E5%8A%AB%E9%95%96%E9%83%A8" _heading="1" _color="#dc2d1e">
		<outline text="法定抵销的概念" _mubu_text="%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="法定抵销是指依法律规定以当事人一方的意思表示所作的抵销。" _mubu_text="%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E4%BE%9D%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E4%BB%A5%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E7%9A%84%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E6%89%80%E4%BD%9C%E7%9A%84%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="用作抵销的债权称为主动债权或自动债权，被抵销的债权称为被动债权。" _mubu_text="%E7%94%A8%E4%BD%9C%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E7%A7%B0%E4%B8%BA%E4%B8%BB%E5%8A%A8%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E6%88%96%E8%87%AA%E5%8A%A8%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%8C%E8%A2%AB%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E7%A7%B0%E4%B8%BA%E8%A2%AB%E5%8A%A8%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(1)须双方当事人互负债务、互享债权。" _mubu_text="(1)%E9%A1%BB%E5%8F%8C%E6%96%B9%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%BA%92%E8%B4%9F%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E3%80%81%E4%BA%92%E4%BA%AB%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="(2)须自动债权即提出抵销的债权已届清偿期。" _mubu_text="(2)%E9%A1%BB%E8%87%AA%E5%8A%A8%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E5%8D%B3%E6%8F%90%E5%87%BA%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%B7%B2%E5%B1%8A%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF%E6%9C%9F%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		<outline text="(3)须双方债务的标的物种类、品质相同。" _mubu_text="(3)%E9%A1%BB%E5%8F%8C%E6%96%B9%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E7%9A%84%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E7%89%A9%E7%A7%8D%E7%B1%BB%E3%80%81%E5%93%81%E8%B4%A8%E7%9B%B8%E5%90%8C%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="(4)须不存在按照合同性质或者依照法律规定不得抵销的情形。" _mubu_text="(4)%E9%A1%BB%E4%B8%8D%E5%AD%98%E5%9C%A8%E6%8C%89%E7%85%A7%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%80%A7%E8%B4%A8%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E4%BE%9D%E7%85%A7%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E4%B8%8D%E5%BE%97%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E7%9A%84%E6%83%85%E5%BD%A2%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="法定抵销的特征" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E7%9A%84%E7%89%B9%E5%BE%81%3C/span%3E" _note="@简答题&nbsp;@题眼@口诀&nbsp;法蒂整形童登苏​" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E9%A2%98%E7%9C%BC%3C/span%3E%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E6%B3%95%E8%92%82%E6%95%B4%E5%BD%A2%E7%AB%A5%E7%99%BB%E8%8B%8F%E2%80%8B" _heading="1" _color="#dc2d1e">
		<outline text="（1）抵销权属于形成权，享有抵销权的当事人只需通知对方即可发生抵销后果，无须对方同意。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E6%9D%83%E5%B1%9E%E4%BA%8E%E5%BD%A2%E6%88%90%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%8C%E4%BA%AB%E6%9C%89%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%AA%E9%9C%80%E9%80%9A%E7%9F%A5%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E5%8D%B3%E5%8F%AF%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E5%90%8E%E6%9E%9C%EF%BC%8C%E6%97%A0%E9%A1%BB%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E5%90%8C%E6%84%8F%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（2）当事人主张抵销的，应当通知对方，通知自到达对方时生效；但抵销不得附条件或者期限。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%BB%E5%BC%A0%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E9%80%9A%E7%9F%A5%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%EF%BC%8C%E9%80%9A%E7%9F%A5%E8%87%AA%E5%88%B0%E8%BE%BE%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E6%97%B6%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%EF%BC%9B%E4%BD%86%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E4%B8%8D%E5%BE%97%E9%99%84%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E6%9C%9F%E9%99%90%E3%80%82" _note="@考点" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E8%80%83%E7%82%B9%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（3）抵销使当事人双方的债权在对等数额内消灭，对于未抵销的债务部分，债务人仍然负有清偿义务。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E4%BD%BF%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%8C%E6%96%B9%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E5%9C%A8%E5%AF%B9%E7%AD%89%E6%95%B0%E9%A2%9D%E5%86%85%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%EF%BC%8C%E5%AF%B9%E4%BA%8E%E6%9C%AA%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E9%83%A8%E5%88%86%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E4%BB%8D%E7%84%B6%E8%B4%9F%E6%9C%89%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（4）抵销具有溯及力，溯及到抵销权成立之时。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%884%EF%BC%89%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E5%85%B7%E6%9C%89%E6%BA%AF%E5%8F%8A%E5%8A%9B%EF%BC%8C%E6%BA%AF%E5%8F%8A%E5%88%B0%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E6%9D%83%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E4%B9%8B%E6%97%B6%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="意思是即使抵销权成立时，当事人未行使，但是实际上抵销权已经生效了，在生效后的某一天抵销权人可以行使此权利并且其效力可以追溯到生效之日。" _mubu_text="%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E6%98%AF%E5%8D%B3%E4%BD%BF%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E6%9D%83%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E6%97%B6%EF%BC%8C%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E6%9C%AA%E8%A1%8C%E4%BD%BF%EF%BC%8C%E4%BD%86%E6%98%AF%E5%AE%9E%E9%99%85%E4%B8%8A%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E6%9D%83%E5%B7%B2%E7%BB%8F%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E4%BA%86%EF%BC%8C%E5%9C%A8%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E5%90%8E%E7%9A%84%E6%9F%90%E4%B8%80%E5%A4%A9%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E8%A1%8C%E4%BD%BF%E6%AD%A4%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E5%B9%B6%E4%B8%94%E5%85%B6%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E8%BF%BD%E6%BA%AF%E5%88%B0%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E4%B9%8B%E6%97%A5%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="合意抵销" _mubu_text="%E5%90%88%E6%84%8F%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80">
		<outline text="合意抵销的概念" _mubu_text="%E5%90%88%E6%84%8F%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="是指当事人协商一致时，双方的债权债务按对等数额消灭的抵销方式。" _mubu_text="%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E5%8D%8F%E5%95%86%E4%B8%80%E8%87%B4%E6%97%B6%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%8C%E6%96%B9%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E6%8C%89%E5%AF%B9%E7%AD%89%E6%95%B0%E9%A2%9D%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%E7%9A%84%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E6%96%B9%E5%BC%8F%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="合意抵销的特点" _mubu_text="%E5%90%88%E6%84%8F%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E7%9A%84%E7%89%B9%E7%82%B9">
		<outline text="（1）合意抵销是当事人意思自治的具体体现，法律不应禁止。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E5%90%88%E6%84%8F%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E6%98%AF%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E8%87%AA%E6%B2%BB%E7%9A%84%E5%85%B7%E4%BD%93%E4%BD%93%E7%8E%B0%EF%BC%8C%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E4%B8%8D%E5%BA%94%E7%A6%81%E6%AD%A2%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（2）合意抵销的发生条件、法律后果均须遵从当事人的约定，双方的抵销协议只需满足合同的成立及生效要件即可，不受法定抵销的限制。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%E5%90%88%E6%84%8F%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E7%9A%84%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E3%80%81%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E5%90%8E%E6%9E%9C%E5%9D%87%E9%A1%BB%E9%81%B5%E4%BB%8E%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%8C%E6%96%B9%E7%9A%84%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E5%8D%8F%E8%AE%AE%E5%8F%AA%E9%9C%80%E6%BB%A1%E8%B6%B3%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E5%8F%8A%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6%E5%8D%B3%E5%8F%AF%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%8D%E5%8F%97%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E7%9A%84%E9%99%90%E5%88%B6%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（3）除当事人有特别约定外，抵销合同没有溯及效力。 @考点" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%E9%99%A4%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E6%9C%89%E7%89%B9%E5%88%AB%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E5%A4%96%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%B2%A1%E6%9C%89%E6%BA%AF%E5%8F%8A%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E%20%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E8%80%83%E7%82%B9%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="4.提存" _mubu_text="4.%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98">
		<outline text="提存的概念" _mubu_text="%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="提存是指由于债权人的原因而无法向其交付履行标的物时，债务人将该标的物交付给提存机关以消灭债务的行为。" _mubu_text="%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E7%94%B1%E4%BA%8E%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%8E%9F%E5%9B%A0%E8%80%8C%E6%97%A0%E6%B3%95%E5%90%91%E5%85%B6%E4%BA%A4%E4%BB%98%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E7%89%A9%E6%97%B6%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E5%B0%86%E8%AF%A5%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E7%89%A9%E4%BA%A4%E4%BB%98%E7%BB%99%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E6%9C%BA%E5%85%B3%E4%BB%A5%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E7%9A%84%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="提存须具备的条件" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E9%A1%BB%E5%85%B7%E5%A4%87%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%3C/span%3E" _note="@简答题&nbsp;@口诀&nbsp;剔挑饮食城" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E5%89%94%E6%8C%91%E9%A5%AE%E9%A3%9F%E5%9F%8E" _heading="1" _color="#3da8f5">
		<outline text="提存的概念" _mubu_text="%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="提存是指由于债权人的原因而无法向其交付履行标的物时，债务人将该标的物交付给提存机关以消灭债务的行为。" _mubu_text="%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E7%94%B1%E4%BA%8E%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%8E%9F%E5%9B%A0%E8%80%8C%E6%97%A0%E6%B3%95%E5%90%91%E5%85%B6%E4%BA%A4%E4%BB%98%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E7%89%A9%E6%97%B6%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E5%B0%86%E8%AF%A5%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E7%89%A9%E4%BA%A4%E4%BB%98%E7%BB%99%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E6%9C%BA%E5%85%B3%E4%BB%A5%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E7%9A%84%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="（1）需有因债权人方面的原因，使债务人难以履行债务的客观情况发生。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E9%9C%80%E6%9C%89%E5%9B%A0%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E6%96%B9%E9%9D%A2%E7%9A%84%E5%8E%9F%E5%9B%A0%EF%BC%8C%E4%BD%BF%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E9%9A%BE%E4%BB%A5%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E7%9A%84%E5%AE%A2%E8%A7%82%E6%83%85%E5%86%B5%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="①债权人无正当理由拒绝受领" _mubu_text="%E2%91%A0%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E6%97%A0%E6%AD%A3%E5%BD%93%E7%90%86%E7%94%B1%E6%8B%92%E7%BB%9D%E5%8F%97%E9%A2%86">
		</outline>
		<outline text="②债权人下落不明" _mubu_text="%E2%91%A1%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%8B%E8%90%BD%E4%B8%8D%E6%98%8E">
		</outline>
		<outline text="③债权人死亡、未确定继承人，或者丧失行为能力未确定监护人。" _mubu_text="%E2%91%A2%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E6%AD%BB%E4%BA%A1%E3%80%81%E6%9C%AA%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%E7%BB%A7%E6%89%BF%E4%BA%BA%EF%BC%8C%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E4%B8%A7%E5%A4%B1%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E8%83%BD%E5%8A%9B%E6%9C%AA%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%E7%9B%91%E6%8A%A4%E4%BA%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="（2）须提存的标的物适宜提存。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%E9%A1%BB%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E7%9A%84%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E7%89%A9%E9%80%82%E5%AE%9C%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="如果标的物不适于提存或者提存费用过高，债务人依法可以拍卖或者变卖标的物，提存所得的价款。" _mubu_text="%E5%A6%82%E6%9E%9C%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E7%89%A9%E4%B8%8D%E9%80%82%E4%BA%8E%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E8%B4%B9%E7%94%A8%E8%BF%87%E9%AB%98%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E4%BE%9D%E6%B3%95%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E6%8B%8D%E5%8D%96%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%8F%98%E5%8D%96%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E7%89%A9%EF%BC%8C%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E6%89%80%E5%BE%97%E7%9A%84%E4%BB%B7%E6%AC%BE%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="（3）提存须经法定程序进行。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E9%A1%BB%E7%BB%8F%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E7%A8%8B%E5%BA%8F%E8%BF%9B%E8%A1%8C%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="提存的效力" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E7%9A%84%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%3C/span%3E" _note="@简答题&nbsp;@题眼&nbsp;@口诀&nbsp;体校钟飞先捅吾" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E9%A2%98%E7%9C%BC%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E4%BD%93%E6%A0%A1%E9%92%9F%E9%A3%9E%E5%85%88%E6%8D%85%E5%90%BE" _heading="1" _color="#dc2d1e">
		<outline text="（1）提存之日起，债务人与债权人之间的权利义务终止。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E4%B9%8B%E6%97%A5%E8%B5%B7%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%8E%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E4%B9%8B%E9%97%B4%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E7%BB%88%E6%AD%A2%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（2）标的物提存后，其所有权原则上转移给债权人，孳息归债权人所有，提存费用由债权人负担。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E7%89%A9%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E5%90%8E%EF%BC%8C%E5%85%B6%E6%89%80%E6%9C%89%E6%9D%83%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99%E4%B8%8A%E8%BD%AC%E7%A7%BB%E7%BB%99%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%EF%BC%8C%E5%AD%B3%E6%81%AF%E5%BD%92%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E6%89%80%E6%9C%89%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E8%B4%B9%E7%94%A8%E7%94%B1%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E8%B4%9F%E6%8B%85%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（3）提存期间提存物毁损灭失的风险亦由债权人承担。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E6%9C%9F%E9%97%B4%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E7%89%A9%E6%AF%81%E6%8D%9F%E7%81%AD%E5%A4%B1%E7%9A%84%E9%A3%8E%E9%99%A9%E4%BA%A6%E7%94%B1%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E6%89%BF%E6%8B%85%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（4）标的物提存后，债务人应当及时通知债权人或者债权人的继承人、监护人。若债务人无法通知，应由提存机关履行此义务。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%884%EF%BC%89%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E7%89%A9%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E5%90%8E%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E5%8F%8A%E6%97%B6%E9%80%9A%E7%9F%A5%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E7%BB%A7%E6%89%BF%E4%BA%BA%E3%80%81%E7%9B%91%E6%8A%A4%E4%BA%BA%E3%80%82%E8%8B%A5%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E6%97%A0%E6%B3%95%E9%80%9A%E7%9F%A5%EF%BC%8C%E5%BA%94%E7%94%B1%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E6%9C%BA%E5%85%B3%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%AD%A4%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（5）债权人领取提存物的权利，自提存之日起5年内不行使而消灭，提存物扣除提存费用后归国家所有。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%885%EF%BC%89%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E9%A2%86%E5%8F%96%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E7%89%A9%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%EF%BC%8C%E8%87%AA%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E4%B9%8B%E6%97%A5%E8%B5%B75%E5%B9%B4%E5%86%85%E4%B8%8D%E8%A1%8C%E4%BD%BF%E8%80%8C%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%EF%BC%8C%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E7%89%A9%E6%89%A3%E9%99%A4%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E8%B4%B9%E7%94%A8%E5%90%8E%E5%BD%92%E5%9B%BD%E5%AE%B6%E6%89%80%E6%9C%89%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="5.免除" _mubu_text="5.%E5%85%8D%E9%99%A4">
		<outline text="免除的概念" _mubu_text="%E5%85%8D%E9%99%A4%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="免除即债权人以消灭债为目的而向债务人作出的抛弃债权的行为。" _mubu_text="%E5%85%8D%E9%99%A4%E5%8D%B3%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E4%BB%A5%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%E5%80%BA%E4%B8%BA%E7%9B%AE%E7%9A%84%E8%80%8C%E5%90%91%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%8A%9B%E5%BC%83%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="免除的特点" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%85%8D%E9%99%A4%E7%9A%84%E7%89%B9%E7%82%B9%3C/span%3E" _note="@简答题&nbsp;@题眼&nbsp;@口诀&nbsp;摘棉不耽误飞车主" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E9%A2%98%E7%9C%BC%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E6%91%98%E6%A3%89%E4%B8%8D%E8%80%BD%E8%AF%AF%E9%A3%9E%E8%BD%A6%E4%B8%BB" _heading="1" _color="#dc2d1e">
		<outline text="免除的概念" _mubu_text="%E5%85%8D%E9%99%A4%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="免除即债权人以消灭债为目的而向债务人作出的抛弃债权的行为。" _mubu_text="%E5%85%8D%E9%99%A4%E5%8D%B3%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E4%BB%A5%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%E5%80%BA%E4%B8%BA%E7%9B%AE%E7%9A%84%E8%80%8C%E5%90%91%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%8A%9B%E5%BC%83%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="（1）免除的对象可以是部分债务，也可以是全部债务。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E5%85%8D%E9%99%A4%E7%9A%84%E5%AF%B9%E8%B1%A1%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E6%98%AF%E9%83%A8%E5%88%86%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%EF%BC%8C%E4%B9%9F%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E6%98%AF%E5%85%A8%E9%83%A8%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（2）免除为单方、无偿、非要式法律行为。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%E5%85%8D%E9%99%A4%E4%B8%BA%E5%8D%95%E6%96%B9%E3%80%81%E6%97%A0%E5%81%BF%E3%80%81%E9%9D%9E%E8%A6%81%E5%BC%8F%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（3）一经通知对方即发生效力，不得撤销。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%E4%B8%80%E7%BB%8F%E9%80%9A%E7%9F%A5%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E5%8D%B3%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%8D%E5%BE%97%E6%92%A4%E9%94%80%E3%80%82" _color="#dc2d1e">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（4）免除的效力在于债务全部免除时，主债务与从债务全部消灭；部分免除时，主债务与从债务部分消灭。但债权人仅免除从债务时，主债务并不消灭。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%884%EF%BC%89%E5%85%8D%E9%99%A4%E7%9A%84%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%E5%9C%A8%E4%BA%8E%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E5%85%A8%E9%83%A8%E5%85%8D%E9%99%A4%E6%97%B6%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%BB%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%B8%8E%E4%BB%8E%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E5%85%A8%E9%83%A8%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%EF%BC%9B%E9%83%A8%E5%88%86%E5%85%8D%E9%99%A4%E6%97%B6%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%BB%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%B8%8E%E4%BB%8E%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E9%83%A8%E5%88%86%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%E3%80%82%E4%BD%86%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E4%BB%85%E5%85%8D%E9%99%A4%E4%BB%8E%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E6%97%B6%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%BB%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E5%B9%B6%E4%B8%8D%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="6.混同" _mubu_text="6.%E6%B7%B7%E5%90%8C">
		<outline text="混同的概念" _mubu_text="%E6%B7%B7%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="混同是指债权人和债务人合为一人的事实。混同无须以任何人的意思表示为成立要件，故属于法律事实中的事件。" _mubu_text="%E6%B7%B7%E5%90%8C%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E5%92%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E5%90%88%E4%B8%BA%E4%B8%80%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E4%BA%8B%E5%AE%9E%E3%80%82%E6%B7%B7%E5%90%8C%E6%97%A0%E9%A1%BB%E4%BB%A5%E4%BB%BB%E4%BD%95%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E4%B8%BA%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6%EF%BC%8C%E6%95%85%E5%B1%9E%E4%BA%8E%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E4%BA%8B%E5%AE%9E%E4%B8%AD%E7%9A%84%E4%BA%8B%E4%BB%B6%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="混同的成立原因主要有：" _mubu_text="%E6%B7%B7%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E5%8E%9F%E5%9B%A0%E4%B8%BB%E8%A6%81%E6%9C%89%EF%BC%9A">
		<outline text="(1)概括承受。" _mubu_text="(1)%E6%A6%82%E6%8B%AC%E6%89%BF%E5%8F%97%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="①企业法人和其他组织的概括承受" _mubu_text="%E2%91%A0%E4%BC%81%E4%B8%9A%E6%B3%95%E4%BA%BA%E5%92%8C%E5%85%B6%E4%BB%96%E7%BB%84%E7%BB%87%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E6%8B%AC%E6%89%BF%E5%8F%97">
		<outline text="如相互有债权债务关系的企业合并为一个企业，债权债务即因同归于一个企业而消灭。" _mubu_text="%E5%A6%82%E7%9B%B8%E4%BA%92%E6%9C%89%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E7%9A%84%E4%BC%81%E4%B8%9A%E5%90%88%E5%B9%B6%E4%B8%BA%E4%B8%80%E4%B8%AA%E4%BC%81%E4%B8%9A%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E5%8D%B3%E5%9B%A0%E5%90%8C%E5%BD%92%E4%BA%8E%E4%B8%80%E4%B8%AA%E4%BC%81%E4%B8%9A%E8%80%8C%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="②个人的概括承受" _mubu_text="%E2%91%A1%E4%B8%AA%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E6%8B%AC%E6%89%BF%E5%8F%97">
		<outline text="如债权人继承债务人的遗产或者债务人继承债权人的遗产，债权债务因同归继承人而消灭。" _mubu_text="%E5%A6%82%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E7%BB%A7%E6%89%BF%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E9%81%97%E4%BA%A7%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E7%BB%A7%E6%89%BF%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E9%81%97%E4%BA%A7%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E5%9B%A0%E5%90%8C%E5%BD%92%E7%BB%A7%E6%89%BF%E4%BA%BA%E8%80%8C%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(2)特定承受。" _mubu_text="(2)%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E6%89%BF%E5%8F%97%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="这是指在债务人受让债权人的债权，债权人承受债务人的债务的场合，债权债务亦因混同而消灭。" _mubu_text="%E8%BF%99%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%9C%A8%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%97%E8%AE%A9%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E6%89%BF%E5%8F%97%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E7%9A%84%E5%9C%BA%E5%90%88%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%A6%E5%9B%A0%E6%B7%B7%E5%90%8C%E8%80%8C%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="混同的效力在于绝对地消灭合同关系及因合同所生的从债权和从债务，但涉及第三人利益的除外。" _mubu_text="%E6%B7%B7%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%E5%9C%A8%E4%BA%8E%E7%BB%9D%E5%AF%B9%E5%9C%B0%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E5%8F%8A%E5%9B%A0%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%89%80%E7%94%9F%E7%9A%84%E4%BB%8E%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E5%92%8C%E4%BB%8E%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E4%BD%86%E6%B6%89%E5%8F%8A%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E7%9A%84%E9%99%A4%E5%A4%96%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="除上述六种原因外，因为法律规定或者当事人约定的其他情形，如当事人死亡、解除条件成就、终期届至等也可以导致合同终止。" _mubu_text="%E9%99%A4%E4%B8%8A%E8%BF%B0%E5%85%AD%E7%A7%8D%E5%8E%9F%E5%9B%A0%E5%A4%96%EF%BC%8C%E5%9B%A0%E4%B8%BA%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E5%85%B6%E4%BB%96%E6%83%85%E5%BD%A2%EF%BC%8C%E5%A6%82%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E6%AD%BB%E4%BA%A1%E3%80%81%E8%A7%A3%E9%99%A4%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E6%88%90%E5%B0%B1%E3%80%81%E7%BB%88%E6%9C%9F%E5%B1%8A%E8%87%B3%E7%AD%89%E4%B9%9F%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E5%AF%BC%E8%87%B4%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%BB%88%E6%AD%A2%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="322.简述代物清偿的要件" _mubu_text="322.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E4%BB%A3%E7%89%A9%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF%E7%9A%84%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6">
		<outline text="代物清偿须具备以下要件：" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E4%BB%A3%E7%89%A9%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF%E9%A1%BB%E5%85%B7%E5%A4%87%E4%BB%A5%E4%B8%8B%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6%EF%BC%9A%3C/span%3E" _note="@简答题&nbsp;@题眼&nbsp;@口诀&nbsp;代偿村月河守" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E9%A2%98%E7%9C%BC%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E4%BB%A3%E5%81%BF%E6%9D%91%E6%9C%88%E6%B2%B3%E5%AE%88" _heading="1" _color="#dc2d1e">
		<outline text="代物清偿的概念" _mubu_text="%E4%BB%A3%E7%89%A9%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="是指在债的履行过程中，债权人受领他种给付以代替原定给付而使债的关系消灭。" _mubu_text="%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%9C%A8%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E8%BF%87%E7%A8%8B%E4%B8%AD%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%97%E9%A2%86%E4%BB%96%E7%A7%8D%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E4%BB%A5%E4%BB%A3%E6%9B%BF%E5%8E%9F%E5%AE%9A%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E8%80%8C%E4%BD%BF%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(1)有原债务存在；" _mubu_text="(1)%E6%9C%89%E5%8E%9F%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%AD%98%3C/span%3E%E5%9C%A8%EF%BC%9B">
		</outline>
		<outline text="(2)经双方当事人约定，以他种给付代替原定给付；" _mubu_text="(2)%E7%BB%8F%E5%8F%8C%E6%96%B9%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%EF%BC%8C%E4%BB%A5%E4%BB%96%E7%A7%8D%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E4%BB%A3%E6%9B%BF%E5%8E%9F%E5%AE%9A%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%EF%BC%9B">
		</outline>

		</outline>

		<outline text="清偿抵充的概念" _mubu_text="%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF%E6%8A%B5%E5%85%85%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="是指在债务人对于同一债权人负担数宗同种类的债务而清偿人提供的给付不足以清偿全部债务时，决定以该给付抵充何宗债务的规则。" _mubu_text="%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%9C%A8%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E5%AF%B9%E4%BA%8E%E5%90%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E8%B4%9F%E6%8B%85%E6%95%B0%E5%AE%97%E5%90%8C%E7%A7%8D%E7%B1%BB%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E8%80%8C%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF%E4%BA%BA%E6%8F%90%E4%BE%9B%E7%9A%84%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E4%B8%8D%E8%B6%B3%E4%BB%A5%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF%E5%85%A8%E9%83%A8%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E6%97%B6%EF%BC%8C%E5%86%B3%E5%AE%9A%E4%BB%A5%E8%AF%A5%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E6%8A%B5%E5%85%85%E4%BD%95%E5%AE%97%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E7%9A%84%E8%A7%84%E5%88%99%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="1.债权人与债务人对清偿的债务或清偿抵充顺序有约定的依约定进行抵充。" _mubu_text="1.%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%8E%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E5%AF%B9%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E6%88%96%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF%E6%8A%B5%E5%85%85%E9%A1%BA%E5%BA%8F%E6%9C%89%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E4%BE%9D%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E8%BF%9B%E8%A1%8C%E6%8A%B5%E5%85%85%E3%80%82">
		</outline>

		</outline>

		</outline>

		</outline>
		<outline text="6.到期时间相同的，按比例抵充。" _mubu_text="6.%E5%88%B0%E6%9C%9F%E6%97%B6%E9%97%B4%E7%9B%B8%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E6%8C%89%E6%AF%94%E4%BE%8B%E6%8A%B5%E5%85%85%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>

		<outline text="(1)实现债权的有关费用；" _mubu_text="(1)%E5%AE%9E%E7%8E%B0%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E6%9C%89%E5%85%B3%E8%B4%B9%E7%94%A8%EF%BC%9B">

		<outline text="324.简述法定抵消的构成要件" _mubu_text="324.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E6%8A%B5%E6%B6%88%E7%9A%84%E6%9E%84%E6%88%90%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6">
		<outline text="法定抵销的构成要件包括：" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E7%9A%84%E6%9E%84%E6%88%90%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6%E5%8C%85%E6%8B%AC%EF%BC%9A%3C/span%3E" _note="@简答题&nbsp;@题眼&nbsp;@口诀&nbsp;罚地虎劫镖部" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E9%A2%98%E7%9C%BC%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E7%BD%9A%E5%9C%B0%E8%99%8E%E5%8A%AB%E9%95%96%E9%83%A8" _heading="1" _color="#dc2d1e">
		<outline text="法定抵销的概念" _mubu_text="%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="法定抵销是指依法律规定以当事人一方的意思表示所作的抵销。" _mubu_text="%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E4%BE%9D%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E4%BB%A5%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E7%9A%84%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E6%89%80%E4%BD%9C%E7%9A%84%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="用作抵销的债权称为主动债权或自动债权，被抵销的债权称为被动债权。" _mubu_text="%E7%94%A8%E4%BD%9C%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E7%A7%B0%E4%B8%BA%E4%B8%BB%E5%8A%A8%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E6%88%96%E8%87%AA%E5%8A%A8%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%8C%E8%A2%AB%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E7%A7%B0%E4%B8%BA%E8%A2%AB%E5%8A%A8%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="(1)须双方当事人互负债务、互享债权。" _mubu_text="(1)%E9%A1%BB%E5%8F%8C%E6%96%B9%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%BA%92%E8%B4%9F%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E3%80%81%E4%BA%92%E4%BA%AB%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E3%80%82">
		</outline>

		</outline>
		<outline text="(3)须双方债务的标的物种类、品质相同。" _mubu_text="(3)%E9%A1%BB%E5%8F%8C%E6%96%B9%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E7%9A%84%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E7%89%A9%E7%A7%8D%E7%B1%BB%E3%80%81%E5%93%81%E8%B4%A8%E7%9B%B8%E5%90%8C%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="(4)须不存在按照合同性质或者依照法律规定不得抵销的情形。" _mubu_text="(4)%E9%A1%BB%E4%B8%8D%E5%AD%98%E5%9C%A8%E6%8C%89%E7%85%A7%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%80%A7%E8%B4%A8%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E4%BE%9D%E7%85%A7%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E4%B8%8D%E5%BE%97%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E7%9A%84%E6%83%85%E5%BD%A2%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="法定抵销的特征" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E7%9A%84%E7%89%B9%E5%BE%81%3C/span%3E" _note="@简答题&nbsp;@题眼&nbsp;@口诀&nbsp;法蒂整形童登苏​" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E9%A2%98%E7%9C%BC%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E6%B3%95%E8%92%82%E6%95%B4%E5%BD%A2%E7%AB%A5%E7%99%BB%E8%8B%8F%E2%80%8B" _heading="1" _color="#dc2d1e">
		<outline text="（1）抵销权属于形成权，享有抵销权的当事人只需通知对方即可发生抵销后果，无须对方同意。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E6%9D%83%E5%B1%9E%E4%BA%8E%E5%BD%A2%E6%88%90%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%8C%E4%BA%AB%E6%9C%89%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%AA%E9%9C%80%E9%80%9A%E7%9F%A5%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E5%8D%B3%E5%8F%AF%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E5%90%8E%E6%9E%9C%EF%BC%8C%E6%97%A0%E9%A1%BB%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E5%90%8C%E6%84%8F%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（2）当事人主张抵销的，应当通知对方，通知自到达对方时生效；但抵销不得附条件或者期限。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%BB%E5%BC%A0%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E9%80%9A%E7%9F%A5%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%EF%BC%8C%E9%80%9A%E7%9F%A5%E8%87%AA%E5%88%B0%E8%BE%BE%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E6%97%B6%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%EF%BC%9B%E4%BD%86%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E4%B8%8D%E5%BE%97%E9%99%84%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E6%9C%9F%E9%99%90%E3%80%82" _note="@考点" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E8%80%83%E7%82%B9%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（3）抵销使当事人双方的债权在对等数额内消灭，对于未抵销的债务部分，债务人仍然负有清偿义务。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E4%BD%BF%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%8C%E6%96%B9%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E5%9C%A8%E5%AF%B9%E7%AD%89%E6%95%B0%E9%A2%9D%E5%86%85%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%EF%BC%8C%E5%AF%B9%E4%BA%8E%E6%9C%AA%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E9%83%A8%E5%88%86%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E4%BB%8D%E7%84%B6%E8%B4%9F%E6%9C%89%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（4）抵销具有溯及力，溯及到抵销权成立之时。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%884%EF%BC%89%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E5%85%B7%E6%9C%89%E6%BA%AF%E5%8F%8A%E5%8A%9B%EF%BC%8C%E6%BA%AF%E5%8F%8A%E5%88%B0%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E6%9D%83%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E4%B9%8B%E6%97%B6%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="意思是即使抵销权成立时，当事人未行使，但是实际上抵销权已经生效了，在生效后的某一天抵销权人可以行使此权利并且其效力可以追溯到生效之日。" _mubu_text="%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E6%98%AF%E5%8D%B3%E4%BD%BF%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E6%9D%83%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E6%97%B6%EF%BC%8C%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E6%9C%AA%E8%A1%8C%E4%BD%BF%EF%BC%8C%E4%BD%86%E6%98%AF%E5%AE%9E%E9%99%85%E4%B8%8A%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E6%9D%83%E5%B7%B2%E7%BB%8F%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E4%BA%86%EF%BC%8C%E5%9C%A8%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E5%90%8E%E7%9A%84%E6%9F%90%E4%B8%80%E5%A4%A9%E6%8A%B5%E9%94%80%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E8%A1%8C%E4%BD%BF%E6%AD%A4%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E5%B9%B6%E4%B8%94%E5%85%B6%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E8%BF%BD%E6%BA%AF%E5%88%B0%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E4%B9%8B%E6%97%A5%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="325.简述提存需要具备的条件、效力" _mubu_text="325.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E9%9C%80%E8%A6%81%E5%85%B7%E5%A4%87%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E3%80%81%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B">
		<outline text="提存须具备的条件" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E9%A1%BB%E5%85%B7%E5%A4%87%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%3C/span%3E" _note="@简答题&nbsp;@口诀&nbsp;剔挑饮食城" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E5%89%94%E6%8C%91%E9%A5%AE%E9%A3%9F%E5%9F%8E" _heading="1" _color="#3da8f5">
		<outline text="提存的概念" _mubu_text="%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="提存是指由于债权人的原因而无法向其交付履行标的物时，债务人将该标的物交付给提存机关以消灭债务的行为。" _mubu_text="%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E7%94%B1%E4%BA%8E%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%8E%9F%E5%9B%A0%E8%80%8C%E6%97%A0%E6%B3%95%E5%90%91%E5%85%B6%E4%BA%A4%E4%BB%98%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E7%89%A9%E6%97%B6%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E5%B0%86%E8%AF%A5%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E7%89%A9%E4%BA%A4%E4%BB%98%E7%BB%99%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E6%9C%BA%E5%85%B3%E4%BB%A5%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E7%9A%84%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="（1）需有因债权人方面的原因，使债务人难以履行债务的客观情况发生。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E9%9C%80%E6%9C%89%E5%9B%A0%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E6%96%B9%E9%9D%A2%E7%9A%84%E5%8E%9F%E5%9B%A0%EF%BC%8C%E4%BD%BF%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E9%9A%BE%E4%BB%A5%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E7%9A%84%E5%AE%A2%E8%A7%82%E6%83%85%E5%86%B5%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="①债权人无正当理由拒绝受领" _mubu_text="%E2%91%A0%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E6%97%A0%E6%AD%A3%E5%BD%93%E7%90%86%E7%94%B1%E6%8B%92%E7%BB%9D%E5%8F%97%E9%A2%86">
		</outline>
		<outline text="②债权人下落不明" _mubu_text="%E2%91%A1%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%8B%E8%90%BD%E4%B8%8D%E6%98%8E">
		</outline>
		<outline text="③债权人死亡、未确定继承人，或者丧失行为能力未确定监护人。" _mubu_text="%E2%91%A2%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E6%AD%BB%E4%BA%A1%E3%80%81%E6%9C%AA%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%E7%BB%A7%E6%89%BF%E4%BA%BA%EF%BC%8C%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E4%B8%A7%E5%A4%B1%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E8%83%BD%E5%8A%9B%E6%9C%AA%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%E7%9B%91%E6%8A%A4%E4%BA%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="（2）须提存的标的物适宜提存。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%E9%A1%BB%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E7%9A%84%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E7%89%A9%E9%80%82%E5%AE%9C%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="如果标的物不适于提存或者提存费用过高，债务人依法可以拍卖或者变卖标的物，提存所得的价款。" _mubu_text="%E5%A6%82%E6%9E%9C%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E7%89%A9%E4%B8%8D%E9%80%82%E4%BA%8E%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E8%B4%B9%E7%94%A8%E8%BF%87%E9%AB%98%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E4%BE%9D%E6%B3%95%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E6%8B%8D%E5%8D%96%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%8F%98%E5%8D%96%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E7%89%A9%EF%BC%8C%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E6%89%80%E5%BE%97%E7%9A%84%E4%BB%B7%E6%AC%BE%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="（3）提存须经法定程序进行。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E9%A1%BB%E7%BB%8F%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E7%A8%8B%E5%BA%8F%E8%BF%9B%E8%A1%8C%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="提存的效力" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E7%9A%84%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%3C/span%3E" _note="@简答题&nbsp;@题眼&nbsp;@口诀&nbsp;体校钟飞先捅吾" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E9%A2%98%E7%9C%BC%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E4%BD%93%E6%A0%A1%E9%92%9F%E9%A3%9E%E5%85%88%E6%8D%85%E5%90%BE" _heading="1" _color="#dc2d1e">
		<outline text="（1）提存之日起，债务人与债权人之间的权利义务终止。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E4%B9%8B%E6%97%A5%E8%B5%B7%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%8E%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E4%B9%8B%E9%97%B4%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E7%BB%88%E6%AD%A2%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（2）标的物提存后，其所有权原则上转移给债权人，孳息归债权人所有，提存费用由债权人负担。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E7%89%A9%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E5%90%8E%EF%BC%8C%E5%85%B6%E6%89%80%E6%9C%89%E6%9D%83%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99%E4%B8%8A%E8%BD%AC%E7%A7%BB%E7%BB%99%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%EF%BC%8C%E5%AD%B3%E6%81%AF%E5%BD%92%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E6%89%80%E6%9C%89%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E8%B4%B9%E7%94%A8%E7%94%B1%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E8%B4%9F%E6%8B%85%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（3）提存期间提存物毁损灭失的风险亦由债权人承担。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E6%9C%9F%E9%97%B4%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E7%89%A9%E6%AF%81%E6%8D%9F%E7%81%AD%E5%A4%B1%E7%9A%84%E9%A3%8E%E9%99%A9%E4%BA%A6%E7%94%B1%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E6%89%BF%E6%8B%85%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（4）标的物提存后，债务人应当及时通知债权人或者债权人的继承人、监护人。若债务人无法通知，应由提存机关履行此义务。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%884%EF%BC%89%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E7%89%A9%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E5%90%8E%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E5%8F%8A%E6%97%B6%E9%80%9A%E7%9F%A5%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E7%BB%A7%E6%89%BF%E4%BA%BA%E3%80%81%E7%9B%91%E6%8A%A4%E4%BA%BA%E3%80%82%E8%8B%A5%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E6%97%A0%E6%B3%95%E9%80%9A%E7%9F%A5%EF%BC%8C%E5%BA%94%E7%94%B1%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E6%9C%BA%E5%85%B3%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%AD%A4%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（5）债权人领取提存物的权利，自提存之日起5年内不行使而消灭，提存物扣除提存费用后归国家所有。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%885%EF%BC%89%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E9%A2%86%E5%8F%96%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E7%89%A9%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%EF%BC%8C%E8%87%AA%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E4%B9%8B%E6%97%A5%E8%B5%B75%E5%B9%B4%E5%86%85%E4%B8%8D%E8%A1%8C%E4%BD%BF%E8%80%8C%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%EF%BC%8C%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E7%89%A9%E6%89%A3%E9%99%A4%E6%8F%90%E5%AD%98%E8%B4%B9%E7%94%A8%E5%90%8E%E5%BD%92%E5%9B%BD%E5%AE%B6%E6%89%80%E6%9C%89%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="326.简述混同成立的原因" _mubu_text="326.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E6%B7%B7%E5%90%8C%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E7%9A%84%E5%8E%9F%E5%9B%A0">
		<outline text="混同的概念" _mubu_text="%E6%B7%B7%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="混同是指债权人和债务人合为一人的事实。混同无须以任何人的意思表示为成立要件，故属于法律事实中的事件。" _mubu_text="%E6%B7%B7%E5%90%8C%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E5%92%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E5%90%88%E4%B8%BA%E4%B8%80%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E4%BA%8B%E5%AE%9E%E3%80%82%E6%B7%B7%E5%90%8C%E6%97%A0%E9%A1%BB%E4%BB%A5%E4%BB%BB%E4%BD%95%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E4%B8%BA%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6%EF%BC%8C%E6%95%85%E5%B1%9E%E4%BA%8E%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E4%BA%8B%E5%AE%9E%E4%B8%AD%E7%9A%84%E4%BA%8B%E4%BB%B6%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="混同的成立原因主要有：" _mubu_text="%E6%B7%B7%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E5%8E%9F%E5%9B%A0%E4%B8%BB%E8%A6%81%E6%9C%89%EF%BC%9A">
		<outline text="(1)概括承受。" _mubu_text="(1)%E6%A6%82%E6%8B%AC%E6%89%BF%E5%8F%97%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="①企业法人和其他组织的概括承受" _mubu_text="%E2%91%A0%E4%BC%81%E4%B8%9A%E6%B3%95%E4%BA%BA%E5%92%8C%E5%85%B6%E4%BB%96%E7%BB%84%E7%BB%87%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E6%8B%AC%E6%89%BF%E5%8F%97">
		<outline text="如相互有债权债务关系的企业合并为一个企业，债权债务即因同归于一个企业而消灭。" _mubu_text="%E5%A6%82%E7%9B%B8%E4%BA%92%E6%9C%89%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E7%9A%84%E4%BC%81%E4%B8%9A%E5%90%88%E5%B9%B6%E4%B8%BA%E4%B8%80%E4%B8%AA%E4%BC%81%E4%B8%9A%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E5%8D%B3%E5%9B%A0%E5%90%8C%E5%BD%92%E4%BA%8E%E4%B8%80%E4%B8%AA%E4%BC%81%E4%B8%9A%E8%80%8C%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="②个人的概括承受" _mubu_text="%E2%91%A1%E4%B8%AA%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E6%8B%AC%E6%89%BF%E5%8F%97">
		<outline text="如债权人继承债务人的遗产或者债务人继承债权人的遗产，债权债务因同归继承人而消灭。" _mubu_text="%E5%A6%82%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E7%BB%A7%E6%89%BF%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E9%81%97%E4%BA%A7%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E7%BB%A7%E6%89%BF%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E9%81%97%E4%BA%A7%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E5%9B%A0%E5%90%8C%E5%BD%92%E7%BB%A7%E6%89%BF%E4%BA%BA%E8%80%8C%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(2)特定承受。" _mubu_text="(2)%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E6%89%BF%E5%8F%97%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="这是指在债务人受让债权人的债权，债权人承受债务人的债务的场合，债权债务亦因混同而消灭。" _mubu_text="%E8%BF%99%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%9C%A8%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%97%E8%AE%A9%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E6%89%BF%E5%8F%97%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E7%9A%84%E5%9C%BA%E5%90%88%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%A6%E5%9B%A0%E6%B7%B7%E5%90%8C%E8%80%8C%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="混同的效力在于绝对地消灭合同关系及因合同所生的从债权和从债务，但涉及第三人利益的除外。" _mubu_text="%E6%B7%B7%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%E5%9C%A8%E4%BA%8E%E7%BB%9D%E5%AF%B9%E5%9C%B0%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E5%8F%8A%E5%9B%A0%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%89%80%E7%94%9F%E7%9A%84%E4%BB%8E%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E5%92%8C%E4%BB%8E%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E4%BD%86%E6%B6%89%E5%8F%8A%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E7%9A%84%E9%99%A4%E5%A4%96%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="327.简述不当得利（概念，构成要件，效力）" _mubu_text="327.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E4%B8%8D%E5%BD%93%E5%BE%97%E5%88%A9%EF%BC%88%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5%EF%BC%8C%E6%9E%84%E6%88%90%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6%EF%BC%8C%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%EF%BC%89">
		<outline text="不当得利之债的构成要件" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E4%B8%8D%E5%BD%93%E5%BE%97%E5%88%A9%E4%B9%8B%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%9E%84%E6%88%90%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6%3C/span%3E" _note="@口诀&nbsp;不利要件一利一损因果无惧@简答题&nbsp;@题眼" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E4%B8%8D%E5%88%A9%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6%E4%B8%80%E5%88%A9%E4%B8%80%E6%8D%9F%E5%9B%A0%E6%9E%9C%E6%97%A0%E6%83%A7%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E9%A2%98%E7%9C%BC%3C/span%3E" _heading="1" _color="#dc2d1e">
		<outline text="不当得利的概念" _mubu_text="%E4%B8%8D%E5%BD%93%E5%BE%97%E5%88%A9%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="不当得利，是指一方没有合法根据或事后丧失合法根据取得利益而使另一方财产受损的事实。" _mubu_text="%E4%B8%8D%E5%BD%93%E5%BE%97%E5%88%A9%EF%BC%8C%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E6%B2%A1%E6%9C%89%E5%90%88%E6%B3%95%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE%E6%88%96%E4%BA%8B%E5%90%8E%E4%B8%A7%E5%A4%B1%E5%90%88%E6%B3%95%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE%E5%8F%96%E5%BE%97%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E8%80%8C%E4%BD%BF%E5%8F%A6%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E8%B4%A2%E4%BA%A7%E5%8F%97%E6%8D%9F%E7%9A%84%E4%BA%8B%E5%AE%9E%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="（1）一方获得利益" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E8%8E%B7%E5%BE%97%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A">
		<outline text="一方获得利益，是指财产的增加。财产的增加，包括积极增加与消极增加两种情况。" _mubu_text="%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E8%8E%B7%E5%BE%97%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%EF%BC%8C%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E8%B4%A2%E4%BA%A7%E7%9A%84%E5%A2%9E%E5%8A%A0%E3%80%82%E8%B4%A2%E4%BA%A7%E7%9A%84%E5%A2%9E%E5%8A%A0%EF%BC%8C%E5%8C%85%E6%8B%AC%E7%A7%AF%E6%9E%81%E5%A2%9E%E5%8A%A0%E4%B8%8E%E6%B6%88%E6%9E%81%E5%A2%9E%E5%8A%A0%E4%B8%A4%E7%A7%8D%E6%83%85%E5%86%B5%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="①财产的积极增加" _mubu_text="%E2%91%A0%E8%B4%A2%E4%BA%A7%E7%9A%84%E7%A7%AF%E6%9E%81%E5%A2%9E%E5%8A%A0">
		<outline text="是指财产或权利范围的增加或扩大，如取得所有权。" _mubu_text="%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E8%B4%A2%E4%BA%A7%E6%88%96%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E8%8C%83%E5%9B%B4%E7%9A%84%E5%A2%9E%E5%8A%A0%E6%88%96%E6%89%A9%E5%A4%A7%EF%BC%8C%E5%A6%82%E5%8F%96%E5%BE%97%E6%89%80%E6%9C%89%E6%9D%83%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="②财产的消极增加" _mubu_text="%E2%91%A1%E8%B4%A2%E4%BA%A7%E7%9A%84%E6%B6%88%E6%9E%81%E5%A2%9E%E5%8A%A0">
		<outline text="是指财产本应减少，却因一定事实而未减少，如没有支付出本应由自己支付的费用，未承担本应承担的债务。" _mubu_text="%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E8%B4%A2%E4%BA%A7%E6%9C%AC%E5%BA%94%E5%87%8F%E5%B0%91%EF%BC%8C%E5%8D%B4%E5%9B%A0%E4%B8%80%E5%AE%9A%E4%BA%8B%E5%AE%9E%E8%80%8C%E6%9C%AA%E5%87%8F%E5%B0%91%EF%BC%8C%E5%A6%82%E6%B2%A1%E6%9C%89%E6%94%AF%E4%BB%98%E5%87%BA%E6%9C%AC%E5%BA%94%E7%94%B1%E8%87%AA%E5%B7%B1%E6%94%AF%E4%BB%98%E7%9A%84%E8%B4%B9%E7%94%A8%EF%BC%8C%E6%9C%AA%E6%89%BF%E6%8B%85%E6%9C%AC%E5%BA%94%E6%89%BF%E6%8B%85%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="（2）另一方受有损失" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%E5%8F%A6%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E5%8F%97%E6%9C%89%E6%8D%9F%E5%A4%B1">
		<outline text="①现有财产的减少" _mubu_text="%E2%91%A0%E7%8E%B0%E6%9C%89%E8%B4%A2%E4%BA%A7%E7%9A%84%E5%87%8F%E5%B0%91">
		</outline>
		<outline text="②财产本应增加而未增加" _mubu_text="%E2%91%A1%E8%B4%A2%E4%BA%A7%E6%9C%AC%E5%BA%94%E5%A2%9E%E5%8A%A0%E8%80%8C%E6%9C%AA%E5%A2%9E%E5%8A%A0">
		<outline text="财产本应增加而未增加即应得利益的损失。" _mubu_text="%E8%B4%A2%E4%BA%A7%E6%9C%AC%E5%BA%94%E5%A2%9E%E5%8A%A0%E8%80%8C%E6%9C%AA%E5%A2%9E%E5%8A%A0%E5%8D%B3%E5%BA%94%E5%BE%97%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E7%9A%84%E6%8D%9F%E5%A4%B1%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="此处的应得利益是指在正常情形下可以得到的利益，而不是指必然得到的利益，如无合法根据耕种他人土地，所有人丧失了对该土地的收益属于应得利益，尽管该利益并非所有人必然得到的。" _mubu_text="%E6%AD%A4%E5%A4%84%E7%9A%84%E5%BA%94%E5%BE%97%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%9C%A8%E6%AD%A3%E5%B8%B8%E6%83%85%E5%BD%A2%E4%B8%8B%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E5%BE%97%E5%88%B0%E7%9A%84%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%EF%BC%8C%E8%80%8C%E4%B8%8D%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%BF%85%E7%84%B6%E5%BE%97%E5%88%B0%E7%9A%84%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%EF%BC%8C%3C/span%3E%E5%A6%82%E6%97%A0%E5%90%88%E6%B3%95%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE%E8%80%95%E7%A7%8D%E4%BB%96%E4%BA%BA%E5%9C%9F%E5%9C%B0%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%EF%BC%8C%E6%89%80%E6%9C%89%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%A7%E5%A4%B1%E4%BA%86%E5%AF%B9%E8%AF%A5%E5%9C%9F%E5%9C%B0%E7%9A%84%E6%94%B6%E7%9B%8A%E5%B1%9E%E4%BA%8E%E5%BA%94%E5%BE%97%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%EF%BC%8C%E5%B0%BD%E7%AE%A1%E8%AF%A5%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E5%B9%B6%E9%9D%9E%E6%89%80%E6%9C%89%E4%BA%BA%E5%BF%85%E7%84%B6%E5%BE%97%E5%88%B0%E7%9A%84%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E" _note="@考点" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E8%80%83%E7%82%B9%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="（3）一方获益和另一方受损之间有因果关系" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E8%8E%B7%E7%9B%8A%E5%92%8C%E5%8F%A6%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E5%8F%97%E6%8D%9F%E4%B9%8B%E9%97%B4%E6%9C%89%E5%9B%A0%E6%9E%9C%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB">
		<outline text="此处的因果关系表现为，另一方的损失是因一方受益造成的，而一方受益是另一方受损的原因。" _mubu_text="%E6%AD%A4%E5%A4%84%E7%9A%84%E5%9B%A0%E6%9E%9C%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E8%A1%A8%E7%8E%B0%E4%B8%BA%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%A6%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E7%9A%84%E6%8D%9F%E5%A4%B1%E6%98%AF%E5%9B%A0%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E5%8F%97%E7%9B%8A%E9%80%A0%E6%88%90%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E8%80%8C%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E5%8F%97%E7%9B%8A%E6%98%AF%E5%8F%A6%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E5%8F%97%E6%8D%9F%E7%9A%84%E5%8E%9F%E5%9B%A0%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="（4）获益没有合法根据" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%884%EF%BC%89%E8%8E%B7%E7%9B%8A%E6%B2%A1%E6%9C%89%E5%90%88%E6%B3%95%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE">
		<outline text="没有合法根据指的是一方获益既无法律上的根据，亦无合同上的根据。" _mubu_text="%E6%B2%A1%E6%9C%89%E5%90%88%E6%B3%95%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE%E6%8C%87%E7%9A%84%E6%98%AF%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E8%8E%B7%E7%9B%8A%E6%97%A2%E6%97%A0%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E4%B8%8A%E7%9A%84%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE%EF%BC%8C%E4%BA%A6%E6%97%A0%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E4%B8%8A%E7%9A%84%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="没有合法根据包括两种情形：" _mubu_text="%E6%B2%A1%E6%9C%89%E5%90%88%E6%B3%95%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE%E5%8C%85%E6%8B%AC%E4%B8%A4%E7%A7%8D%E6%83%85%E5%BD%A2%EF%BC%9A">
		<outline text="①取得利益时即无合法根据" _mubu_text="%E2%91%A0%E5%8F%96%E5%BE%97%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E6%97%B6%E5%8D%B3%E6%97%A0%E5%90%88%E6%B3%95%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE">
		</outline>
		<outline text="②取得利益时虽有合法根据但事后丧失" _mubu_text="%E2%91%A1%E5%8F%96%E5%BE%97%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E6%97%B6%E8%99%BD%E6%9C%89%E5%90%88%E6%B3%95%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE%E4%BD%86%E4%BA%8B%E5%90%8E%E4%B8%A7%E5%A4%B1">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="不当得利之债的效力" _mubu_text="%E4%B8%8D%E5%BD%93%E5%BE%97%E5%88%A9%E4%B9%8B%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B" _note="@考点" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E8%80%83%E7%82%B9%3C/span%3E">
		<outline text="不当得利一经成立，当事人之间形成债的关系，受有损失的一方享有请求返还其利益的权利，获得利益的一方负有返还利益的义务。" _mubu_text="%E4%B8%8D%E5%BD%93%E5%BE%97%E5%88%A9%E4%B8%80%E7%BB%8F%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%EF%BC%8C%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%B9%8B%E9%97%B4%E5%BD%A2%E6%88%90%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%97%E6%9C%89%E6%8D%9F%E5%A4%B1%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E4%BA%AB%E6%9C%89%E8%AF%B7%E6%B1%82%E8%BF%94%E8%BF%98%E5%85%B6%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%EF%BC%8C%E8%8E%B7%E5%BE%97%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E8%B4%9F%E6%9C%89%E8%BF%94%E8%BF%98%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E7%9A%84%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="应予返还的利益" _mubu_text="%E5%BA%94%E4%BA%88%E8%BF%94%E8%BF%98%E7%9A%84%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A" _note="@考点" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E8%80%83%E7%82%B9%3C/span%3E">
		<outline text="（1）原物" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E5%8E%9F%E7%89%A9">

		</outline>
		<outline text="（3）利用原物所取得的其他利益" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%E5%88%A9%E7%94%A8%E5%8E%9F%E7%89%A9%E6%89%80%E5%8F%96%E5%BE%97%E7%9A%84%E5%85%B6%E4%BB%96%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="返还利益的具体范围" _mubu_text="%E8%BF%94%E8%BF%98%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E7%9A%84%E5%85%B7%E4%BD%93%E8%8C%83%E5%9B%B4">
		<outline text="（1）受益方为善意时" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E5%8F%97%E7%9B%8A%E6%96%B9%E4%B8%BA%E5%96%84%E6%84%8F%E6%97%B6">
		<outline text="①若损失大于利益，只返还现存利益;" _mubu_text="%E2%91%A0%E8%8B%A5%E6%8D%9F%E5%A4%B1%E5%A4%A7%E4%BA%8E%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%AA%E8%BF%94%E8%BF%98%E7%8E%B0%E5%AD%98%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A;">
		</outline>
		<outline text="②若损失小于利益，返还利益的范围以损失为准。" _mubu_text="%E2%91%A1%E8%8B%A5%E6%8D%9F%E5%A4%B1%E5%B0%8F%E4%BA%8E%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%EF%BC%8C%E8%BF%94%E8%BF%98%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E7%9A%84%E8%8C%83%E5%9B%B4%E4%BB%A5%E6%8D%9F%E5%A4%B1%E4%B8%BA%E5%87%86%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="（2）受益方为恶意时" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%E5%8F%97%E7%9B%8A%E6%96%B9%E4%B8%BA%E6%81%B6%E6%84%8F%E6%97%B6">
		<outline text="①应返还其取得的全部利益;" _mubu_text="%E2%91%A0%E5%BA%94%E8%BF%94%E8%BF%98%E5%85%B6%E5%8F%96%E5%BE%97%E7%9A%84%E5%85%A8%E9%83%A8%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A;">
		</outline>
		<outline text="②若利益少于损失，还须就损失与利益之间的差额进行赔偿。" _mubu_text="%E2%91%A1%E8%8B%A5%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E5%B0%91%E4%BA%8E%E6%8D%9F%E5%A4%B1%EF%BC%8C%E8%BF%98%E9%A1%BB%E5%B0%B1%E6%8D%9F%E5%A4%B1%E4%B8%8E%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E4%B9%8B%E9%97%B4%E7%9A%84%E5%B7%AE%E9%A2%9D%E8%BF%9B%E8%A1%8C%E8%B5%94%E5%81%BF%E3%80%82">
		</outline>

		<outline text="328.简述无因管理（概念，构成要件，效力）" _mubu_text="328.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E6%97%A0%E5%9B%A0%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%EF%BC%88%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5%EF%BC%8C%E6%9E%84%E6%88%90%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6%EF%BC%8C%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%EF%BC%89">
		<outline text="无因管理之债的构成要件" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%97%A0%E5%9B%A0%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E4%B9%8B%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%9E%84%E6%88%90%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6%3C/span%3E" _note="@口诀&nbsp;武官腰间管某物&nbsp;@简答题" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E6%AD%A6%E5%AE%98%E8%85%B0%E9%97%B4%E7%AE%A1%E6%9F%90%E7%89%A9&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E" _heading="1" _color="#3da8f5">
		<outline text="无因管理的概念" _mubu_text="%E6%97%A0%E5%9B%A0%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="无因管理是没有法定的或者约定的义务，为避免他人利益受损而进行管理或者服务的行为。" _mubu_text="%E6%97%A0%E5%9B%A0%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E6%98%AF%E6%B2%A1%E6%9C%89%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%BA%E9%81%BF%E5%85%8D%E4%BB%96%E4%BA%BA%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E5%8F%97%E6%8D%9F%E8%80%8C%E8%BF%9B%E8%A1%8C%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E6%9C%8D%E5%8A%A1%E7%9A%84%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="法学通说认为无因管理为事实行为。" _mubu_text="%E6%B3%95%E5%AD%A6%E9%80%9A%E8%AF%B4%E8%AE%A4%E4%B8%BA%E6%97%A0%E5%9B%A0%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E4%B8%BA%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E4%BA%8B%E5%AE%9E%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%3C/span%3E%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="（1）管理他人事物" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E4%BB%96%E4%BA%BA%E4%BA%8B%E7%89%A9">
		<outline text="他人事务是指" _mubu_text="%E4%BB%96%E4%BA%BA%E4%BA%8B%E5%8A%A1%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87">
		<outline text="有关人们生活利益的一切事项，可以是有关财产的，也可以是非财产性的，但不包括公益事业。" _mubu_text="%E6%9C%89%E5%85%B3%E4%BA%BA%E4%BB%AC%E7%94%9F%E6%B4%BB%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%80%E5%88%87%E4%BA%8B%E9%A1%B9%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E6%98%AF%E6%9C%89%E5%85%B3%E8%B4%A2%E4%BA%A7%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E4%B9%9F%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E6%98%AF%E9%9D%9E%E8%B4%A2%E4%BA%A7%E6%80%A7%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E4%BD%86%E4%B8%8D%E5%8C%85%E6%8B%AC%E5%85%AC%E7%9B%8A%E4%BA%8B%E4%B8%9A%E3%80%82" _note="@法条分析" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E6%B3%95%E6%9D%A1%E5%88%86%E6%9E%90%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="管理是指" _mubu_text="%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87">
		<outline text="处理事务的行为，包括事实行为和民事法律行为。但并非对所有事务的管理均会构成无因管理。" _mubu_text="%E5%A4%84%E7%90%86%E4%BA%8B%E5%8A%A1%E7%9A%84%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%EF%BC%8C%E5%8C%85%E6%8B%AC%E4%BA%8B%E5%AE%9E%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E5%92%8C%E6%B0%91%E4%BA%8B%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E3%80%82%E4%BD%86%E5%B9%B6%E9%9D%9E%E5%AF%B9%E6%89%80%E6%9C%89%E4%BA%8B%E5%8A%A1%E7%9A%84%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E5%9D%87%E4%BC%9A%E6%9E%84%E6%88%90%E6%97%A0%E5%9B%A0%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E3%80%82" _note="@法条分析" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E6%B3%95%E6%9D%A1%E5%88%86%E6%9E%90%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="不发生无因管理的情形：" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E4%B8%8D%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E6%97%A0%E5%9B%A0%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E7%9A%84%E6%83%85%E5%BD%A2%EF%BC%9A%3C/span%3E" _note="@口诀&nbsp;不乏武官未到总办寝宫&nbsp;@简答题" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E4%B8%8D%E4%B9%8F%E6%AD%A6%E5%AE%98%E6%9C%AA%E5%88%B0%E6%80%BB%E5%8A%9E%E5%AF%9D%E5%AE%AB&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E" _heading="1" _color="#3da8f5">
		<outline text="1）违法或者违背社会公德的行为；" _mubu_text="1%EF%BC%89%E8%BF%9D%E6%B3%95%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E8%BF%9D%E8%83%8C%E7%A4%BE%E4%BC%9A%E5%85%AC%E5%BE%B7%E7%9A%84%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%EF%BC%9B">
		</outline>
		<outline text="2）纯粹道义上、宗教上或一般生活事务，如招待客人；" _mubu_text="2%EF%BC%89%E7%BA%AF%E7%B2%B9%E9%81%93%E4%B9%89%E4%B8%8A%E3%80%81%E5%AE%97%E6%95%99%E4%B8%8A%E6%88%96%E4%B8%80%E8%88%AC%E7%94%9F%E6%B4%BB%E4%BA%8B%E5%8A%A1%EF%BC%8C%E5%A6%82%E6%8B%9B%E5%BE%85%E5%AE%A2%E4%BA%BA%EF%BC%9B">
		</outline>
		<outline text="3）依法须由本人亲自实施或须经本人授权才能实施的行为，如放弃继承权。" _mubu_text="3%EF%BC%89%E4%BE%9D%E6%B3%95%E9%A1%BB%E7%94%B1%E6%9C%AC%E4%BA%BA%E4%BA%B2%E8%87%AA%E5%AE%9E%E6%96%BD%E6%88%96%E9%A1%BB%E7%BB%8F%E6%9C%AC%E4%BA%BA%E6%8E%88%E6%9D%83%E6%89%8D%E8%83%BD%E5%AE%9E%E6%96%BD%E7%9A%84%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%EF%BC%8C%E5%A6%82%E6%94%BE%E5%BC%83%E7%BB%A7%E6%89%BF%E6%9D%83%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="4）公益事业。" _mubu_text="4%EF%BC%89%E5%85%AC%E7%9B%8A%E4%BA%8B%E4%B8%9A%E3%80%82">

		</outline>
		<outline text="（2）有为他人谋利益的意思" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%E6%9C%89%E4%B8%BA%E4%BB%96%E4%BA%BA%E8%B0%8B%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E7%9A%84%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D">
		<outline text="这是无因管理成立的主观要件，也是无因管理阻却违法性的根本原因。" _mubu_text="%E8%BF%99%E6%98%AF%E6%97%A0%E5%9B%A0%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%BB%E8%A7%82%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E4%B9%9F%E6%98%AF%E6%97%A0%E5%9B%A0%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E9%98%BB%E5%8D%B4%E8%BF%9D%E6%B3%95%E6%80%A7%E7%9A%84%E6%A0%B9%E6%9C%AC%E5%8E%9F%E5%9B%A0%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		<outline text="该意思无需表示，只要管理行为在客观上避免了他人利益受损且管理人不纯粹是出于为自己谋利的目的，就构成无因管理行为，即使管理人主观上有为自己的动机且客观上使自己同时受益，仍不影响无因管理的成立。" _mubu_text="%E8%AF%A5%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E6%97%A0%E9%9C%80%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%AA%E8%A6%81%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E5%9C%A8%E5%AE%A2%E8%A7%82%E4%B8%8A%E9%81%BF%E5%85%8D%E4%BA%86%E4%BB%96%E4%BA%BA%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E5%8F%97%E6%8D%9F%E4%B8%94%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%8D%E7%BA%AF%E7%B2%B9%E6%98%AF%E5%87%BA%E4%BA%8E%E4%B8%BA%E8%87%AA%E5%B7%B1%E8%B0%8B%E5%88%A9%E7%9A%84%E7%9B%AE%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E5%B0%B1%E6%9E%84%E6%88%90%E6%97%A0%E5%9B%A0%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%EF%BC%8C%E5%8D%B3%E4%BD%BF%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%BB%E8%A7%82%E4%B8%8A%E6%9C%89%E4%B8%BA%E8%87%AA%E5%B7%B1%E7%9A%84%E5%8A%A8%E6%9C%BA%E4%B8%94%E5%AE%A2%E8%A7%82%E4%B8%8A%E4%BD%BF%E8%87%AA%E5%B7%B1%E5%90%8C%E6%97%B6%E5%8F%97%E7%9B%8A%EF%BC%8C%E4%BB%8D%E4%B8%8D%E5%BD%B1%E5%93%8D%E6%97%A0%E5%9B%A0%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E7%9A%84%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="（3）无法律上的义务" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%E6%97%A0%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E4%B8%8A%E7%9A%84%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1">
		<outline text="法律上的义务，包括法定义务和约定义务。" _mubu_text="%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E4%B8%8A%E7%9A%84%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%EF%BC%8C%E5%8C%85%E6%8B%AC%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E5%92%8C%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="法定义务" _mubu_text="%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1">
		<outline text="如抚养义务。" _mubu_text="%E5%A6%82%E6%8A%9A%E5%85%BB%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="约定义务" _mubu_text="%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1">
		<outline text="如受托人对委托人承担的义务。" _mubu_text="%E5%A6%82%E5%8F%97%E6%89%98%E4%BA%BA%E5%AF%B9%E5%A7%94%E6%89%98%E4%BA%BA%E6%89%BF%E6%8B%85%E7%9A%84%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="无法律上的义务，应当以管理人开始管理时的客观事实而定。" _mubu_text="%E6%97%A0%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E4%B8%8A%E7%9A%84%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%EF%BC%8C%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E4%BB%A5%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E4%BA%BA%E5%BC%80%E5%A7%8B%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E6%97%B6%E7%9A%84%E5%AE%A2%E8%A7%82%E4%BA%8B%E5%AE%9E%E8%80%8C%E5%AE%9A%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="无因管理之债的效力" _mubu_text="%E6%97%A0%E5%9B%A0%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E4%B9%8B%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B">
		<outline text="无因管理一经成立，当事人之间即形成债的关系。" _mubu_text="%E6%97%A0%E5%9B%A0%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E4%B8%80%E7%BB%8F%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%EF%BC%8C%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%B9%8B%E9%97%B4%E5%8D%B3%E5%BD%A2%E6%88%90%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="管理人的权利" _mubu_text="%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9">
		<outline text="管理人享有请求偿还因管理或服务所支出的必要费用的权利。" _mubu_text="%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E4%BA%BA%E4%BA%AB%E6%9C%89%E8%AF%B7%E6%B1%82%E5%81%BF%E8%BF%98%E5%9B%A0%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E6%88%96%E6%9C%8D%E5%8A%A1%E6%89%80%E6%94%AF%E5%87%BA%E7%9A%84%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%BF%85%E8%A6%81%E8%B4%B9%E7%94%A8%3C/span%3E%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="管理人的义务" _mubu_text="%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1">
		<outline text="管理人承担适当管理、通知以及报告与计算的义务。" _mubu_text="%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E4%BA%BA%E6%89%BF%E6%8B%85%E9%80%82%E5%BD%93%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E3%80%81%E9%80%9A%E7%9F%A5%E4%BB%A5%E5%8F%8A%E6%8A%A5%E5%91%8A%E4%B8%8E%E8%AE%A1%E7%AE%97%E7%9A%84%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="本人负有偿付该费用的义务。" _mubu_text="%E6%9C%AC%E4%BA%BA%E8%B4%9F%E6%9C%89%E5%81%BF%E4%BB%98%E8%AF%A5%E8%B4%B9%E7%94%A8%E7%9A%84%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="必要费用的范围" _mubu_text="%E5%BF%85%E8%A6%81%E8%B4%B9%E7%94%A8%E7%9A%84%E8%8C%83%E5%9B%B4" _note="@法条分析&nbsp;@考点" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E6%B3%95%E6%9D%A1%E5%88%86%E6%9E%90%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E8%80%83%E7%82%B9%3C/span%3E">
		<outline text="（1）管理人在管理或服务活动中直接支出的费用，以及在活动中受到的实际损失。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E4%BA%BA%E5%9C%A8%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E6%88%96%E6%9C%8D%E5%8A%A1%E6%B4%BB%E5%8A%A8%E4%B8%AD%E7%9B%B4%E6%8E%A5%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%94%AF%E5%87%BA%E7%9A%84%E8%B4%B9%E7%94%A8%3C/span%3E%EF%BC%8C%E4%BB%A5%E5%8F%8A%E5%9C%A8%E6%B4%BB%E5%8A%A8%E4%B8%AD%E5%8F%97%E5%88%B0%E7%9A%84%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%AE%9E%E9%99%85%E6%8D%9F%E5%A4%B1%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（2）管理人为本人利益而以管理人的名义负担的债务，有权要求本人直接向债权人清偿。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%BA%E6%9C%AC%E4%BA%BA%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E8%80%8C%E4%BB%A5%E7%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%90%8D%E4%B9%89%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E8%B4%9F%E6%8B%85%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%3C/span%3E%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%9C%89%E6%9D%83%E8%A6%81%E6%B1%82%E6%9C%AC%E4%BA%BA%E7%9B%B4%E6%8E%A5%E5%90%91%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（3）该必要费用一般以本人所受利益范围为限。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E8%AF%A5%E5%BF%85%E8%A6%81%E8%B4%B9%E7%94%A8%E4%B8%80%E8%88%AC%E4%BB%A5%E6%9C%AC%E4%BA%BA%E6%89%80%E5%8F%97%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E8%8C%83%E5%9B%B4%E4%B8%BA%E9%99%90%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		</outline>
