		<outline text="329.简述合同的概念和特点" _mubu_text="329.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5%E5%92%8C%E7%89%B9%E7%82%B9">
		<outline text="合同的特征" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E7%89%B9%E5%BE%81%3C/span%3E" _note="@简答题&nbsp;@口诀&nbsp;何政性和睦" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E4%BD%95%E6%94%BF%E6%80%A7%E5%92%8C%E7%9D%A6" _heading="1" _color="#3da8f5">
		<outline text="合同的概念" _mubu_text="%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="合同是平等主体的自然人、法人及其他组织之间设立、变更、终止民事权利义务关系的协议。" _mubu_text="%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%98%AF%E5%B9%B3%E7%AD%89%E4%B8%BB%E4%BD%93%E7%9A%84%E8%87%AA%E7%84%B6%E4%BA%BA%E3%80%81%E6%B3%95%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%8A%E5%85%B6%E4%BB%96%E7%BB%84%E7%BB%87%E4%B9%8B%E9%97%B4%E8%AE%BE%E7%AB%8B%E3%80%81%E5%8F%98%E6%9B%B4%E3%80%81%E7%BB%88%E6%AD%A2%E6%B0%91%E4%BA%8B%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E7%9A%84%E5%8D%8F%E8%AE%AE%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="广义的合同不仅包括有关财产关系的协议，也包括有关身份关系的协议。" _mubu_text="%E5%B9%BF%E4%B9%89%E7%9A%84%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E4%B8%8D%E4%BB%85%E5%8C%85%E6%8B%AC%E6%9C%89%E5%85%B3%E8%B4%A2%E4%BA%A7%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E7%9A%84%E5%8D%8F%E8%AE%AE%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E4%B9%9F%E5%8C%85%E6%8B%AC%E6%9C%89%E5%85%B3%E8%BA%AB%E4%BB%BD%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E7%9A%84%E5%8D%8F%E8%AE%AE%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		<outline text="狭义的合同即指有关财产关系的协议。本章所研究的是狭义的合同。" _mubu_text="%E7%8B%AD%E4%B9%89%E7%9A%84%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E5%8D%B3%E6%8C%87%E6%9C%89%E5%85%B3%E8%B4%A2%E4%BA%A7%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E7%9A%84%E5%8D%8F%E8%AE%AE%E3%80%82%E6%9C%AC%E7%AB%A0%E6%89%80%E7%A0%94%E7%A9%B6%E7%9A%84%E6%98%AF%E7%8B%AD%E4%B9%89%E7%9A%84%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="（1）合同是一种民事法律行为，以意思表示为要素并依意思表示的内容发生相应法律后果。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%98%AF%E4%B8%80%E7%A7%8D%E6%B0%91%E4%BA%8B%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%EF%BC%8C%E4%BB%A5%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E4%B8%BA%E8%A6%81%E7%B4%A0%E5%B9%B6%E4%BE%9D%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E7%9B%B8%E5%BA%94%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E5%90%8E%E6%9E%9C%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（2）合同是两方以上当事人意思表示一致的民事法律行为，是平等当事人之间的一种协议或合意。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%98%AF%E4%B8%A4%E6%96%B9%E4%BB%A5%E4%B8%8A%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E4%B8%80%E8%87%B4%E7%9A%84%E6%B0%91%E4%BA%8B%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%EF%BC%8C%E6%98%AF%E5%B9%B3%E7%AD%89%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%B9%8B%E9%97%B4%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%80%E7%A7%8D%E5%8D%8F%E8%AE%AE%E6%88%96%E5%90%88%E6%84%8F%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（3）合同以设立、变更、终止民事权利义务关系为目的。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E4%BB%A5%E8%AE%BE%E7%AB%8B%E3%80%81%E5%8F%98%E6%9B%B4%E3%80%81%E7%BB%88%E6%AD%A2%E6%B0%91%E4%BA%8B%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E4%B8%BA%E7%9B%AE%E7%9A%84%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="330.简述合同法的基本原则" _mubu_text="330.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%B3%95%E7%9A%84%E5%9F%BA%E6%9C%AC%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99">
		<outline text="合同法的基本原则" _mubu_text="%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%B3%95%E7%9A%84%E5%9F%BA%E6%9C%AC%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99" _note="@口诀&nbsp;菏泽自演义" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E8%8F%8F%E6%B3%BD%E8%87%AA%E6%BC%94%E4%B9%89">
		<outline text="合同法的基本原则的概念" _mubu_text="%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%B3%95%E7%9A%84%E5%9F%BA%E6%9C%AC%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="合同法的基本原则 ，是指合同立法的指导思想以及调整民事主体之间合同关系应遵循的基本方针和准则。" _mubu_text="%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%B3%95%E7%9A%84%E5%9F%BA%E6%9C%AC%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99%20%EF%BC%8C%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%AB%8B%E6%B3%95%E7%9A%84%E6%8C%87%E5%AF%BC%E6%80%9D%E6%83%B3%E4%BB%A5%E5%8F%8A%E8%B0%83%E6%95%B4%E6%B0%91%E4%BA%8B%E4%B8%BB%E4%BD%93%E4%B9%8B%E9%97%B4%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E5%BA%94%E9%81%B5%E5%BE%AA%E7%9A%84%E5%9F%BA%E6%9C%AC%E6%96%B9%E9%92%88%E5%92%8C%E5%87%86%E5%88%99%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="合同法是民法的组成部分，民法的基本原则当然适用于合同法，但合同法领域也存在着专有的基本原则：" _mubu_text="%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%B3%95%E6%98%AF%E6%B0%91%E6%B3%95%E7%9A%84%E7%BB%84%E6%88%90%E9%83%A8%E5%88%86%EF%BC%8C%E6%B0%91%E6%B3%95%E7%9A%84%E5%9F%BA%E6%9C%AC%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99%E5%BD%93%E7%84%B6%E9%80%82%E7%94%A8%E4%BA%8E%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%B3%95%EF%BC%8C%E4%BD%86%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%B3%95%E9%A2%86%E5%9F%9F%E4%B9%9F%E5%AD%98%E5%9C%A8%E7%9D%80%E4%B8%93%E6%9C%89%E7%9A%84%E5%9F%BA%E6%9C%AC%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99%EF%BC%9A">
		<outline text="1.合同自由原则" _mubu_text="1.%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E8%87%AA%E7%94%B1%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99">
		<outline text="合同自由原则的概念" _mubu_text="%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E8%87%AA%E7%94%B1%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="合同自由原则,是指合同当事人有权对权利、义务关系进行自由协商,不受国家权力和其他主体的非法干预。根据合同自由原则,当事人：" _mubu_text="%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E8%87%AA%E7%94%B1%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99,%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E6%9C%89%E6%9D%83%E5%AF%B9%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E3%80%81%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E8%BF%9B%E8%A1%8C%E8%87%AA%E7%94%B1%E5%8D%8F%E5%95%86,%E4%B8%8D%E5%8F%97%E5%9B%BD%E5%AE%B6%E6%9D%83%E5%8A%9B%E5%92%8C%E5%85%B6%E4%BB%96%E4%B8%BB%E4%BD%93%E7%9A%84%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%B9%B2%E9%A2%84%E3%80%82%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E8%87%AA%E7%94%B1%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99,%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%EF%BC%9A">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="合同自由原则的含义" _mubu_text="%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E8%87%AA%E7%94%B1%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99%E7%9A%84%E5%90%AB%E4%B9%89" _note="@口诀&nbsp;合资则是巷内性感" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E5%90%88%E8%B5%84%E5%88%99%E6%98%AF%E5%B7%B7%E5%86%85%E6%80%A7%E6%84%9F">
		<outline text="（1）当事人有权决定是否与他人签订合同" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E6%9C%89%E6%9D%83%E5%86%B3%E5%AE%9A%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%98%AF%3C/span%3E%E5%90%A6%E4%B8%8E%E4%BB%96%E4%BA%BA%E7%AD%BE%E8%AE%A2%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（2）有权选择交易对象" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%E6%9C%89%E6%9D%83%E9%80%89%E6%8B%A9%E4%BA%A4%E6%98%93%E5%AF%B9%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E8%B1%A1%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（3）有权决定合同的具体内容" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%E6%9C%89%E6%9D%83%E5%86%B3%E5%AE%9A%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E5%85%B7%E4%BD%93%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%86%85%3C/span%3E%E5%AE%B9">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（4）有权选择合同形式" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%884%EF%BC%89%E6%9C%89%E6%9D%83%E9%80%89%E6%8B%A9%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%BD%A2%3C/span%3E%E5%BC%8F">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（5）但是国家可以依法对当事人的合同自由进行干预，以实现合同自由和合同正义的统一。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%885%EF%BC%89%E4%BD%86%E6%98%AF%E5%9B%BD%E5%AE%B6%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E4%BE%9D%E6%B3%95%E5%AF%B9%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E8%87%AA%E7%94%B1%E8%BF%9B%E8%A1%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%B9%B2%3C/span%3E%E9%A2%84%EF%BC%8C%E4%BB%A5%E5%AE%9E%E7%8E%B0%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E8%87%AA%E7%94%B1%E5%92%8C%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%AD%A3%E4%B9%89%E7%9A%84%E7%BB%9F%E4%B8%80%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="2.合同严守原则" _mubu_text="2.%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E4%B8%A5%E5%AE%88%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99">
		<outline text="合同严守原则的概念" _mubu_text="%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E4%B8%A5%E5%AE%88%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="合同严守原则，是指依法成立的合同在当事人之间具有法律约束力，当事人必须严格遵守，不得擅自变更或者解除合同，也不得随意违约。" _mubu_text="%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E4%B8%A5%E5%AE%88%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99%EF%BC%8C%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E4%BE%9D%E6%B3%95%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E7%9A%84%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E5%9C%A8%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%B9%8B%E9%97%B4%E5%85%B7%E6%9C%89%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E7%BA%A6%E6%9D%9F%E5%8A%9B%EF%BC%8C%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E5%BF%85%E9%A1%BB%E4%B8%A5%E6%A0%BC%E9%81%B5%E5%AE%88%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%8D%E5%BE%97%E6%93%85%E8%87%AA%E5%8F%98%E6%9B%B4%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E8%A7%A3%E9%99%A4%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%EF%BC%8C%E4%B9%9F%E4%B8%8D%E5%BE%97%E9%9A%8F%E6%84%8F%E8%BF%9D%E7%BA%A6%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="合同严守原则的含义" _mubu_text="%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E4%B8%A5%E5%AE%88%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99%E7%9A%84%E5%90%AB%E4%B9%89" _note="@口诀&nbsp;贺寿择月出泽" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E8%B4%BA%E5%AF%BF%E6%8B%A9%E6%9C%88%E5%87%BA%E6%B3%BD">
		<outline text="（1）根据合同严守原则，自合同依法成立时起，双方当事人都要受到合同的约束;" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E4%B8%A5%E5%AE%88%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99%EF%BC%8C%E8%87%AA%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E4%BE%9D%E6%B3%95%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E6%97%B6%E8%B5%B7%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%8C%E6%96%B9%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E9%83%BD%E8%A6%81%E5%8F%97%E5%88%B0%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E7%BA%A6%E6%9D%9F;">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（2）在符合变更或者解除合同的条件时，当事人应按照约定或法律的规定协商解决，任何一方都不得擅自变更或解除合同；" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%E5%9C%A8%E7%AC%A6%E5%90%88%E5%8F%98%E6%9B%B4%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E8%A7%A3%E9%99%A4%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E6%97%B6%EF%BC%8C%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E5%BA%94%E6%8C%89%E7%85%A7%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E6%88%96%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E7%9A%84%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E5%8D%8F%E5%95%86%E8%A7%A3%E5%86%B3%EF%BC%8C%E4%BB%BB%E4%BD%95%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E9%83%BD%E4%B8%8D%E5%BE%97%E6%93%85%E8%87%AA%E5%8F%98%E6%9B%B4%E6%88%96%E8%A7%A3%E9%99%A4%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%EF%BC%9B">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（3）除法律规定的免责事由外，任何一方当事人不履行合同义务或者履行合同义务不符合约定时，都要承担违约责任。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%E9%99%A4%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E5%85%8D%E8%B4%A3%E4%BA%8B%E7%94%B1%E5%A4%96%EF%BC%8C%E4%BB%BB%E4%BD%95%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%8D%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E4%B8%8D%E7%AC%A6%E5%90%88%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E6%97%B6%EF%BC%8C%E9%83%BD%E8%A6%81%E6%89%BF%E6%8B%85%E8%BF%9D%E7%BA%A6%E8%B4%A3%E4%BB%BB%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="3.鼓励交易原则" _mubu_text="3.%E9%BC%93%E5%8A%B1%E4%BA%A4%E6%98%93%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99">
		<outline text="鼓励交易原则的概念" _mubu_text="%E9%BC%93%E5%8A%B1%E4%BA%A4%E6%98%93%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="鼓励交易原则，是指合同法以降低当事人的交易成本，减少交易的制度障碍为指导思想，以促进当事人通过合同实现交易目标。" _mubu_text="%E9%BC%93%E5%8A%B1%E4%BA%A4%E6%98%93%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99%EF%BC%8C%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%B3%95%E4%BB%A5%E9%99%8D%E4%BD%8E%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E4%BA%A4%E6%98%93%E6%88%90%E6%9C%AC%EF%BC%8C%E5%87%8F%E5%B0%91%E4%BA%A4%E6%98%93%E7%9A%84%E5%88%B6%E5%BA%A6%E9%9A%9C%E7%A2%8D%E4%B8%BA%E6%8C%87%E5%AF%BC%E6%80%9D%E6%83%B3%EF%BC%8C%E4%BB%A5%E4%BF%83%E8%BF%9B%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E9%80%9A%E8%BF%87%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E5%AE%9E%E7%8E%B0%E4%BA%A4%E6%98%93%E7%9B%AE%E6%A0%87%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="鼓励交易原则在我国合同法中有全面体现：" _mubu_text="%E9%BC%93%E5%8A%B1%E4%BA%A4%E6%98%93%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99%E5%9C%A8%E6%88%91%E5%9B%BD%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%B3%95%E4%B8%AD%E6%9C%89%E5%85%A8%E9%9D%A2%E4%BD%93%E7%8E%B0%EF%BC%9A" _note="@口诀&nbsp;河谷泽城简介" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E6%B2%B3%E8%B0%B7%E6%B3%BD%E5%9F%8E%E7%AE%80%E4%BB%8B">
		<outline text="（1）尽可能使当事人之间的合同成立;" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E5%B0%BD%E5%8F%AF%E8%83%BD%E4%BD%BF%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%B9%8B%E9%97%B4%E7%9A%84%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B;">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（2）减少无效合同的种类;" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%E5%87%8F%E5%B0%91%E6%97%A0%E6%95%88%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E7%A7%8D%E7%B1%BB;">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（3）对合同解除规定了严格的法定条件等。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%E5%AF%B9%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E8%A7%A3%E9%99%A4%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E4%BA%86%E4%B8%A5%E6%A0%BC%E7%9A%84%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E7%AD%89%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="合同的成立要件" _mubu_text="%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6">
		<outline text="一般成立要件" _mubu_text="%E4%B8%80%E8%88%AC%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6">
		<outline text="一般成立要件是所有合同成立均须具备的条件，包括：" _mubu_text="%E4%B8%80%E8%88%AC%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6%E6%98%AF%E6%89%80%E6%9C%89%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E5%9D%87%E9%A1%BB%E5%85%B7%E5%A4%87%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%EF%BC%8C%E5%8C%85%E6%8B%AC%EF%BC%9A">
		<outline text="有双方或多方当事人" _mubu_text="%E6%9C%89%E5%8F%8C%E6%96%B9%E6%88%96%E5%A4%9A%E6%96%B9%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA">
		</outline>
		<outline text="当事人就合同必要条款达成合意、合同内容明确。" _mubu_text="%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E5%B0%B1%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E5%BF%85%E8%A6%81%E6%9D%A1%E6%AC%BE%E8%BE%BE%E6%88%90%E5%90%88%E6%84%8F%E3%80%81%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E6%98%8E%E7%A1%AE%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="经过要约和承诺阶段等。" _mubu_text="%E7%BB%8F%E8%BF%87%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E5%92%8C%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5%E7%AD%89%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="对合同是否成立的认定" _mubu_text="%E5%AF%B9%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%98%AF%E5%90%A6%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E7%9A%84%E8%AE%A4%E5%AE%9A">
		<outline text="除法律另有规定或者当事人另有约定外，当事人对合同是否成立存在争议，能够确定当事人名称或者姓名、标的和数量的，一般应当认定合同成立。" _mubu_text="%E9%99%A4%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E5%8F%A6%E6%9C%89%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%A6%E6%9C%89%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E5%A4%96%EF%BC%8C%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E5%AF%B9%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%98%AF%E5%90%A6%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E5%AD%98%E5%9C%A8%E4%BA%89%E8%AE%AE%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E8%83%BD%E5%A4%9F%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E5%90%8D%E7%A7%B0%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%A7%93%E5%90%8D%E3%80%81%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E5%92%8C%E6%95%B0%E9%87%8F%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%80%E8%88%AC%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E8%AE%A4%E5%AE%9A%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E" _note="@考点" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E8%80%83%E7%82%B9%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="特别成立要件。" _mubu_text="%E7%89%B9%E5%88%AB%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="特别成立要件是指某些合同成立必须具备的要件，如某些合同需要具备特定的形式才能成立,某些合同须以交付标的物作为成立要件。" _mubu_text="%E7%89%B9%E5%88%AB%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E6%9F%90%E4%BA%9B%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E5%BF%85%E9%A1%BB%E5%85%B7%E5%A4%87%E7%9A%84%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6%EF%BC%8C%E5%A6%82%E6%9F%90%E4%BA%9B%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E9%9C%80%E8%A6%81%E5%85%B7%E5%A4%87%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E5%BD%A2%E5%BC%8F%E6%89%8D%E8%83%BD%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B,%E6%9F%90%E4%BA%9B%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E9%A1%BB%E4%BB%A5%E4%BA%A4%E4%BB%98%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E7%89%A9%E4%BD%9C%E4%B8%BA%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="332.简述合同订立的一般程序" _mubu_text="332.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E8%AE%A2%E7%AB%8B%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%80%E8%88%AC%E7%A8%8B%E5%BA%8F">
		<outline text="合同订立的一般程序" _mubu_text="%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E8%AE%A2%E7%AB%8B%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%80%E8%88%AC%E7%A8%8B%E5%BA%8F">
		<outline text="合同成立通常需要经过要约和承诺两个阶段。" _mubu_text="%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E9%80%9A%E5%B8%B8%E9%9C%80%E8%A6%81%E7%BB%8F%E8%BF%87%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E5%92%8C%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E4%B8%A4%E4%B8%AA%E9%98%B6%E6%AE%B5%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="要约" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6">
		<outline text="要约的概念" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="要约是当事人一方向对方发出的希望与对方订立合同的意思表示。" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E6%98%AF%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E5%90%91%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E5%8F%91%E5%87%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%B8%8C%E6%9C%9B%E4%B8%8E%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E8%AE%A2%E7%AB%8B%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="要约的条件" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%3C/span%3E" _note="@简答题&nbsp;@题眼&nbsp;@口诀&nbsp;要约条件特目内承" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E9%A2%98%E7%9C%BC%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E7%89%B9%E7%9B%AE%E5%86%85%E6%89%BF" _heading="1" _color="#dc2d1e">
		<outline text="要约的概念" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="要约是当事人一方向对方发出的希望与对方订立合同的意思表示。" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E6%98%AF%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E5%90%91%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E5%8F%91%E5%87%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%B8%8C%E6%9C%9B%E4%B8%8E%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E8%AE%A2%E7%AB%8B%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(1)要约必须是特定人向相对人发出的意思表示。" _mubu_text="(1)%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E5%BF%85%E9%A1%BB%E6%98%AF%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E4%BA%BA%E5%90%91%E7%9B%B8%E5%AF%B9%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%91%E5%87%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="换言之，要约人必须是在客观上可以确定的人；而要约的相对人则既可以是特定的某个人，也可以是不特定的社会公众。如商店的商品标价陈列，可以看作向不特定的人发出的要约。" _mubu_text="%E6%8D%A2%E8%A8%80%E4%B9%8B%EF%BC%8C%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E5%BF%85%E9%A1%BB%E6%98%AF%E5%9C%A8%E5%AE%A2%E8%A7%82%E4%B8%8A%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E4%BA%BA%EF%BC%9B%E8%80%8C%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E7%9B%B8%E5%AF%B9%E4%BA%BA%E5%88%99%E6%97%A2%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E6%98%AF%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E6%9F%90%E4%B8%AA%E4%BA%BA%EF%BC%8C%E4%B9%9F%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E6%98%AF%E4%B8%8D%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E7%A4%BE%E4%BC%9A%E5%85%AC%E4%BC%97%E3%80%82%E5%A6%82%E5%95%86%E5%BA%97%E7%9A%84%E5%95%86%E5%93%81%E6%A0%87%E4%BB%B7%E9%99%88%E5%88%97%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E7%9C%8B%E4%BD%9C%E5%90%91%E4%B8%8D%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%91%E5%87%BA%E7%9A%84%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(2)要约必须以缔结合同为目的。" _mubu_text="(2)%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E5%BF%85%E9%A1%BB%E4%BB%A5%E7%BC%94%E7%BB%93%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E4%B8%BA%E7%9B%AE%E7%9A%84%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="非以缔结合同为目的的表示不属于要约。" _mubu_text="%E9%9D%9E%E4%BB%A5%E7%BC%94%E7%BB%93%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E4%B8%BA%E7%9B%AE%E7%9A%84%E7%9A%84%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E4%B8%8D%E5%B1%9E%E4%BA%8E%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(3)要约的内容应具体确定。" _mubu_text="(3)%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E5%BA%94%E5%85%B7%E4%BD%93%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="要约一经相对人承诺即导致合同成立。因此，要约的内容必须具体确定，至少应包括拟订立合同的必备条款，以供相对人考虑是否承诺。" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%B8%80%E7%BB%8F%E7%9B%B8%E5%AF%B9%E4%BA%BA%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E5%8D%B3%E5%AF%BC%E8%87%B4%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E3%80%82%E5%9B%A0%E6%AD%A4%EF%BC%8C%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E5%BF%85%E9%A1%BB%E5%85%B7%E4%BD%93%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E8%87%B3%E5%B0%91%E5%BA%94%E5%8C%85%E6%8B%AC%E6%8B%9F%E8%AE%A2%E7%AB%8B%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E5%BF%85%E5%A4%87%E6%9D%A1%E6%AC%BE%EF%BC%8C%E4%BB%A5%E4%BE%9B%E7%9B%B8%E5%AF%B9%E4%BA%BA%E8%80%83%E8%99%91%E6%98%AF%E5%90%A6%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(4)要约必须表明经受要约人承诺，要约人即受该意思表示约束。" _mubu_text="(4)%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E5%BF%85%E9%A1%BB%E8%A1%A8%E6%98%8E%E7%BB%8F%E5%8F%97%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%EF%BC%8C%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E5%8D%B3%E5%8F%97%E8%AF%A5%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E7%BA%A6%E6%9D%9F%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="要约的法律效力。" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="（1）要约生效后，要约人应受要约的约束，在要约有效期内不得随意撤销或变更要约；（针对要约人的效力）" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E5%90%8E%EF%BC%8C%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E5%BA%94%E5%8F%97%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E7%BA%A6%E6%9D%9F%EF%BC%8C%E5%9C%A8%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E6%9C%89%E6%95%88%E6%9C%9F%E5%86%85%E4%B8%8D%E5%BE%97%E9%9A%8F%E6%84%8F%E6%92%A4%E9%94%80%E6%88%96%E5%8F%98%E6%9B%B4%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%EF%BC%9B%EF%BC%88%E9%92%88%E5%AF%B9%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%EF%BC%89">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（2）受要约人则取得了承诺的权利，受要约人有权在要约的有效期限内作出接受要约的答复，而不负必须承诺的义务。即使受要约人不承诺，也没有通知要约人的义务。（针对受要约人的效力）" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%E5%8F%97%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E5%88%99%E5%8F%96%E5%BE%97%E4%BA%86%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%97%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E6%9C%89%E6%9D%83%E5%9C%A8%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E6%9C%89%E6%95%88%E6%9C%9F%E9%99%90%E5%86%85%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E6%8E%A5%E5%8F%97%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E7%AD%94%E5%A4%8D%EF%BC%8C%E8%80%8C%E4%B8%8D%E8%B4%9F%E5%BF%85%E9%A1%BB%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E7%9A%84%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E3%80%82%E5%8D%B3%E4%BD%BF%E5%8F%97%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%8D%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%EF%BC%8C%E4%B9%9F%E6%B2%A1%E6%9C%89%E9%80%9A%E7%9F%A5%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E3%80%82%EF%BC%88%E9%92%88%E5%AF%B9%E5%8F%97%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%EF%BC%89">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（3）要约的生效时间因要约形式的不同而有所不同。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E6%97%B6%E9%97%B4%E5%9B%A0%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E5%BD%A2%E5%BC%8F%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%8D%E5%90%8C%E8%80%8C%E6%9C%89%E6%89%80%E4%B8%8D%E5%90%8C%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="一般来说，口头要约自受要约人了解时生效，书面要约自要约到达受要约人时生效。在要约生效前，要约人可以撤回要约；要约生效后，在符合法定条件时，要约人可以撤销要约。" _mubu_text="%E4%B8%80%E8%88%AC%E6%9D%A5%E8%AF%B4%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%A3%E5%A4%B4%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E8%87%AA%E5%8F%97%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E4%BA%86%E8%A7%A3%E6%97%B6%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%EF%BC%8C%E4%B9%A6%E9%9D%A2%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E8%87%AA%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E5%88%B0%E8%BE%BE%E5%8F%97%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E6%97%B6%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E3%80%82%E5%9C%A8%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E5%89%8D%EF%BC%8C%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E6%92%A4%E5%9B%9E%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%EF%BC%9B%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E5%90%8E%EF%BC%8C%E5%9C%A8%E7%AC%A6%E5%90%88%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E6%97%B6%EF%BC%8C%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E6%92%A4%E9%94%80%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="要约与要约邀请的相同之处是:" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%B8%8E%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E9%82%80%E8%AF%B7%E7%9A%84%E7%9B%B8%E5%90%8C%E4%B9%8B%E5%A4%84%E6%98%AF:%3C/span%3E" _note="@口诀&nbsp;姚姚同特意&nbsp;@简答题" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E5%A7%9A%E5%A7%9A%E5%90%8C%E7%89%B9%E6%84%8F&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E" _heading="1" _color="#3da8f5">
		<outline text="要约邀请的概念" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E9%82%80%E8%AF%B7%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="要约邀请，是一方向他方作出的希望他方向自己发出要约的意思表示。" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E9%82%80%E8%AF%B7%EF%BC%8C%E6%98%AF%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E5%90%91%E4%BB%96%E6%96%B9%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%B8%8C%E6%9C%9B%E4%BB%96%E6%96%B9%E5%90%91%E8%87%AA%E5%B7%B1%E5%8F%91%E5%87%BA%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="要约的概念" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="要约是当事人一方向对方发出的希望与对方订立合同的意思表示。" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E6%98%AF%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E5%90%91%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E5%8F%91%E5%87%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%B8%8C%E6%9C%9B%E4%B8%8E%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E8%AE%A2%E7%AB%8B%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(1)由特定人向特定人或不特定人发出。" _mubu_text="(1)%E7%94%B1%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E4%BA%BA%E5%90%91%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E4%BA%BA%E6%88%96%E4%B8%8D%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%91%E5%87%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="(2)均属于意思表示，故应具备意思表示的成立要件。" _mubu_text="(2)%E5%9D%87%E5%B1%9E%E4%BA%8E%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%EF%BC%8C%E6%95%85%E5%BA%94%E5%85%B7%E5%A4%87%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="要约与要约邀的请区别是:" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%B8%8E%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E9%82%80%E7%9A%84%E8%AF%B7%E5%8C%BA%E5%88%AB%E6%98%AF:">
		<outline text="(1)目的不同。" _mubu_text="(1)%E7%9B%AE%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%8D%E5%90%8C%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="要约的目的在于获得对方的承诺以成立合同；" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E7%9B%AE%E7%9A%84%E5%9C%A8%E4%BA%8E%E8%8E%B7%E5%BE%97%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E7%9A%84%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E4%BB%A5%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%EF%BC%9B">
		</outline>
		<outline text="要约邀请的目的在于引出对方的要约。" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E9%82%80%E8%AF%B7%E7%9A%84%E7%9B%AE%E7%9A%84%E5%9C%A8%E4%BA%8E%E5%BC%95%E5%87%BA%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E7%9A%84%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(2)条件不同。" _mubu_text="(2)%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E4%B8%8D%E5%90%8C%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="要约的条件如前所述；" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E5%A6%82%E5%89%8D%E6%89%80%E8%BF%B0%EF%BC%9B">
		</outline>
		<outline text="要约邀请无须具备前述条件，如无须内容具体确定只要邀请人足以确定即可。" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E9%82%80%E8%AF%B7%E6%97%A0%E9%A1%BB%E5%85%B7%E5%A4%87%E5%89%8D%E8%BF%B0%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%EF%BC%8C%E5%A6%82%E6%97%A0%E9%A1%BB%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E5%85%B7%E4%BD%93%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%E5%8F%AA%E8%A6%81%E9%82%80%E8%AF%B7%E4%BA%BA%E8%B6%B3%E4%BB%A5%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%E5%8D%B3%E5%8F%AF%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(3)效力不同。" _mubu_text="(3)%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%E4%B8%8D%E5%90%8C%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="要约人须受要约约束；" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E9%A1%BB%E5%8F%97%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%BA%A6%E6%9D%9F%EF%BC%9B">
		</outline>
		<outline text="要约邀请本身没有法律效力，故邀请人不受要约邀请的约束。" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E9%82%80%E8%AF%B7%E6%9C%AC%E8%BA%AB%E6%B2%A1%E6%9C%89%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%EF%BC%8C%E6%95%85%E9%82%80%E8%AF%B7%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%8D%E5%8F%97%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E9%82%80%E8%AF%B7%E7%9A%84%E7%BA%A6%E6%9D%9F%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="一般来讲，寄送的价目表、拍卖公告、招标公告、招股说明书、商业广告等均为要约邀请。但商业广告的内容符合要约规定的,视为要约。" _mubu_text="%E4%B8%80%E8%88%AC%E6%9D%A5%E8%AE%B2%EF%BC%8C%E5%AF%84%E9%80%81%E7%9A%84%E4%BB%B7%E7%9B%AE%E8%A1%A8%E3%80%81%E6%8B%8D%E5%8D%96%E5%85%AC%E5%91%8A%E3%80%81%E6%8B%9B%E6%A0%87%E5%85%AC%E5%91%8A%E3%80%81%E6%8B%9B%E8%82%A1%E8%AF%B4%E6%98%8E%E4%B9%A6%E3%80%81%E5%95%86%E4%B8%9A%E5%B9%BF%E5%91%8A%E7%AD%89%E5%9D%87%E4%B8%BA%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E9%82%80%E8%AF%B7%E3%80%82%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E4%BD%86%E5%95%86%E4%B8%9A%E5%B9%BF%E5%91%8A%E7%9A%84%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E7%AC%A6%E5%90%88%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84,%E8%A7%86%E4%B8%BA%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="承诺" _mubu_text="%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA">
		<outline text="承诺的概念" _mubu_text="%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="承诺是受要约人向要约人作出的同意要约的意思表示。" _mubu_text="%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E6%98%AF%E5%8F%97%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E5%90%91%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%90%8C%E6%84%8F%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="承诺的条件包括:" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E5%8C%85%E6%8B%AC:%3C/span%3E" _note="@简答题&nbsp;@题眼&nbsp;@口诀&nbsp;承诺本期一名" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E9%A2%98%E7%9C%BC%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E6%9C%AC%E6%9C%9F%E4%B8%80%E5%90%8D" _heading="1" _color="#dc2d1e">
		<outline text="承诺的概念" _mubu_text="%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="承诺是受要约人向要约人作出的同意要约的意思表示。" _mubu_text="%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E6%98%AF%E5%8F%97%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E5%90%91%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%90%8C%E6%84%8F%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(1)承诺必须是由受要约人本人或其代理人向要约人作出。" _mubu_text="(1)%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E5%BF%85%E9%A1%BB%E6%98%AF%E7%94%B1%E5%8F%97%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E6%9C%AC%E4%BA%BA%E6%88%96%E5%85%B6%E4%BB%A3%E7%90%86%E4%BA%BA%E5%90%91%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="(2)承诺必须在要约确定的期限内到达要约人。" _mubu_text="(2)%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E5%BF%85%E9%A1%BB%E5%9C%A8%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E6%9C%9F%E9%99%90%E5%86%85%E5%88%B0%E8%BE%BE%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="要约没有确定承诺期限的，若要约是以对话方式作出的，除当事人另有约定外，受要约人应当即时作出承诺；若要约是以非对话方式作出的，承诺应当在合理期限内到达。" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E6%B2%A1%E6%9C%89%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E6%9C%9F%E9%99%90%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E8%8B%A5%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E6%98%AF%E4%BB%A5%E5%AF%B9%E8%AF%9D%E6%96%B9%E5%BC%8F%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E9%99%A4%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%A6%E6%9C%89%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E5%A4%96%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%97%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E5%8D%B3%E6%97%B6%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%EF%BC%9B%E8%8B%A5%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E6%98%AF%E4%BB%A5%E9%9D%9E%E5%AF%B9%E8%AF%9D%E6%96%B9%E5%BC%8F%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E5%9C%A8%E5%90%88%E7%90%86%E6%9C%9F%E9%99%90%E5%86%85%E5%88%B0%E8%BE%BE%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(3)承诺的内容应当与要约的内容一致。" _mubu_text="(3)%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E4%B8%8E%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E4%B8%80%E8%87%B4%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="受要约人对要约的内容作出实质性变更的，为新要约；" _mubu_text="%E5%8F%97%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E5%AF%B9%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E5%AE%9E%E8%B4%A8%E6%80%A7%E5%8F%98%E6%9B%B4%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%BA%E6%96%B0%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%EF%BC%9B">
		<outline text="有关合同标的、数量、质量、价款或者报酬、履行期限、履行地点和方式、违约责任和解决争议方法等的变更，是对要约内容的实质性变更。" _mubu_text="%E6%9C%89%E5%85%B3%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E3%80%81%E6%95%B0%E9%87%8F%E3%80%81%E8%B4%A8%E9%87%8F%E3%80%81%E4%BB%B7%E6%AC%BE%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E6%8A%A5%E9%85%AC%E3%80%81%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%9C%9F%E9%99%90%E3%80%81%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E5%9C%B0%E7%82%B9%E5%92%8C%E6%96%B9%E5%BC%8F%E3%80%81%E8%BF%9D%E7%BA%A6%E8%B4%A3%E4%BB%BB%E5%92%8C%E8%A7%A3%E5%86%B3%E4%BA%89%E8%AE%AE%E6%96%B9%E6%B3%95%E7%AD%89%E7%9A%84%E5%8F%98%E6%9B%B4%EF%BC%8C%E6%98%AF%E5%AF%B9%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E7%9A%84%E5%AE%9E%E8%B4%A8%E6%80%A7%E5%8F%98%E6%9B%B4%E3%80%82" _note="@考点" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E8%80%83%E7%82%B9%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="作出非实质性变更的，除要约人及时表示反对或者要约表明承诺不得对要约的内容作出任何变更的以外，该承诺有效。" _mubu_text="%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E9%9D%9E%E5%AE%9E%E8%B4%A8%E6%80%A7%E5%8F%98%E6%9B%B4%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E9%99%A4%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%8A%E6%97%B6%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E5%8F%8D%E5%AF%B9%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E8%A1%A8%E6%98%8E%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E4%B8%8D%E5%BE%97%E5%AF%B9%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E4%BB%BB%E4%BD%95%E5%8F%98%E6%9B%B4%E7%9A%84%E4%BB%A5%E5%A4%96%EF%BC%8C%E8%AF%A5%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E6%9C%89%E6%95%88%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(4) 承诺原则上应以明示方式作出，特殊情况下依交易习惯或者要约的规定也可以行为作出。但除法律有特别规定或当事人事先有明确约定外，沉默不能视为承诺的形式。" _mubu_text="(4)%20%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99%E4%B8%8A%E5%BA%94%E4%BB%A5%E6%98%8E%E7%A4%BA%E6%96%B9%E5%BC%8F%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%EF%BC%8C%E7%89%B9%E6%AE%8A%E6%83%85%E5%86%B5%E4%B8%8B%E4%BE%9D%E4%BA%A4%E6%98%93%E4%B9%A0%E6%83%AF%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E4%B9%9F%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E3%80%82%E4%BD%86%E9%99%A4%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E6%9C%89%E7%89%B9%E5%88%AB%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E6%88%96%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%BA%8B%E5%85%88%E6%9C%89%E6%98%8E%E7%A1%AE%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E5%A4%96%EF%BC%8C%E6%B2%89%E9%BB%98%E4%B8%8D%E8%83%BD%E8%A7%86%E4%B8%BA%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%BD%A2%E5%BC%8F%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="承诺的效力" _mubu_text="%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B">
		<outline text="承诺的效力在于承诺生效意味着合同成立，双方当事人由此承担合同产生的权利与义务。" _mubu_text="%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%E5%9C%A8%E4%BA%8E%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E6%84%8F%E5%91%B3%E7%9D%80%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%8C%E6%96%B9%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E7%94%B1%E6%AD%A4%E6%89%BF%E6%8B%85%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E4%BA%A7%E7%94%9F%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E4%B8%8E%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="承诺生效的时间" _mubu_text="%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E7%9A%84%E6%97%B6%E9%97%B4">
		<outline text="我国合同法采取“到达主义&quot;，规定承诺在承诺通知到达要约人时生效。" _mubu_text="%E6%88%91%E5%9B%BD%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%B3%95%E9%87%87%E5%8F%96%E2%80%9C%E5%88%B0%E8%BE%BE%E4%B8%BB%E4%B9%89%22%EF%BC%8C%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E5%9C%A8%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E9%80%9A%E7%9F%A5%E5%88%B0%E8%BE%BE%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E6%97%B6%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E3%80%82" _note="@考点" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E8%80%83%E7%82%B9%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		<outline text="承诺不需要通知的，根据交易习惯或者要约的要求作出承诺的行为时生效。" _mubu_text="%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E4%B8%8D%E9%9C%80%E8%A6%81%E9%80%9A%E7%9F%A5%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE%E4%BA%A4%E6%98%93%E4%B9%A0%E6%83%AF%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E8%A6%81%E6%B1%82%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E7%9A%84%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E6%97%B6%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E3%80%82" _note="@考点" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E8%80%83%E7%82%B9%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="承诺的撤回" _mubu_text="%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%92%A4%E5%9B%9E">
		<outline text="承诺可以撤回，撤回承诺的通知应当在承诺通知到达要约人之前或与承诺通知同时到达要约人。" _mubu_text="%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E6%92%A4%E5%9B%9E%EF%BC%8C%E6%92%A4%E5%9B%9E%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E7%9A%84%E9%80%9A%E7%9F%A5%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E5%9C%A8%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E9%80%9A%E7%9F%A5%E5%88%B0%E8%BE%BE%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E4%B9%8B%E5%89%8D%E6%88%96%E4%B8%8E%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E9%80%9A%E7%9F%A5%E5%90%8C%E6%97%B6%E5%88%B0%E8%BE%BE%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="合同成立的一般程序的举例" _mubu_text="%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%80%E8%88%AC%E7%A8%8B%E5%BA%8F%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%BE%E4%BE%8B">
		<outline text="以拍卖为例" _mubu_text="%E4%BB%A5%E6%8B%8D%E5%8D%96%E4%B8%BA%E4%BE%8B">
		<outline text="以拍卖方式订立合同的，拍卖公告属于要约邀请，竟买人的应价(或称报价)行为构成要约，拍卖人的买定表示构成承诺。" _mubu_text="%E4%BB%A5%E6%8B%8D%E5%8D%96%E6%96%B9%E5%BC%8F%E8%AE%A2%E7%AB%8B%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E6%8B%8D%E5%8D%96%E5%85%AC%E5%91%8A%E5%B1%9E%E4%BA%8E%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E9%82%80%E8%AF%B7%EF%BC%8C%E7%AB%9F%E4%B9%B0%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%BA%94%E4%BB%B7(%E6%88%96%E7%A7%B0%E6%8A%A5%E4%BB%B7)%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E6%9E%84%E6%88%90%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%8B%8D%E5%8D%96%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E4%B9%B0%E5%AE%9A%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E6%9E%84%E6%88%90%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%3C/span%3E%E3%80%82" _note="@考点" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E8%80%83%E7%82%B9%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		<outline text="在竞买人的最高应价经拍卖师落槌或者以其他公开表示买定的方式确认后，合同成立。其后,买受人和拍卖人应当签署成交确认书。" _mubu_text="%E5%9C%A8%E7%AB%9E%E4%B9%B0%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%9C%80%E9%AB%98%E5%BA%94%E4%BB%B7%E7%BB%8F%E6%8B%8D%E5%8D%96%E5%B8%88%E8%90%BD%E6%A7%8C%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E4%BB%A5%E5%85%B6%E4%BB%96%E5%85%AC%E5%BC%80%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E4%B9%B0%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E6%96%B9%E5%BC%8F%E7%A1%AE%E8%AE%A4%E5%90%8E%EF%BC%8C%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E3%80%82%E5%85%B6%E5%90%8E,%E4%B9%B0%E5%8F%97%E4%BA%BA%E5%92%8C%E6%8B%8D%E5%8D%96%E4%BA%BA%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E7%AD%BE%E7%BD%B2%E6%88%90%E4%BA%A4%E7%A1%AE%E8%AE%A4%E4%B9%A6%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="以招标为例" _mubu_text="%E4%BB%A5%E6%8B%9B%E6%A0%87%E4%B8%BA%E4%BE%8B">
		<outline text="以招标投标方式订立合同的，招标为要约邀请，投标为要约，定标为承诺。" _mubu_text="%E4%BB%A5%E6%8B%9B%E6%A0%87%E6%8A%95%E6%A0%87%E6%96%B9%E5%BC%8F%E8%AE%A2%E7%AB%8B%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E6%8B%9B%E6%A0%87%E4%B8%BA%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E9%82%80%E8%AF%B7%EF%BC%8C%E6%8A%95%E6%A0%87%E4%B8%BA%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%EF%BC%8C%E5%AE%9A%E6%A0%87%E4%B8%BA%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E3%80%82" _note="@考点" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E8%80%83%E7%82%B9%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		<outline text="定标后，招标人应当向中标人发出中标通知书，中标通知书对招标人和中标人具有法律效力，双方应当自中标通知书发出之日起30日内订立书面合同。" _mubu_text="%E5%AE%9A%E6%A0%87%E5%90%8E%EF%BC%8C%E6%8B%9B%E6%A0%87%E4%BA%BA%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E5%90%91%E4%B8%AD%E6%A0%87%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%91%E5%87%BA%E4%B8%AD%E6%A0%87%E9%80%9A%E7%9F%A5%E4%B9%A6%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%AD%E6%A0%87%E9%80%9A%E7%9F%A5%E4%B9%A6%E5%AF%B9%E6%8B%9B%E6%A0%87%E4%BA%BA%E5%92%8C%E4%B8%AD%E6%A0%87%E4%BA%BA%E5%85%B7%E6%9C%89%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%8C%E6%96%B9%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E8%87%AA%E4%B8%AD%E6%A0%87%E9%80%9A%E7%9F%A5%E4%B9%A6%E5%8F%91%E5%87%BA%E4%B9%8B%E6%97%A5%E8%B5%B730%E6%97%A5%E5%86%85%E8%AE%A2%E7%AB%8B%E4%B9%A6%E9%9D%A2%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="333.简述要约，承诺的概念、条件、法律效力" _mubu_text="333.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%EF%BC%8C%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5%E3%80%81%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E3%80%81%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B">
		<outline text="要约" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6">
		<outline text="要约的概念" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="要约是当事人一方向对方发出的希望与对方订立合同的意思表示。" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E6%98%AF%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E5%90%91%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E5%8F%91%E5%87%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%B8%8C%E6%9C%9B%E4%B8%8E%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E8%AE%A2%E7%AB%8B%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="要约的条件" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%3C/span%3E" _note="@简答题&nbsp;@题眼&nbsp;@口诀&nbsp;要约条件特目内承" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E9%A2%98%E7%9C%BC%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E7%89%B9%E7%9B%AE%E5%86%85%E6%89%BF" _heading="1" _color="#dc2d1e">
		<outline text="要约的概念" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="要约是当事人一方向对方发出的希望与对方订立合同的意思表示。" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E6%98%AF%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E5%90%91%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E5%8F%91%E5%87%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%B8%8C%E6%9C%9B%E4%B8%8E%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E8%AE%A2%E7%AB%8B%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(1)要约必须是特定人向相对人发出的意思表示。" _mubu_text="(1)%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E5%BF%85%E9%A1%BB%E6%98%AF%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E4%BA%BA%E5%90%91%E7%9B%B8%E5%AF%B9%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%91%E5%87%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="换言之，要约人必须是在客观上可以确定的人；而要约的相对人则既可以是特定的某个人，也可以是不特定的社会公众。如商店的商品标价陈列，可以看作向不特定的人发出的要约。" _mubu_text="%E6%8D%A2%E8%A8%80%E4%B9%8B%EF%BC%8C%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E5%BF%85%E9%A1%BB%E6%98%AF%E5%9C%A8%E5%AE%A2%E8%A7%82%E4%B8%8A%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E4%BA%BA%EF%BC%9B%E8%80%8C%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E7%9B%B8%E5%AF%B9%E4%BA%BA%E5%88%99%E6%97%A2%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E6%98%AF%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E6%9F%90%E4%B8%AA%E4%BA%BA%EF%BC%8C%E4%B9%9F%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E6%98%AF%E4%B8%8D%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E7%A4%BE%E4%BC%9A%E5%85%AC%E4%BC%97%E3%80%82%E5%A6%82%E5%95%86%E5%BA%97%E7%9A%84%E5%95%86%E5%93%81%E6%A0%87%E4%BB%B7%E9%99%88%E5%88%97%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E7%9C%8B%E4%BD%9C%E5%90%91%E4%B8%8D%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%91%E5%87%BA%E7%9A%84%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(2)要约必须以缔结合同为目的。" _mubu_text="(2)%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E5%BF%85%E9%A1%BB%E4%BB%A5%E7%BC%94%E7%BB%93%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E4%B8%BA%E7%9B%AE%E7%9A%84%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="非以缔结合同为目的的表示不属于要约。" _mubu_text="%E9%9D%9E%E4%BB%A5%E7%BC%94%E7%BB%93%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E4%B8%BA%E7%9B%AE%E7%9A%84%E7%9A%84%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E4%B8%8D%E5%B1%9E%E4%BA%8E%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(3)要约的内容应具体确定。" _mubu_text="(3)%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E5%BA%94%E5%85%B7%E4%BD%93%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="要约一经相对人承诺即导致合同成立。因此，要约的内容必须具体确定，至少应包括拟订立合同的必备条款，以供相对人考虑是否承诺。" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%B8%80%E7%BB%8F%E7%9B%B8%E5%AF%B9%E4%BA%BA%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E5%8D%B3%E5%AF%BC%E8%87%B4%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E3%80%82%E5%9B%A0%E6%AD%A4%EF%BC%8C%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E5%BF%85%E9%A1%BB%E5%85%B7%E4%BD%93%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E8%87%B3%E5%B0%91%E5%BA%94%E5%8C%85%E6%8B%AC%E6%8B%9F%E8%AE%A2%E7%AB%8B%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E5%BF%85%E5%A4%87%E6%9D%A1%E6%AC%BE%EF%BC%8C%E4%BB%A5%E4%BE%9B%E7%9B%B8%E5%AF%B9%E4%BA%BA%E8%80%83%E8%99%91%E6%98%AF%E5%90%A6%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(4)要约必须表明经受要约人承诺，要约人即受该意思表示约束。" _mubu_text="(4)%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E5%BF%85%E9%A1%BB%E8%A1%A8%E6%98%8E%E7%BB%8F%E5%8F%97%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%EF%BC%8C%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E5%8D%B3%E5%8F%97%E8%AF%A5%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E7%BA%A6%E6%9D%9F%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="要约的法律效力。" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="（1）要约生效后，要约人应受要约的约束，在要约有效期内不得随意撤销或变更要约；（针对要约人的效力）" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E5%90%8E%EF%BC%8C%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E5%BA%94%E5%8F%97%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E7%BA%A6%E6%9D%9F%EF%BC%8C%E5%9C%A8%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E6%9C%89%E6%95%88%E6%9C%9F%E5%86%85%E4%B8%8D%E5%BE%97%E9%9A%8F%E6%84%8F%E6%92%A4%E9%94%80%E6%88%96%E5%8F%98%E6%9B%B4%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%EF%BC%9B%EF%BC%88%E9%92%88%E5%AF%B9%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%EF%BC%89">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（2）受要约人则取得了承诺的权利，受要约人有权在要约的有效期限内作出接受要约的答复，而不负必须承诺的义务。即使受要约人不承诺，也没有通知要约人的义务。（针对受要约人的效力）" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%E5%8F%97%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E5%88%99%E5%8F%96%E5%BE%97%E4%BA%86%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%97%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E6%9C%89%E6%9D%83%E5%9C%A8%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E6%9C%89%E6%95%88%E6%9C%9F%E9%99%90%E5%86%85%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E6%8E%A5%E5%8F%97%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E7%AD%94%E5%A4%8D%EF%BC%8C%E8%80%8C%E4%B8%8D%E8%B4%9F%E5%BF%85%E9%A1%BB%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E7%9A%84%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E3%80%82%E5%8D%B3%E4%BD%BF%E5%8F%97%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%8D%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%EF%BC%8C%E4%B9%9F%E6%B2%A1%E6%9C%89%E9%80%9A%E7%9F%A5%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E3%80%82%EF%BC%88%E9%92%88%E5%AF%B9%E5%8F%97%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%EF%BC%89">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（3）要约的生效时间因要约形式的不同而有所不同。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E6%97%B6%E9%97%B4%E5%9B%A0%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E5%BD%A2%E5%BC%8F%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%8D%E5%90%8C%E8%80%8C%E6%9C%89%E6%89%80%E4%B8%8D%E5%90%8C%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="一般来说，口头要约自受要约人了解时生效，书面要约自要约到达受要约人时生效。在要约生效前，要约人可以撤回要约；要约生效后，在符合法定条件时，要约人可以撤销要约。" _mubu_text="%E4%B8%80%E8%88%AC%E6%9D%A5%E8%AF%B4%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%A3%E5%A4%B4%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E8%87%AA%E5%8F%97%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E4%BA%86%E8%A7%A3%E6%97%B6%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%EF%BC%8C%E4%B9%A6%E9%9D%A2%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E8%87%AA%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E5%88%B0%E8%BE%BE%E5%8F%97%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E6%97%B6%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E3%80%82%E5%9C%A8%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E5%89%8D%EF%BC%8C%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E6%92%A4%E5%9B%9E%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%EF%BC%9B%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E5%90%8E%EF%BC%8C%E5%9C%A8%E7%AC%A6%E5%90%88%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E6%97%B6%EF%BC%8C%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E6%92%A4%E9%94%80%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="要约与要约邀请的相同之处是:" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%B8%8E%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E9%82%80%E8%AF%B7%E7%9A%84%E7%9B%B8%E5%90%8C%E4%B9%8B%E5%A4%84%E6%98%AF:%3C/span%3E" _note="@口诀&nbsp;姚姚同特意&nbsp;@简答题" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E5%A7%9A%E5%A7%9A%E5%90%8C%E7%89%B9%E6%84%8F&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E" _heading="1" _color="#3da8f5">
		<outline text="要约邀请的概念" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E9%82%80%E8%AF%B7%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="要约邀请，是一方向他方作出的希望他方向自己发出要约的意思表示。" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E9%82%80%E8%AF%B7%EF%BC%8C%E6%98%AF%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E5%90%91%E4%BB%96%E6%96%B9%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%B8%8C%E6%9C%9B%E4%BB%96%E6%96%B9%E5%90%91%E8%87%AA%E5%B7%B1%E5%8F%91%E5%87%BA%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="要约的概念" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="要约是当事人一方向对方发出的希望与对方订立合同的意思表示。" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E6%98%AF%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E5%90%91%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E5%8F%91%E5%87%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%B8%8C%E6%9C%9B%E4%B8%8E%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E8%AE%A2%E7%AB%8B%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(1)由特定人向特定人或不特定人发出。" _mubu_text="(1)%E7%94%B1%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E4%BA%BA%E5%90%91%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E4%BA%BA%E6%88%96%E4%B8%8D%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%91%E5%87%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="(2)均属于意思表示，故应具备意思表示的成立要件。" _mubu_text="(2)%E5%9D%87%E5%B1%9E%E4%BA%8E%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%EF%BC%8C%E6%95%85%E5%BA%94%E5%85%B7%E5%A4%87%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="要约与要约邀的请区别是:" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%B8%8E%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E9%82%80%E7%9A%84%E8%AF%B7%E5%8C%BA%E5%88%AB%E6%98%AF:">
		<outline text="(1)目的不同。" _mubu_text="(1)%E7%9B%AE%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%8D%E5%90%8C%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="要约的目的在于获得对方的承诺以成立合同；" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E7%9B%AE%E7%9A%84%E5%9C%A8%E4%BA%8E%E8%8E%B7%E5%BE%97%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E7%9A%84%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E4%BB%A5%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%EF%BC%9B">
		</outline>
		<outline text="要约邀请的目的在于引出对方的要约。" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E9%82%80%E8%AF%B7%E7%9A%84%E7%9B%AE%E7%9A%84%E5%9C%A8%E4%BA%8E%E5%BC%95%E5%87%BA%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E7%9A%84%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(2)条件不同。" _mubu_text="(2)%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E4%B8%8D%E5%90%8C%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="要约的条件如前所述；" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E5%A6%82%E5%89%8D%E6%89%80%E8%BF%B0%EF%BC%9B">
		</outline>
		<outline text="要约邀请无须具备前述条件，如无须内容具体确定只要邀请人足以确定即可。" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E9%82%80%E8%AF%B7%E6%97%A0%E9%A1%BB%E5%85%B7%E5%A4%87%E5%89%8D%E8%BF%B0%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%EF%BC%8C%E5%A6%82%E6%97%A0%E9%A1%BB%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E5%85%B7%E4%BD%93%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%E5%8F%AA%E8%A6%81%E9%82%80%E8%AF%B7%E4%BA%BA%E8%B6%B3%E4%BB%A5%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%E5%8D%B3%E5%8F%AF%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(3)效力不同。" _mubu_text="(3)%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%E4%B8%8D%E5%90%8C%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="要约人须受要约约束；" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E9%A1%BB%E5%8F%97%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%BA%A6%E6%9D%9F%EF%BC%9B">
		</outline>
		<outline text="要约邀请本身没有法律效力，故邀请人不受要约邀请的约束。" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E9%82%80%E8%AF%B7%E6%9C%AC%E8%BA%AB%E6%B2%A1%E6%9C%89%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%EF%BC%8C%E6%95%85%E9%82%80%E8%AF%B7%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%8D%E5%8F%97%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E9%82%80%E8%AF%B7%E7%9A%84%E7%BA%A6%E6%9D%9F%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="一般来讲，寄送的价目表、拍卖公告、招标公告、招股说明书、商业广告等均为要约邀请。但商业广告的内容符合要约规定的,视为要约。" _mubu_text="%E4%B8%80%E8%88%AC%E6%9D%A5%E8%AE%B2%EF%BC%8C%E5%AF%84%E9%80%81%E7%9A%84%E4%BB%B7%E7%9B%AE%E8%A1%A8%E3%80%81%E6%8B%8D%E5%8D%96%E5%85%AC%E5%91%8A%E3%80%81%E6%8B%9B%E6%A0%87%E5%85%AC%E5%91%8A%E3%80%81%E6%8B%9B%E8%82%A1%E8%AF%B4%E6%98%8E%E4%B9%A6%E3%80%81%E5%95%86%E4%B8%9A%E5%B9%BF%E5%91%8A%E7%AD%89%E5%9D%87%E4%B8%BA%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E9%82%80%E8%AF%B7%E3%80%82%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E4%BD%86%E5%95%86%E4%B8%9A%E5%B9%BF%E5%91%8A%E7%9A%84%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E7%AC%A6%E5%90%88%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84,%E8%A7%86%E4%B8%BA%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="承诺" _mubu_text="%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA">
		<outline text="承诺的概念" _mubu_text="%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="承诺是受要约人向要约人作出的同意要约的意思表示。" _mubu_text="%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E6%98%AF%E5%8F%97%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E5%90%91%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%90%8C%E6%84%8F%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="承诺的条件包括:" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E5%8C%85%E6%8B%AC:%3C/span%3E" _note="@简答题&nbsp;@题眼&nbsp;@口诀&nbsp;承诺本期一名" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E9%A2%98%E7%9C%BC%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E6%9C%AC%E6%9C%9F%E4%B8%80%E5%90%8D" _heading="1" _color="#dc2d1e">
		<outline text="承诺的概念" _mubu_text="%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="承诺是受要约人向要约人作出的同意要约的意思表示。" _mubu_text="%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E6%98%AF%E5%8F%97%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E5%90%91%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%90%8C%E6%84%8F%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(1)承诺必须是由受要约人本人或其代理人向要约人作出。" _mubu_text="(1)%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E5%BF%85%E9%A1%BB%E6%98%AF%E7%94%B1%E5%8F%97%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E6%9C%AC%E4%BA%BA%E6%88%96%E5%85%B6%E4%BB%A3%E7%90%86%E4%BA%BA%E5%90%91%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="(2)承诺必须在要约确定的期限内到达要约人。" _mubu_text="(2)%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E5%BF%85%E9%A1%BB%E5%9C%A8%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E6%9C%9F%E9%99%90%E5%86%85%E5%88%B0%E8%BE%BE%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="要约没有确定承诺期限的，若要约是以对话方式作出的，除当事人另有约定外，受要约人应当即时作出承诺；若要约是以非对话方式作出的，承诺应当在合理期限内到达。" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E6%B2%A1%E6%9C%89%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E6%9C%9F%E9%99%90%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E8%8B%A5%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E6%98%AF%E4%BB%A5%E5%AF%B9%E8%AF%9D%E6%96%B9%E5%BC%8F%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E9%99%A4%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%A6%E6%9C%89%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E5%A4%96%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%97%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E5%8D%B3%E6%97%B6%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%EF%BC%9B%E8%8B%A5%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E6%98%AF%E4%BB%A5%E9%9D%9E%E5%AF%B9%E8%AF%9D%E6%96%B9%E5%BC%8F%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E5%9C%A8%E5%90%88%E7%90%86%E6%9C%9F%E9%99%90%E5%86%85%E5%88%B0%E8%BE%BE%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(3)承诺的内容应当与要约的内容一致。" _mubu_text="(3)%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E4%B8%8E%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E4%B8%80%E8%87%B4%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="受要约人对要约的内容作出实质性变更的，为新要约；" _mubu_text="%E5%8F%97%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E5%AF%B9%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E5%AE%9E%E8%B4%A8%E6%80%A7%E5%8F%98%E6%9B%B4%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%BA%E6%96%B0%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%EF%BC%9B">
		<outline text="有关合同标的、数量、质量、价款或者报酬、履行期限、履行地点和方式、违约责任和解决争议方法等的变更，是对要约内容的实质性变更。" _mubu_text="%E6%9C%89%E5%85%B3%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E3%80%81%E6%95%B0%E9%87%8F%E3%80%81%E8%B4%A8%E9%87%8F%E3%80%81%E4%BB%B7%E6%AC%BE%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E6%8A%A5%E9%85%AC%E3%80%81%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%9C%9F%E9%99%90%E3%80%81%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E5%9C%B0%E7%82%B9%E5%92%8C%E6%96%B9%E5%BC%8F%E3%80%81%E8%BF%9D%E7%BA%A6%E8%B4%A3%E4%BB%BB%E5%92%8C%E8%A7%A3%E5%86%B3%E4%BA%89%E8%AE%AE%E6%96%B9%E6%B3%95%E7%AD%89%E7%9A%84%E5%8F%98%E6%9B%B4%EF%BC%8C%E6%98%AF%E5%AF%B9%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E7%9A%84%E5%AE%9E%E8%B4%A8%E6%80%A7%E5%8F%98%E6%9B%B4%E3%80%82" _note="@考点" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E8%80%83%E7%82%B9%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="作出非实质性变更的，除要约人及时表示反对或者要约表明承诺不得对要约的内容作出任何变更的以外，该承诺有效。" _mubu_text="%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E9%9D%9E%E5%AE%9E%E8%B4%A8%E6%80%A7%E5%8F%98%E6%9B%B4%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E9%99%A4%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%8A%E6%97%B6%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E5%8F%8D%E5%AF%B9%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E8%A1%A8%E6%98%8E%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E4%B8%8D%E5%BE%97%E5%AF%B9%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E4%BB%BB%E4%BD%95%E5%8F%98%E6%9B%B4%E7%9A%84%E4%BB%A5%E5%A4%96%EF%BC%8C%E8%AF%A5%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E6%9C%89%E6%95%88%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(4) 承诺原则上应以明示方式作出，特殊情况下依交易习惯或者要约的规定也可以行为作出。但除法律有特别规定或当事人事先有明确约定外，沉默不能视为承诺的形式。" _mubu_text="(4)%20%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99%E4%B8%8A%E5%BA%94%E4%BB%A5%E6%98%8E%E7%A4%BA%E6%96%B9%E5%BC%8F%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%EF%BC%8C%E7%89%B9%E6%AE%8A%E6%83%85%E5%86%B5%E4%B8%8B%E4%BE%9D%E4%BA%A4%E6%98%93%E4%B9%A0%E6%83%AF%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E4%B9%9F%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E3%80%82%E4%BD%86%E9%99%A4%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E6%9C%89%E7%89%B9%E5%88%AB%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E6%88%96%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%BA%8B%E5%85%88%E6%9C%89%E6%98%8E%E7%A1%AE%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E5%A4%96%EF%BC%8C%E6%B2%89%E9%BB%98%E4%B8%8D%E8%83%BD%E8%A7%86%E4%B8%BA%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%BD%A2%E5%BC%8F%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="承诺的效力" _mubu_text="%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B">
		<outline text="承诺的效力在于承诺生效意味着合同成立，双方当事人由此承担合同产生的权利与义务。" _mubu_text="%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%E5%9C%A8%E4%BA%8E%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E6%84%8F%E5%91%B3%E7%9D%80%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%8C%E6%96%B9%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E7%94%B1%E6%AD%A4%E6%89%BF%E6%8B%85%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E4%BA%A7%E7%94%9F%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E4%B8%8E%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="承诺生效的时间" _mubu_text="%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E7%9A%84%E6%97%B6%E9%97%B4">
		<outline text="我国合同法采取“到达主义&quot;，规定承诺在承诺通知到达要约人时生效。" _mubu_text="%E6%88%91%E5%9B%BD%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%B3%95%E9%87%87%E5%8F%96%E2%80%9C%E5%88%B0%E8%BE%BE%E4%B8%BB%E4%B9%89%22%EF%BC%8C%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E5%9C%A8%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E9%80%9A%E7%9F%A5%E5%88%B0%E8%BE%BE%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E6%97%B6%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E3%80%82" _note="@考点" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E8%80%83%E7%82%B9%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		<outline text="承诺不需要通知的，根据交易习惯或者要约的要求作出承诺的行为时生效。" _mubu_text="%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E4%B8%8D%E9%9C%80%E8%A6%81%E9%80%9A%E7%9F%A5%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE%E4%BA%A4%E6%98%93%E4%B9%A0%E6%83%AF%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E8%A6%81%E6%B1%82%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E7%9A%84%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E6%97%B6%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E3%80%82" _note="@考点" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E8%80%83%E7%82%B9%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="承诺的撤回" _mubu_text="%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%92%A4%E5%9B%9E">
		<outline text="承诺可以撤回，撤回承诺的通知应当在承诺通知到达要约人之前或与承诺通知同时到达要约人。" _mubu_text="%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E6%92%A4%E5%9B%9E%EF%BC%8C%E6%92%A4%E5%9B%9E%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E7%9A%84%E9%80%9A%E7%9F%A5%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E5%9C%A8%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E9%80%9A%E7%9F%A5%E5%88%B0%E8%BE%BE%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E4%B9%8B%E5%89%8D%E6%88%96%E4%B8%8E%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E9%80%9A%E7%9F%A5%E5%90%8C%E6%97%B6%E5%88%B0%E8%BE%BE%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="334.简述要约与要约邀请的区别" _mubu_text="334.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%B8%8E%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E9%82%80%E8%AF%B7%E7%9A%84%E5%8C%BA%E5%88%AB">
		<outline text="要约与要约邀请的相同之处是:" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%B8%8E%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E9%82%80%E8%AF%B7%E7%9A%84%E7%9B%B8%E5%90%8C%E4%B9%8B%E5%A4%84%E6%98%AF:%3C/span%3E" _note="@口诀&nbsp;姚姚同特意&nbsp;@简答题" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E5%A7%9A%E5%A7%9A%E5%90%8C%E7%89%B9%E6%84%8F&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E" _heading="1" _color="#3da8f5">
		<outline text="要约邀请的概念" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E9%82%80%E8%AF%B7%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="要约邀请，是一方向他方作出的希望他方向自己发出要约的意思表示。" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E9%82%80%E8%AF%B7%EF%BC%8C%E6%98%AF%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E5%90%91%E4%BB%96%E6%96%B9%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%B8%8C%E6%9C%9B%E4%BB%96%E6%96%B9%E5%90%91%E8%87%AA%E5%B7%B1%E5%8F%91%E5%87%BA%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="要约的概念" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="要约是当事人一方向对方发出的希望与对方订立合同的意思表示。" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E6%98%AF%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E5%90%91%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E5%8F%91%E5%87%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%B8%8C%E6%9C%9B%E4%B8%8E%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E8%AE%A2%E7%AB%8B%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(1)由特定人向特定人或不特定人发出。" _mubu_text="(1)%E7%94%B1%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E4%BA%BA%E5%90%91%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E4%BA%BA%E6%88%96%E4%B8%8D%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%91%E5%87%BA%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="(2)均属于意思表示，故应具备意思表示的成立要件。" _mubu_text="(2)%E5%9D%87%E5%B1%9E%E4%BA%8E%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%EF%BC%8C%E6%95%85%E5%BA%94%E5%85%B7%E5%A4%87%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="要约与要约邀的请区别是:" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%B8%8E%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E9%82%80%E7%9A%84%E8%AF%B7%E5%8C%BA%E5%88%AB%E6%98%AF:">
		<outline text="(1)目的不同。" _mubu_text="(1)%E7%9B%AE%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%8D%E5%90%8C%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="要约的目的在于获得对方的承诺以成立合同；" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E7%9B%AE%E7%9A%84%E5%9C%A8%E4%BA%8E%E8%8E%B7%E5%BE%97%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E7%9A%84%E6%89%BF%E8%AF%BA%E4%BB%A5%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%EF%BC%9B">
		</outline>
		<outline text="要约邀请的目的在于引出对方的要约。" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E9%82%80%E8%AF%B7%E7%9A%84%E7%9B%AE%E7%9A%84%E5%9C%A8%E4%BA%8E%E5%BC%95%E5%87%BA%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E7%9A%84%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(2)条件不同。" _mubu_text="(2)%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E4%B8%8D%E5%90%8C%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="要约的条件如前所述；" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E5%A6%82%E5%89%8D%E6%89%80%E8%BF%B0%EF%BC%9B">
		</outline>
		<outline text="要约邀请无须具备前述条件，如无须内容具体确定只要邀请人足以确定即可。" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E9%82%80%E8%AF%B7%E6%97%A0%E9%A1%BB%E5%85%B7%E5%A4%87%E5%89%8D%E8%BF%B0%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%EF%BC%8C%E5%A6%82%E6%97%A0%E9%A1%BB%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E5%85%B7%E4%BD%93%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%E5%8F%AA%E8%A6%81%E9%82%80%E8%AF%B7%E4%BA%BA%E8%B6%B3%E4%BB%A5%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%E5%8D%B3%E5%8F%AF%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(3)效力不同。" _mubu_text="(3)%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%E4%B8%8D%E5%90%8C%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="要约人须受要约约束；" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E4%BA%BA%E9%A1%BB%E5%8F%97%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E7%BA%A6%E6%9D%9F%EF%BC%9B">
		</outline>
		<outline text="要约邀请本身没有法律效力，故邀请人不受要约邀请的约束。" _mubu_text="%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E9%82%80%E8%AF%B7%E6%9C%AC%E8%BA%AB%E6%B2%A1%E6%9C%89%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%EF%BC%8C%E6%95%85%E9%82%80%E8%AF%B7%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%8D%E5%8F%97%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E9%82%80%E8%AF%B7%E7%9A%84%E7%BA%A6%E6%9D%9F%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="一般来讲，寄送的价目表、拍卖公告、招标公告、招股说明书、商业广告等均为要约邀请。但商业广告的内容符合要约规定的,视为要约。" _mubu_text="%E4%B8%80%E8%88%AC%E6%9D%A5%E8%AE%B2%EF%BC%8C%E5%AF%84%E9%80%81%E7%9A%84%E4%BB%B7%E7%9B%AE%E8%A1%A8%E3%80%81%E6%8B%8D%E5%8D%96%E5%85%AC%E5%91%8A%E3%80%81%E6%8B%9B%E6%A0%87%E5%85%AC%E5%91%8A%E3%80%81%E6%8B%9B%E8%82%A1%E8%AF%B4%E6%98%8E%E4%B9%A6%E3%80%81%E5%95%86%E4%B8%9A%E5%B9%BF%E5%91%8A%E7%AD%89%E5%9D%87%E4%B8%BA%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E9%82%80%E8%AF%B7%E3%80%82%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E4%BD%86%E5%95%86%E4%B8%9A%E5%B9%BF%E5%91%8A%E7%9A%84%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E7%AC%A6%E5%90%88%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84,%E8%A7%86%E4%B8%BA%E8%A6%81%E7%BA%A6%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="335.简述格式条款的特殊要求" _mubu_text="335.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E6%A0%BC%E5%BC%8F%E6%9D%A1%E6%AC%BE%E7%9A%84%E7%89%B9%E6%AE%8A%E8%A6%81%E6%B1%82">
		<outline text="格式条款的概念" _mubu_text="%E6%A0%BC%E5%BC%8F%E6%9D%A1%E6%AC%BE%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="格式条款，是指当事人为了重复使用而预先拟订，并在订立合同时未与对方协商的条款。" _mubu_text="%E6%A0%BC%E5%BC%8F%E6%9D%A1%E6%AC%BE%EF%BC%8C%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%BA%E4%BA%86%E9%87%8D%E5%A4%8D%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8%E8%80%8C%E9%A2%84%E5%85%88%E6%8B%9F%E8%AE%A2%EF%BC%8C%E5%B9%B6%E5%9C%A8%E8%AE%A2%E7%AB%8B%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%97%B6%E6%9C%AA%E4%B8%8E%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E5%8D%8F%E5%95%86%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%A1%E6%AC%BE%E3%80%82" _note="@必须掌握的概念" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%BF%85%E9%A1%BB%E6%8E%8C%E6%8F%A1%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="我国合同法对格式条款的特殊要求体现在:" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%88%91%E5%9B%BD%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%B3%95%E5%AF%B9%E6%A0%BC%E5%BC%8F%E6%9D%A1%E6%AC%BE%E7%9A%84%E7%89%B9%E6%AE%8A%E8%A6%81%E6%B1%82%E4%BD%93%E7%8E%B0%E5%9C%A8:%3C/span%3E" _note="@简答题&nbsp;@题眼&nbsp;@口诀&nbsp;格式要求供体吴小姐试飞" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E9%A2%98%E7%9C%BC%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E6%A0%BC%E5%BC%8F%E8%A6%81%E6%B1%82%E4%BE%9B%E4%BD%93%E5%90%B4%E5%B0%8F%E5%A7%90%E8%AF%95%E9%A3%9E" _heading="1" _color="#dc2d1e">
		<outline text="（1）提供格式条款的一方应当遵循公平原则确定当事人之间的权利和义务，并采取合理的方式如采用足以引起对方注意的文字、符号、字体等特别标识提请对方注意免除或者限制其责任的条款，按照对方的要求，对该条款予以说明。否则，对方当事人有权申请撤销该格式条款。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E6%8F%90%E4%BE%9B%E6%A0%BC%E5%BC%8F%E6%9D%A1%E6%AC%BE%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E9%81%B5%E5%BE%AA%E5%85%AC%E5%B9%B3%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%B9%8B%E9%97%B4%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E5%92%8C%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%EF%BC%8C%E5%B9%B6%E9%87%87%E5%8F%96%E5%90%88%E7%90%86%E7%9A%84%E6%96%B9%E5%BC%8F%E5%A6%82%E9%87%87%E7%94%A8%E8%B6%B3%E4%BB%A5%E5%BC%95%E8%B5%B7%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E6%B3%A8%E6%84%8F%E7%9A%84%E6%96%87%E5%AD%97%E3%80%81%E7%AC%A6%E5%8F%B7%E3%80%81%E5%AD%97%E4%BD%93%E7%AD%89%E7%89%B9%E5%88%AB%E6%A0%87%E8%AF%86%E6%8F%90%E8%AF%B7%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E6%B3%A8%E6%84%8F%E5%85%8D%E9%99%A4%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E9%99%90%E5%88%B6%E5%85%B6%E8%B4%A3%E4%BB%BB%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%A1%E6%AC%BE%EF%BC%8C%E6%8C%89%E7%85%A7%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E7%9A%84%E8%A6%81%E6%B1%82%EF%BC%8C%E5%AF%B9%E8%AF%A5%E6%9D%A1%E6%AC%BE%E4%BA%88%E4%BB%A5%E8%AF%B4%E6%98%8E%E3%80%82%E5%90%A6%E5%88%99%EF%BC%8C%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E6%9C%89%E6%9D%83%E7%94%B3%E8%AF%B7%E6%92%A4%E9%94%80%E8%AF%A5%E6%A0%BC%E5%BC%8F%E6%9D%A1%E6%AC%BE%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（2）提供格式条款的一方未尽公平拟约或者提示和说明义务，同时又有下列情形之一的，格式条款无效：" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%E6%8F%90%E4%BE%9B%E6%A0%BC%E5%BC%8F%E6%9D%A1%E6%AC%BE%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E6%9C%AA%E5%B0%BD%E5%85%AC%E5%B9%B3%E6%8B%9F%E7%BA%A6%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E6%8F%90%E7%A4%BA%E5%92%8C%E8%AF%B4%E6%98%8E%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%EF%BC%8C%E5%90%8C%E6%97%B6%E5%8F%88%E6%9C%89%E4%B8%8B%E5%88%97%E6%83%85%E5%BD%A2%E4%B9%8B%E4%B8%80%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E6%A0%BC%E5%BC%8F%E6%9D%A1%E6%AC%BE%E6%97%A0%E6%95%88%EF%BC%9A">
		<outline text="①一是格式条款中有合同无效事由。" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E2%91%A0%E4%B8%80%E6%98%AF%E6%A0%BC%E5%BC%8F%E6%9D%A1%E6%AC%BE%E4%B8%AD%E6%9C%89%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%97%A0%E6%95%88%E4%BA%8B%E7%94%B1%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E" _heading="3" _color="#dc2d1e">
		</outline>
		<outline text="②二是提供格式条款一方免除其责任、加重对方责任、排除对方主要权利的。" _mubu_text="%E2%91%A1%E4%BA%8C%E6%98%AF%E6%8F%90%E4%BE%9B%E6%A0%BC%E5%BC%8F%E6%9D%A1%E6%AC%BE%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E5%85%8D%E9%99%A4%E5%85%B6%E8%B4%A3%E4%BB%BB%E3%80%81%E5%8A%A0%E9%87%8D%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E8%B4%A3%E4%BB%BB%E3%80%81%E6%8E%92%E9%99%A4%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E4%B8%BB%E8%A6%81%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E7%9A%84%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="③三是格式条款中的造成对方人身损害的、因故意或者重大过失造成对方财产损失的免责条款无效。" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E2%91%A2%E4%B8%89%E6%98%AF%E6%A0%BC%E5%BC%8F%E6%9D%A1%E6%AC%BE%E4%B8%AD%E7%9A%84%E9%80%A0%E6%88%90%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E4%BA%BA%E8%BA%AB%E6%8D%9F%E5%AE%B3%E7%9A%84%E3%80%81%E5%9B%A0%E6%95%85%E6%84%8F%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E9%87%8D%E5%A4%A7%E8%BF%87%E5%A4%B1%E9%80%A0%E6%88%90%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E8%B4%A2%E4%BA%A7%E6%8D%9F%E5%A4%B1%E7%9A%84%E5%85%8D%E8%B4%A3%E6%9D%A1%E6%AC%BE%E6%97%A0%E6%95%88%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="（3）对格式条款的理解发生争议的，应当按照通常理解予以解释。对格式条款有两种以上解释，应当作出不利于提供格式条款一方的解释。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%E5%AF%B9%E6%A0%BC%E5%BC%8F%E6%9D%A1%E6%AC%BE%E7%9A%84%E7%90%86%E8%A7%A3%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E4%BA%89%E8%AE%AE%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E6%8C%89%E7%85%A7%E9%80%9A%E5%B8%B8%E7%90%86%E8%A7%A3%E4%BA%88%E4%BB%A5%E8%A7%A3%E9%87%8A%E3%80%82%E5%AF%B9%E6%A0%BC%E5%BC%8F%E6%9D%A1%E6%AC%BE%E6%9C%89%E4%B8%A4%E7%A7%8D%E4%BB%A5%E4%B8%8A%E8%A7%A3%E9%87%8A%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E4%B8%8D%E5%88%A9%E4%BA%8E%E6%8F%90%E4%BE%9B%E6%A0%BC%E5%BC%8F%E6%9D%A1%E6%AC%BE%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E7%9A%84%E8%A7%A3%E9%87%8A%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（4）格式条款和非格式条款不一致的，应当采用非格式条款。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%884%EF%BC%89%E6%A0%BC%E5%BC%8F%E6%9D%A1%E6%AC%BE%E5%92%8C%E9%9D%9E%E6%A0%BC%E5%BC%8F%E6%9D%A1%E6%AC%BE%E4%B8%8D%E4%B8%80%E8%87%B4%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E9%87%87%E7%94%A8%E9%9D%9E%E6%A0%BC%E5%BC%8F%E6%9D%A1%E6%AC%BE%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="336.简述缔约过失责任制度（概念、适用情形、构成要件、赔偿范围）" _mubu_text="336.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E7%BC%94%E7%BA%A6%E8%BF%87%E5%A4%B1%E8%B4%A3%E4%BB%BB%E5%88%B6%E5%BA%A6%EF%BC%88%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5%E3%80%81%E9%80%82%E7%94%A8%E6%83%85%E5%BD%A2%E3%80%81%E6%9E%84%E6%88%90%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6%E3%80%81%E8%B5%94%E5%81%BF%E8%8C%83%E5%9B%B4%EF%BC%89">
		<outline text="缔约过失责任的概念" _mubu_text="%E7%BC%94%E7%BA%A6%E8%BF%87%E5%A4%B1%E8%B4%A3%E4%BB%BB%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">

		<outline text="合同形式，是指合同当事人设立、变更终止民事权利义务关系的一致协议的表现形式。" _mubu_text="%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E5%BD%A2%E5%BC%8F%EF%BC%8C%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E8%AE%BE%E7%AB%8B%E3%80%81%E5%8F%98%E6%9B%B4%E7%BB%88%E6%AD%A2%E6%B0%91%E4%BA%8B%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%80%E8%87%B4%E5%8D%8F%E8%AE%AE%E7%9A%84%E8%A1%A8%E7%8E%B0%E5%BD%A2%E5%BC%8F%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="是指合同当事人以口头交谈方式相互作出意思表示而订立的合同。" _mubu_text="%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%BB%A5%E5%8F%A3%E5%A4%B4%E4%BA%A4%E8%B0%88%E6%96%B9%E5%BC%8F%E7%9B%B8%E4%BA%92%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E8%80%8C%E8%AE%A2%E7%AB%8B%E7%9A%84%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="口头形式除了有约定的答复期限外，对方应立即作出接受的答复，否则，合同就不能成立。" _mubu_text="%E5%8F%A3%E5%A4%B4%E5%BD%A2%E5%BC%8F%E9%99%A4%E4%BA%86%E6%9C%89%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E7%AD%94%E5%A4%8D%E6%9C%9F%E9%99%90%E5%A4%96%EF%BC%8C%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E5%BA%94%E7%AB%8B%E5%8D%B3%E4%BD%9C%E5%87%BA%E6%8E%A5%E5%8F%97%E7%9A%84%E7%AD%94%E5%A4%8D%EF%BC%8C%E5%90%A6%E5%88%99%EF%BC%8C%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E5%B0%B1%E4%B8%8D%E8%83%BD%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>

		<outline text="口头合同形式的优点在于简便、易行、迅速、即时清结；" _mubu_text="%E5%8F%A3%E5%A4%B4%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E5%BD%A2%E5%BC%8F%E7%9A%84%E4%BC%98%E7%82%B9%E5%9C%A8%E4%BA%8E%E7%AE%80%E4%BE%BF%E3%80%81%E6%98%93%E8%A1%8C%E3%80%81%E8%BF%85%E9%80%9F%E3%80%81%E5%8D%B3%E6%97%B6%E6%B8%85%E7%BB%93%EF%BC%9B">

		<outline text="书面形式" _mubu_text="%E4%B9%A6%E9%9D%A2%E5%BD%A2%E5%BC%8F">
		<outline text="书面形式的概念" _mubu_text="%E4%B9%A6%E9%9D%A2%E5%BD%A2%E5%BC%8F%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="书面形式是指合同书、信件和数据电文等有形地表现所载内容的合同形式。" _mubu_text="%E4%B9%A6%E9%9D%A2%E5%BD%A2%E5%BC%8F%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E4%B9%A6%E3%80%81%E4%BF%A1%E4%BB%B6%E5%92%8C%E6%95%B0%E6%8D%AE%E7%94%B5%E6%96%87%E7%AD%89%3C/span%3E%E6%9C%89%E5%BD%A2%E5%9C%B0%E8%A1%A8%E7%8E%B0%E6%89%80%E8%BD%BD%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E7%9A%84%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E5%BD%A2%E5%BC%8F%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>

		<outline text="标的数额比较大、内容较复杂、不能立即履行的合同多采用书面形式。" _mubu_text="%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E6%95%B0%E9%A2%9D%E6%AF%94%E8%BE%83%E5%A4%A7%E3%80%81%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E8%BE%83%E5%A4%8D%E6%9D%82%E3%80%81%E4%B8%8D%E8%83%BD%E7%AB%8B%E5%8D%B3%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E7%9A%84%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E5%A4%9A%E9%87%87%E7%94%A8%E4%B9%A6%E9%9D%A2%E5%BD%A2%E5%BC%8F%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="书面形式包括电报、信件、电传、传真及可以保留所载信息并能够被有形复制的一切方式。" _mubu_text="%E4%B9%A6%E9%9D%A2%E5%BD%A2%E5%BC%8F%E5%8C%85%E6%8B%AC%E7%94%B5%E6%8A%A5%E3%80%81%E4%BF%A1%E4%BB%B6%E3%80%81%E7%94%B5%E4%BC%A0%E3%80%81%E4%BC%A0%E7%9C%9F%E5%8F%8A%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E4%BF%9D%E7%95%99%E6%89%80%E8%BD%BD%E4%BF%A1%E6%81%AF%E5%B9%B6%E8%83%BD%E5%A4%9F%E8%A2%AB%E6%9C%89%E5%BD%A2%E5%A4%8D%E5%88%B6%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%80%E5%88%87%E6%96%B9%E5%BC%8F%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="凡需要公证、鉴证、登记或审批的形式均为特殊书面形式。" _mubu_text="%E5%87%A1%E9%9C%80%E8%A6%81%E5%85%AC%E8%AF%81%E3%80%81%E9%89%B4%E8%AF%81%E3%80%81%E7%99%BB%E8%AE%B0%E6%88%96%E5%AE%A1%E6%89%B9%E7%9A%84%E5%BD%A2%E5%BC%8F%E5%9D%87%E4%B8%BA%E7%89%B9%E6%AE%8A%E4%B9%A6%E9%9D%A2%E5%BD%A2%E5%BC%8F%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="行为默示形式" _mubu_text="%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E9%BB%98%E7%A4%BA%E5%BD%A2%E5%BC%8F">
		<outline text="行为默示形式的概念" _mubu_text="%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E9%BB%98%E7%A4%BA%E5%BD%A2%E5%BC%8F%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="行为默示形式又称推定形式，是指合同当事人以某种表明法律意图的行为间接地表示合同内容的形式。" _mubu_text="%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E9%BB%98%E7%A4%BA%E5%BD%A2%E5%BC%8F%E5%8F%88%E7%A7%B0%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%8E%A8%E5%AE%9A%E5%BD%A2%E5%BC%8F%3C/span%3E%EF%BC%8C%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%BB%A5%E6%9F%90%E7%A7%8D%E8%A1%A8%E6%98%8E%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E6%84%8F%E5%9B%BE%E7%9A%84%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E9%97%B4%E6%8E%A5%E5%9C%B0%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E7%9A%84%E5%BD%A2%E5%BC%8F%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="认定行为默示形式系以合同的开始履行推定合同已经订立。" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E8%AE%A4%E5%AE%9A%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E9%BB%98%E7%A4%BA%E5%BD%A2%E5%BC%8F%E7%B3%BB%E4%BB%A5%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E5%BC%80%E5%A7%8B%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%8E%A8%E5%AE%9A%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E5%B7%B2%E7%BB%8F%E8%AE%A2%E7%AB%8B%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>

		</outline>
		<outline text="338.简述合同的生效要件" _mubu_text="338.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6">
		<outline text="合同的效力的概念" _mubu_text="%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="合同的效力，又称合同的法律效力，是指已成立的合同将对合同当事人乃至第三人产生的法律后果。" _mubu_text="%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%88%E7%A7%B0%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%EF%BC%8C%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%B7%B2%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E7%9A%84%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E5%B0%86%E5%AF%B9%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%B9%83%E8%87%B3%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E4%BA%A7%E7%94%9F%E7%9A%84%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E5%90%8E%E6%9E%9C%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		<outline text="已成立的合同要产生当事人预期的后果，则须满足相应的生效要件。" _mubu_text="%E5%B7%B2%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E7%9A%84%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E8%A6%81%E4%BA%A7%E7%94%9F%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E9%A2%84%E6%9C%9F%E7%9A%84%E5%90%8E%E6%9E%9C%3C/span%3E%EF%BC%8C%E5%88%99%E9%A1%BB%E6%BB%A1%E8%B6%B3%E7%9B%B8%E5%BA%94%E7%9A%84%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="合同的一般生效要件是：" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%80%E8%88%AC%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6%E6%98%AF%EF%BC%9A%3C/span%3E" _note="和民事法律行为的有效要件是一致的@简答题&nbsp;@口诀&nbsp;喝剩一半能遗宿 和声特殊徐二福&nbsp;@题眼" _mubu_note="%E5%92%8C%E6%B0%91%E4%BA%8B%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%9C%89%E6%95%88%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6%E6%98%AF%E4%B8%80%E8%87%B4%E7%9A%84%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E5%96%9D%E5%89%A9%E4%B8%80%E5%8D%8A%E8%83%BD%E9%81%97%E5%AE%BF%20%E5%92%8C%E5%A3%B0%E7%89%B9%E6%AE%8A%E5%BE%90%E4%BA%8C%E7%A6%8F&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E9%A2%98%E7%9C%BC%3C/span%3E" _heading="1" _color="#dc2d1e">
		<outline text="(1)当事人缔约时有相应的缔约能力。" _mubu_text="(1)%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E7%BC%94%E7%BA%A6%E6%97%B6%E6%9C%89%E7%9B%B8%E5%BA%94%E7%9A%84%E7%BC%94%E7%BA%A6%E8%83%BD%E5%8A%9B%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="(2)当事人的意思表示真实。" _mubu_text="(2)%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E7%9C%9F%E5%AE%9E%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="(3}不违反强制性法律规范及公序良俗。" _mubu_text="(3%7D%E4%B8%8D%E8%BF%9D%E5%8F%8D%E5%BC%BA%E5%88%B6%E6%80%A7%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E8%A7%84%E8%8C%83%E5%8F%8A%E5%85%AC%E5%BA%8F%E8%89%AF%E4%BF%97%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="有些合同除了具备一般要件外，还得具备特殊要件才能生效。特别生效要件主要有:" _mubu_text="%E6%9C%89%E4%BA%9B%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E9%99%A4%E4%BA%86%E5%85%B7%E5%A4%87%E4%B8%80%E8%88%AC%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6%E5%A4%96%EF%BC%8C%E8%BF%98%E5%BE%97%E5%85%B7%E5%A4%87%E7%89%B9%E6%AE%8A%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6%E6%89%8D%E8%83%BD%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E3%80%82%E7%89%B9%E5%88%AB%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6%E4%B8%BB%E8%A6%81%E6%9C%89:">
		<outline text="(1)法律、行政法规规定应当办理批准、登记等手续生效的合同，在办理相关手续后生效。" _mubu_text="(1)%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E3%80%81%E8%A1%8C%E6%94%BF%E6%B3%95%E8%A7%84%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E5%8A%9E%E7%90%86%E6%89%B9%E5%87%86%E3%80%81%E7%99%BB%E8%AE%B0%E7%AD%89%E6%89%8B%E7%BB%AD%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E7%9A%84%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%EF%BC%8C%E5%9C%A8%E5%8A%9E%E7%90%86%E7%9B%B8%E5%85%B3%E6%89%8B%E7%BB%AD%E5%90%8E%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="(2)附生效条件的合同自条件成就时生效。" _mubu_text="(2)%E9%99%84%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E7%9A%84%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E8%87%AA%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E6%88%90%E5%B0%B1%E6%97%B6%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="(3)附生效期限的合同自期限届至时生效。" _mubu_text="(3)%E9%99%84%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E6%9C%9F%E9%99%90%E7%9A%84%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E8%87%AA%E6%9C%9F%E9%99%90%E5%B1%8A%E8%87%B3%E6%97%B6%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="339.简述无效合同、可变更可撤销合同、效力待定合同概念、种类" _mubu_text="339.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E6%97%A0%E6%95%88%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E3%80%81%E5%8F%AF%E5%8F%98%E6%9B%B4%E5%8F%AF%E6%92%A4%E9%94%80%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E3%80%81%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%E5%BE%85%E5%AE%9A%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5%E3%80%81%E7%A7%8D%E7%B1%BB">

		<outline text="无效合同是绝对无效、自始无效、当然无效。对于无效合同，任何人都有权主张其无效，法院也可以依职权宣告该合同无效。" _mubu_text="%E6%97%A0%E6%95%88%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%98%AF%E7%BB%9D%E5%AF%B9%E6%97%A0%E6%95%88%E3%80%81%E8%87%AA%E5%A7%8B%E6%97%A0%E6%95%88%E3%80%81%E5%BD%93%E7%84%B6%E6%97%A0%E6%95%88%E3%80%82%E5%AF%B9%E4%BA%8E%E6%97%A0%E6%95%88%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%EF%BC%8C%E4%BB%BB%E4%BD%95%E4%BA%BA%E9%83%BD%E6%9C%89%E6%9D%83%E4%B8%BB%E5%BC%A0%E5%85%B6%E6%97%A0%E6%95%88%EF%BC%8C%E6%B3%95%E9%99%A2%E4%B9%9F%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E4%BE%9D%E8%81%8C%E6%9D%83%E5%AE%A3%E5%91%8A%E8%AF%A5%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%97%A0%E6%95%88%E3%80%82">
