		<outline text="一方以欺诈的手段，使对方在违背真实意思的情况下订立的合同；" _mubu_text="%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E4%BB%A5%E6%AC%BA%E8%AF%88%E7%9A%84%E6%89%8B%E6%AE%B5%EF%BC%8C%E4%BD%BF%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E5%9C%A8%E8%BF%9D%E8%83%8C%E7%9C%9F%E5%AE%9E%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E7%9A%84%E6%83%85%E5%86%B5%E4%B8%8B%E8%AE%A2%E7%AB%8B%E7%9A%84%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%EF%BC%9B">

		</outline>

		<outline text="（3）一方或者第三人以胁迫手段，使对方在违背真实意思的情况下订立的合同。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%E4%BB%A5%E8%83%81%E8%BF%AB%E6%89%8B%E6%AE%B5%EF%BC%8C%E4%BD%BF%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E5%9C%A8%E8%BF%9D%E8%83%8C%E7%9C%9F%E5%AE%9E%E6%84%8F%E6%80%9D%E7%9A%84%E6%83%85%E5%86%B5%E4%B8%8B%E8%AE%A2%E7%AB%8B%E7%9A%84%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E3%80%82" _note="@考点&nbsp;不管和同的向对方知不知道第三人胁迫的存在，受胁迫的一方都享有撤销权。" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E8%80%83%E7%82%B9%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E4%B8%8D%E7%AE%A1%E5%92%8C%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E5%90%91%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E7%9F%A5%E4%B8%8D%E7%9F%A5%E9%81%93%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%E8%83%81%E8%BF%AB%E7%9A%84%E5%AD%98%E5%9C%A8%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%97%E8%83%81%E8%BF%AB%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E9%83%BD%E4%BA%AB%E6%9C%89%E6%92%A4%E9%94%80%E6%9D%83%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（4）一方利用对方处于危困状态、缺乏判断能力等情形，致使订立时显失公平的合同。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%884%EF%BC%89%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E5%88%A9%E7%94%A8%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E5%A4%84%E4%BA%8E%E5%8D%B1%E5%9B%B0%E7%8A%B6%E6%80%81%E3%80%81%E7%BC%BA%E4%B9%8F%E5%88%A4%E6%96%AD%E8%83%BD%E5%8A%9B%E7%AD%89%E6%83%85%E5%BD%A2%EF%BC%8C%E8%87%B4%E4%BD%BF%E8%AE%A2%E7%AB%8B%E6%97%B6%E6%98%BE%E5%A4%B1%E5%85%AC%E5%B9%B3%E7%9A%84%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E3%80%82">
		</outline>

		<outline text="撤销权在下列情形下消灭:" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%92%A4%E9%94%80%E6%9D%83%E5%9C%A8%E4%B8%8B%E5%88%97%E6%83%85%E5%BD%A2%E4%B8%8B%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD:%3C/span%3E" _note="@简答题&nbsp;@题眼&nbsp;@口诀&nbsp;车灭形 知撤一 误三月 胁止一 明放弃 订五年" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E9%A2%98%E7%9C%BC%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E8%BD%A6%E7%81%AD%E5%BD%A2%20%E7%9F%A5%E6%92%A4%E4%B8%80%20%E8%AF%AF%E4%B8%89%E6%9C%88%20%E8%83%81%E6%AD%A2%E4%B8%80%20%E6%98%8E%E6%94%BE%E5%BC%83%20%E8%AE%A2%E4%BA%94%E5%B9%B4" _heading="1" _color="#dc2d1e">
		<outline text="（1）当事人自知道或者应当知道撤销事由之日起一年内、重大误解的当事人自知道或者应当知道撤销事由之日起三个月内没有行使撤销权。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%881%EF%BC%89%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E8%87%AA%E7%9F%A5%E9%81%93%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E7%9F%A5%E9%81%93%E6%92%A4%E9%94%80%E4%BA%8B%E7%94%B1%E4%B9%8B%E6%97%A5%E8%B5%B7%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%86%85%E3%80%81%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E9%87%8D%E5%A4%A7%E8%AF%AF%E8%A7%A3%E7%9A%84%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%3C/span%3E%E8%87%AA%E7%9F%A5%E9%81%93%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E7%9F%A5%E9%81%93%E6%92%A4%E9%94%80%E4%BA%8B%E7%94%B1%E4%B9%8B%E6%97%A5%E8%B5%B7%E4%B8%89%E4%B8%AA%E6%9C%88%E5%86%85%E6%B2%A1%E6%9C%89%E8%A1%8C%E4%BD%BF%E6%92%A4%E9%94%80%E6%9D%83%E3%80%82" _note="@考点&nbsp;重大误解只包括当事人对于合同内容的误解，不包括对于合同动机的误解。" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E8%80%83%E7%82%B9%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E9%87%8D%E5%A4%A7%E8%AF%AF%E8%A7%A3%E5%8F%AA%E5%8C%85%E6%8B%AC%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E5%AF%B9%E4%BA%8E%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E7%9A%84%E8%AF%AF%E8%A7%A3%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%8D%E5%8C%85%E6%8B%AC%E5%AF%B9%E4%BA%8E%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E5%8A%A8%E6%9C%BA%E7%9A%84%E8%AF%AF%E8%A7%A3%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（2）当事人受胁迫，自胁迫行为终止之日起一年内没有行使撤销权。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E5%8F%97%E8%83%81%E8%BF%AB%EF%BC%8C%E8%87%AA%E8%83%81%E8%BF%AB%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E7%BB%88%E6%AD%A2%E4%B9%8B%E6%97%A5%E8%B5%B7%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%86%85%E6%B2%A1%E6%9C%89%E8%A1%8C%E4%BD%BF%E6%92%A4%E9%94%80%E6%9D%83%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="（3）当事人知道撤销事由后明确表示或者以自己的行为表明放弃撤销权。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E7%9F%A5%E9%81%93%E6%92%A4%E9%94%80%E4%BA%8B%E7%94%B1%E5%90%8E%E6%98%8E%E7%A1%AE%E8%A1%A8%E7%A4%BA%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E4%BB%A5%E8%87%AA%E5%B7%B1%E7%9A%84%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E8%A1%A8%E6%98%8E%E6%94%BE%E5%BC%83%E6%92%A4%E9%94%80%E6%9D%83%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="效力待定合同" _mubu_text="%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%E5%BE%85%E5%AE%9A%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C">
		<outline text="效力待定合同的概念" _mubu_text="%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%E5%BE%85%E5%AE%9A%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="效力待定合同，是指虽已成立，但其效力在成立之时尚未确定，有待其他事实予以确定的合同。" _mubu_text="%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%E5%BE%85%E5%AE%9A%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%EF%BC%8C%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E8%99%BD%E5%B7%B2%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%EF%BC%8C%E4%BD%86%E5%85%B6%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%E5%9C%A8%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E4%B9%8B%E6%97%B6%E5%B0%9A%E6%9C%AA%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%EF%BC%8C%E6%9C%89%E5%BE%85%E5%85%B6%E4%BB%96%E4%BA%8B%E5%AE%9E%E4%BA%88%E4%BB%A5%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="(1)限制民事行为能力人依法不能独立订立而又未经其法定代理人事先同意的合同。此种合同是否生效取决于法定代理人是否追认。" _mubu_text="(1)%E9%99%90%E5%88%B6%E6%B0%91%E4%BA%8B%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%BA%E8%83%BD%E5%8A%9B%E4%BA%BA%E4%BE%9D%E6%B3%95%E4%B8%8D%E8%83%BD%E7%8B%AC%E7%AB%8B%E8%AE%A2%E7%AB%8B%E8%80%8C%E5%8F%88%E6%9C%AA%E7%BB%8F%E5%85%B6%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E4%BB%A3%E7%90%86%E4%BA%BA%E4%BA%8B%E5%85%88%E5%90%8C%E6%84%8F%E7%9A%84%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E3%80%82%E6%AD%A4%E7%A7%8D%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%98%AF%E5%90%A6%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E5%8F%96%E5%86%B3%E4%BA%8E%E6%B3%95%E5%AE%9A%E4%BB%A3%E7%90%86%E4%BA%BA%E6%98%AF%E5%90%A6%E8%BF%BD%E8%AE%A4%E3%80%82">
		</outline>

		<outline text="340.简述全面履行原则的规则" _mubu_text="340.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E5%85%A8%E9%9D%A2%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99%E7%9A%84%E8%A7%84%E5%88%99">
		<outline text="全面履行原则" _mubu_text="%E5%85%A8%E9%9D%A2%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99">
		<outline text="全面履行原则，又称正确履行原则或适当履行原则。" _mubu_text="%E5%85%A8%E9%9D%A2%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%88%E7%A7%B0%E6%AD%A3%E7%A1%AE%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99%E6%88%96%E9%80%82%E5%BD%93%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="该原则要求当事人按照合同约定的标的、数量、质量、履行期限、履行地点、履行方式，全面完成合同义务。" _mubu_text="%E8%AF%A5%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99%E8%A6%81%E6%B1%82%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E6%8C%89%E7%85%A7%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E6%A0%87%E7%9A%84%E3%80%81%E6%95%B0%E9%87%8F%E3%80%81%E8%B4%A8%E9%87%8F%E3%80%81%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%9C%9F%E9%99%90%E3%80%81%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E5%9C%B0%E7%82%B9%E3%80%81%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%96%B9%E5%BC%8F%EF%BC%8C%E5%85%A8%E9%9D%A2%E5%AE%8C%E6%88%90%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E3%80%82">
		</outline>

		<outline text="341.简述同时履行抗辩权的概念、成立要件、效力" _mubu_text="341.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E5%90%8C%E6%97%B6%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5%E3%80%81%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6%E3%80%81%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B">
		<outline text="同时履行抗辩权的概念" _mubu_text="%E5%90%8C%E6%97%B6%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="同时履行抗辩权，是指双务合同的当事人在没有约定履行顺序或约定应同时履行的情况下，一方当事人在对方未为对待给付之前，得拒绝履行自己债务的权利。" _mubu_text="%E5%90%8C%E6%97%B6%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%8C%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%8F%8C%E5%8A%A1%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E5%9C%A8%E6%B2%A1%E6%9C%89%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E9%A1%BA%E5%BA%8F%E6%88%96%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E5%BA%94%E5%90%8C%E6%97%B6%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E7%9A%84%E6%83%85%E5%86%B5%E4%B8%8B%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E5%9C%A8%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E6%9C%AA%E4%B8%BA%E5%AF%B9%E5%BE%85%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E4%B9%8B%E5%89%8D%EF%BC%8C%E5%BE%97%E6%8B%92%E7%BB%9D%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E8%87%AA%E5%B7%B1%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E3%80%82" _note="@必须掌握的概念" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%BF%85%E9%A1%BB%E6%8E%8C%E6%8F%A1%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>

		<outline text="同时履行抗辩权的构成要件包括:" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%90%8C%E6%97%B6%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E6%9E%84%E6%88%90%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6%E5%8C%85%E6%8B%AC:%3C/span%3E" _note="@简答题&nbsp;@题眼&nbsp;@口诀&nbsp;铜绿箭筒漆不可" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E9%A2%98%E7%9C%BC%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E9%93%9C%E7%BB%BF%E7%AE%AD%E7%AD%92%E6%BC%86%E4%B8%8D%E5%8F%AF" _heading="1" _color="#dc2d1e">
		<outline text="同时履行抗辩权的概念" _mubu_text="%E5%90%8C%E6%97%B6%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="同时履行抗辩权，是指双务合同的当事人在没有约定履行顺序或约定应同时履行的情况下，一方当事人在对方未为对待给付之前，得拒绝履行自己债务的权利。" _mubu_text="%E5%90%8C%E6%97%B6%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%8C%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%8F%8C%E5%8A%A1%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E5%9C%A8%E6%B2%A1%E6%9C%89%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E9%A1%BA%E5%BA%8F%E6%88%96%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E5%BA%94%E5%90%8C%E6%97%B6%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E7%9A%84%E6%83%85%E5%86%B5%E4%B8%8B%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E5%9C%A8%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E6%9C%AA%E4%B8%BA%E5%AF%B9%E5%BE%85%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E4%B9%8B%E5%89%8D%EF%BC%8C%E5%BE%97%E6%8B%92%E7%BB%9D%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E8%87%AA%E5%B7%B1%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="(1)须当事人就同一双务合同互负债务。" _mubu_text="(1)%E9%A1%BB%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E5%B0%B1%E5%90%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%8F%8C%E5%8A%A1%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E4%BA%92%E8%B4%9F%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="(2)须双方互负的债务均届清偿期。" _mubu_text="(2)%E9%A1%BB%E5%8F%8C%E6%96%B9%E4%BA%92%E8%B4%9F%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E5%9D%87%E5%B1%8A%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF%E6%9C%9F%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="(3)须对方未履行债务或履行债务不符合约定。" _mubu_text="(3)%E9%A1%BB%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E6%9C%AA%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E6%88%96%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%B8%8D%E7%AC%A6%E5%90%88%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="(4)须对方的对待给付是可能履行的。" _mubu_text="(4)%E9%A1%BB%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E7%9A%84%E5%AF%B9%E5%BE%85%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E6%98%AF%E5%8F%AF%E8%83%BD%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E7%9A%84%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="同时履行抗辩权的的适用" _mubu_text="%E5%90%8C%E6%97%B6%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E7%9A%84%E9%80%82%E7%94%A8">
		<outline text="同时履行抗辩权制度主要适用于双务合同，如买卖、租赁、承揽等。" _mubu_text="%E5%90%8C%E6%97%B6%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E6%9D%83%E5%88%B6%E5%BA%A6%E4%B8%BB%E8%A6%81%E9%80%82%E7%94%A8%E4%BA%8E%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%8F%8C%E5%8A%A1%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%3C/span%3E%EF%BC%8C%E5%A6%82%E4%B9%B0%E5%8D%96%E3%80%81%E7%A7%9F%E8%B5%81%E3%80%81%E6%89%BF%E6%8F%BD%E7%AD%89%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="此外,当事人因合同不成立、无效、被撤销或解除而产生的相互义务，若具有对价关系，也可主张同时履行抗辩权。" _mubu_text="%E6%AD%A4%E5%A4%96,%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E5%9B%A0%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E4%B8%8D%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E3%80%81%E6%97%A0%E6%95%88%E3%80%81%E8%A2%AB%E6%92%A4%E9%94%80%E6%88%96%E8%A7%A3%E9%99%A4%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E8%80%8C%E4%BA%A7%E7%94%9F%E7%9A%84%E7%9B%B8%E4%BA%92%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%3C/span%3E%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E8%8B%A5%E5%85%B7%E6%9C%89%E5%AF%B9%E4%BB%B7%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%3C/span%3E%EF%BC%8C%E4%B9%9F%E5%8F%AF%E4%B8%BB%E5%BC%A0%E5%90%8C%E6%97%B6%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E6%9D%83%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="对价关系" _mubu_text="%E5%AF%B9%E4%BB%B7%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB">
		<outline text="对价关系是指双务合同中双方当事人的互负对待给付义务之间的互相依赖关系。" _mubu_text="%E5%AF%B9%E4%BB%B7%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%8F%8C%E5%8A%A1%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E4%B8%AD%E5%8F%8C%E6%96%B9%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E4%BA%92%E8%B4%9F%E5%AF%B9%E5%BE%85%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E4%B9%8B%E9%97%B4%E7%9A%84%E4%BA%92%E7%9B%B8%E4%BE%9D%E8%B5%96%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="同时履行抗辩权的效力（符合一时抗辩权的效力特征）" _mubu_text="%E5%90%8C%E6%97%B6%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%EF%BC%88%E7%AC%A6%E5%90%88%E4%B8%80%E6%97%B6%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%E7%89%B9%E5%BE%81%EF%BC%89">
		<outline text="一时抗辩权的概念" _mubu_text="%E4%B8%80%E6%97%B6%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="一时抗辩权，又叫延缓抗辩权、延期抗辩权，是指抗辩权的行使可以暂时地拒绝相对人的请求权效力。" _mubu_text="%E4%B8%80%E6%97%B6%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%88%E5%8F%AB%E5%BB%B6%E7%BC%93%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E6%9D%83%E3%80%81%E5%BB%B6%E6%9C%9F%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%8C%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E8%A1%8C%E4%BD%BF%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E6%9A%82%E6%97%B6%E5%9C%B0%E6%8B%92%E7%BB%9D%E7%9B%B8%E5%AF%B9%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E8%AF%B7%E6%B1%82%E6%9D%83%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="比如同时履行抗辩权，一方当事人在相对方未为对待给付前, 可行使抗辩权暂时拒绝相对方的请求。一旦相对方已为对待给付并提出请求给付时,则一方无同时履行抗辩权，相对方的请求立即发生效力。" _mubu_text="%E6%AF%94%E5%A6%82%E5%90%8C%E6%97%B6%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%8C%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E5%9C%A8%E7%9B%B8%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E6%9C%AA%E4%B8%BA%E5%AF%B9%E5%BE%85%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E5%89%8D,%20%E5%8F%AF%E8%A1%8C%E4%BD%BF%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E6%9D%83%E6%9A%82%E6%97%B6%E6%8B%92%E7%BB%9D%E7%9B%B8%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E7%9A%84%E8%AF%B7%E6%B1%82%E3%80%82%E4%B8%80%E6%97%A6%E7%9B%B8%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E5%B7%B2%E4%B8%BA%E5%AF%B9%E5%BE%85%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E5%B9%B6%E6%8F%90%E5%87%BA%E8%AF%B7%E6%B1%82%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E6%97%B6,%E5%88%99%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E6%97%A0%E5%90%8C%E6%97%B6%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%8C%E7%9B%B8%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E7%9A%84%E8%AF%B7%E6%B1%82%E7%AB%8B%E5%8D%B3%E5%8F%91%E7%94%9F%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="同时履行抗辩权属于延期抗辩权、一时抗辩权，其效力主要在于对方未履行或履行债务不符合约定时，有拒绝履行自己债务的权利。" _mubu_text="%E5%90%8C%E6%97%B6%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E6%9D%83%E5%B1%9E%E4%BA%8E%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%BB%B6%E6%9C%9F%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E6%9D%83%E3%80%81%E4%B8%80%E6%97%B6%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%8C%E5%85%B6%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%E4%B8%BB%E8%A6%81%E5%9C%A8%E4%BA%8E%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E6%9C%AA%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%88%96%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%B8%8D%E7%AC%A6%E5%90%88%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E6%97%B6%EF%BC%8C%E6%9C%89%E6%8B%92%E7%BB%9D%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E8%87%AA%E5%B7%B1%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		<outline text="如果对方履行了债务，该权利即消灭。" _mubu_text="%E5%A6%82%E6%9E%9C%E5%AF%B9%E6%96%B9%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E4%BA%86%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%EF%BC%8C%E8%AF%A5%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E5%8D%B3%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%E3%80%82">
		</outline>

		<outline text="342.简述先履行抗辩权的概念、成立要件、效力" _mubu_text="342.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E5%85%88%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5%E3%80%81%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6%E3%80%81%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B">
		<outline text="先履行抗辩权的概念" _mubu_text="%E5%85%88%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="先履行抗辩权是指，在当事人互负债务且有先后履行顺序的情况下，负有先履行义务的一方未履行债务或履行债务不符合约定时，后履行一方拒绝其履行要求的权利。" _mubu_text="%E5%85%88%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E6%9D%83%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%EF%BC%8C%E5%9C%A8%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%BA%92%E8%B4%9F%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%B8%94%E6%9C%89%E5%85%88%E5%90%8E%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E9%A1%BA%E5%BA%8F%E7%9A%84%E6%83%85%E5%86%B5%E4%B8%8B%EF%BC%8C%E8%B4%9F%E6%9C%89%E5%85%88%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E6%9C%AA%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E6%88%96%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%B8%8D%E7%AC%A6%E5%90%88%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E6%97%B6%EF%BC%8C%E5%90%8E%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E6%8B%92%E7%BB%9D%E5%85%B6%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E8%A6%81%E6%B1%82%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E3%80%82" _note="@必须掌握的概念" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%BF%85%E9%A1%BB%E6%8E%8C%E6%8F%A1%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5%3C/span%3E">
		</outline>
		</outline>
		<outline text="先履行抗辩权的成立要件包括:" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E5%85%88%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6%E5%8C%85%E6%8B%AC:%3C/span%3E" _note="@简答题&nbsp;@题眼&nbsp;@口诀&nbsp;鲜绿剑筒漆先补" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E7%AE%80%E7%AD%94%E9%A2%98%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E9%A2%98%E7%9C%BC%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E9%B2%9C%E7%BB%BF%E5%89%91%E7%AD%92%E6%BC%86%E5%85%88%E8%A1%A5" _heading="1" _color="#dc2d1e">
		<outline text="先履行抗辩权的概念" _mubu_text="%E5%85%88%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="先履行抗辩权是指，在当事人互负债务且有先后履行顺序的情况下，负有先履行义务的一方未履行债务或履行债务不符合约定时，后履行一方拒绝其履行要求的权利。" _mubu_text="%E5%85%88%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E6%9D%83%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%EF%BC%8C%E5%9C%A8%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E4%BA%92%E8%B4%9F%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%B8%94%E6%9C%89%E5%85%88%E5%90%8E%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E9%A1%BA%E5%BA%8F%E7%9A%84%E6%83%85%E5%86%B5%E4%B8%8B%EF%BC%8C%E8%B4%9F%E6%9C%89%E5%85%88%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E6%9C%AA%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E6%88%96%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%B8%8D%E7%AC%A6%E5%90%88%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%E6%97%B6%EF%BC%8C%E5%90%8E%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E6%8B%92%E7%BB%9D%E5%85%B6%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E8%A6%81%E6%B1%82%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E3%80%82" _note="@必须掌握的概念" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%BF%85%E9%A1%BB%E6%8E%8C%E6%8F%A1%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5%3C/span%3E">

		<outline text="(3)一方当事人有先为履行的义务。" _mubu_text="(3)%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E5%BD%93%E4%BA%8B%E4%BA%BA%E6%9C%89%E5%85%88%E4%B8%BA%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E7%9A%84%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%E3%80%82">
		</outline>
		<outline text="(4)应当先履行的一方未履行债务或者履行债务不符合约定，如履行迟延、不完全履行、部分履行等。" _mubu_text="(4)%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E5%85%88%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E7%9A%84%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E6%9C%AA%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%B8%8D%E7%AC%A6%E5%90%88%E7%BA%A6%E5%AE%9A%EF%BC%8C%E5%A6%82%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E8%BF%9F%E5%BB%B6%E3%80%81%E4%B8%8D%E5%AE%8C%E5%85%A8%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E3%80%81%E9%83%A8%E5%88%86%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E7%AD%89%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="先履行抗辩权的效力（符合一时抗辩权的效力特征）" _mubu_text="%E5%85%88%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%EF%BC%88%E7%AC%A6%E5%90%88%E4%B8%80%E6%97%B6%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%E7%89%B9%E5%BE%81%EF%BC%89">
		<outline text="先履行抗辩权属于一时抗辩权，其成立及行使，使得后履行一方可中止履行自己的债务，以保护自己的期限利益、顺序利益；" _mubu_text="%E5%85%88%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E6%9D%83%E5%B1%9E%E4%BA%8E%E4%B8%80%E6%97%B6%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%8C%E5%85%B6%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E5%8F%8A%E8%A1%8C%E4%BD%BF%EF%BC%8C%E4%BD%BF%E5%BE%97%E5%90%8E%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E5%8F%AF%E4%B8%AD%E6%AD%A2%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E8%87%AA%E5%B7%B1%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%EF%BC%8C%E4%BB%A5%E4%BF%9D%E6%8A%A4%E8%87%AA%E5%B7%B1%E7%9A%84%E6%9C%9F%E9%99%90%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%E3%80%81%E9%A1%BA%E5%BA%8F%E5%88%A9%E7%9B%8A%EF%BC%9B">
		</outline>
		<outline text="在先履行一方采取了补救措施、变违约为适当履行的情况下，先履行抗辩权消灭，后履行一方须履行债务。​" _mubu_text="%E5%9C%A8%E5%85%88%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E9%87%87%E5%8F%96%E4%BA%86%E8%A1%A5%E6%95%91%E6%8E%AA%E6%96%BD%E3%80%81%E5%8F%98%E8%BF%9D%E7%BA%A6%E4%B8%BA%E9%80%82%E5%BD%93%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E7%9A%84%E6%83%85%E5%86%B5%E4%B8%8B%EF%BC%8C%E5%85%88%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E6%9D%83%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%EF%BC%8C%E5%90%8E%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E9%A1%BB%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E3%80%82%E2%80%8B">

		<outline text="不安抗辩权的效力在于:" _mubu_text="%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E4%B8%8D%E5%AE%89%E6%8A%97%E8%BE%A9%E6%9D%83%E7%9A%84%E6%95%88%E5%8A%9B%E5%9C%A8%E4%BA%8E:%3C/span%3E" _note="@口诀&nbsp;不安小丽植保踢回未接" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%8F%A3%E8%AF%80%3C/span%3E&amp;nbsp;%E4%B8%8D%E5%AE%89%E5%B0%8F%E4%B8%BD%E6%A4%8D%E4%BF%9D%E8%B8%A2%E5%9B%9E%E6%9C%AA%E6%8E%A5" _heading="1" _color="#75c940">

		<outline text="（2）在后履行一方提供适当担保时，先履行一方应当恢复履行。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%882%EF%BC%89%E5%9C%A8%E5%90%8E%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E6%8F%90%E4%BE%9B%E9%80%82%E5%BD%93%E6%8B%85%E4%BF%9D%E6%97%B6%EF%BC%8C%E5%85%88%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E5%BA%94%E5%BD%93%E6%81%A2%E5%A4%8D%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="（3）如果后履行一方在合理期限内未恢复履行能力且未提供适当担保，先履行一方可以解除合同。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%883%EF%BC%89%E5%A6%82%E6%9E%9C%E5%90%8E%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E5%9C%A8%E5%90%88%E7%90%86%E6%9C%9F%E9%99%90%E5%86%85%E6%9C%AA%E6%81%A2%E5%A4%8D%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E8%83%BD%E5%8A%9B%E4%B8%94%E6%9C%AA%E6%8F%90%E4%BE%9B%E9%80%82%E5%BD%93%E6%8B%85%E4%BF%9D%EF%BC%8C%E5%85%88%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E4%B8%80%E6%96%B9%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E8%A7%A3%E9%99%A4%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="344.简述债权人的保全权（代位权、撤销权）的概念、成立要件、后果" _mubu_text="344.%E7%AE%80%E8%BF%B0%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E4%BF%9D%E5%85%A8%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%88%E4%BB%A3%E4%BD%8D%E6%9D%83%E3%80%81%E6%92%A4%E9%94%80%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%89%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5%E3%80%81%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E8%A6%81%E4%BB%B6%E3%80%81%E5%90%8E%E6%9E%9C">
		<outline text="合同的保全的概念" _mubu_text="%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E4%BF%9D%E5%85%A8%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5">
		<outline text="合同的保全是指法律为了保障债权人权益而规定的实施保障债务人一般财产（责任财产）完整性的措施。" _mubu_text="%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E4%BF%9D%E5%85%A8%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E4%B8%BA%E4%BA%86%E4%BF%9D%E9%9A%9C%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E6%9D%83%E7%9B%8A%E8%80%8C%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E5%AE%9E%E6%96%BD%E4%BF%9D%E9%9A%9C%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%80%E8%88%AC%E8%B4%A2%E4%BA%A7%EF%BC%88%E8%B4%A3%E4%BB%BB%E8%B4%A2%E4%BA%A7%EF%BC%89%E5%AE%8C%E6%95%B4%E6%80%A7%E7%9A%84%E6%8E%AA%E6%96%BD%E3%80%82" _note="@必须掌握的概念" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E5%BF%85%E9%A1%BB%E6%8E%8C%E6%8F%A1%E7%9A%84%E6%A6%82%E5%BF%B5%3C/span%3E">
		<outline text="合同的保全，又称合同之债的保全，属于广义的合同担保，其理论及立法根据是任何一个债务人原则上均对外承担无限责任，故其一般财产是担保债权实现的总担保，该项财产亦称“责任财产”。法律所规定的保障该项财产完整性的措施即为合同的保全。" _mubu_text="%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E4%BF%9D%E5%85%A8%EF%BC%8C%E5%8F%88%E7%A7%B0%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E4%B9%8B%E5%80%BA%E7%9A%84%E4%BF%9D%E5%85%A8%EF%BC%8C%E5%B1%9E%E4%BA%8E%E5%B9%BF%E4%B9%89%E7%9A%84%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E6%8B%85%E4%BF%9D%EF%BC%8C%E5%85%B6%E7%90%86%E8%AE%BA%E5%8F%8A%E7%AB%8B%E6%B3%95%E6%A0%B9%E6%8D%AE%E6%98%AF%E4%BB%BB%E4%BD%95%E4%B8%80%E4%B8%AA%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E5%8E%9F%E5%88%99%E4%B8%8A%E5%9D%87%E5%AF%B9%E5%A4%96%E6%89%BF%E6%8B%85%E6%97%A0%E9%99%90%E8%B4%A3%E4%BB%BB%EF%BC%8C%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E6%95%85%E5%85%B6%E4%B8%80%E8%88%AC%E8%B4%A2%E4%BA%A7%E6%98%AF%E6%8B%85%E4%BF%9D%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E5%AE%9E%E7%8E%B0%E7%9A%84%E6%80%BB%E6%8B%85%E4%BF%9D%EF%BC%8C%E8%AF%A5%E9%A1%B9%E8%B4%A2%E4%BA%A7%E4%BA%A6%E7%A7%B0%E2%80%9C%E8%B4%A3%E4%BB%BB%E8%B4%A2%E4%BA%A7%E2%80%9D%E3%80%82%E6%B3%95%E5%BE%8B%E6%89%80%E8%A7%84%E5%AE%9A%E7%9A%84%E4%BF%9D%E9%9A%9C%E8%AF%A5%E9%A1%B9%E8%B4%A2%E4%BA%A7%E5%AE%8C%E6%95%B4%E6%80%A7%E7%9A%84%E6%8E%AA%E6%96%BD%E5%8D%B3%E4%B8%BA%E5%90%88%E5%90%8C%E7%9A%84%E4%BF%9D%E5%85%A8%E3%80%82%3C/span%3E">

		</outline>
		<outline text="(2)债务人对第三人享有债权且该债权已到期。" _mubu_text="(2)%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E5%AF%B9%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%E4%BA%AB%E6%9C%89%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%B8%94%E8%AF%A5%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E5%B7%B2%E5%88%B0%E6%9C%9F%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="(3)债务人怠于行使到期债权对债权人造成损害。" _mubu_text="(3)%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E6%80%A0%E4%BA%8E%E8%A1%8C%E4%BD%BF%E5%88%B0%E6%9C%9F%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E5%AF%B9%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E9%80%A0%E6%88%90%E6%8D%9F%E5%AE%B3%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="这是指债务人不履行其对债权人的到期债务,又不以诉讼方式或者仲裁方式向其债务人主张其享有的具有金钱给付内容的到期债权，致使债权人的到期债权未能实现。" _mubu_text="%E8%BF%99%E6%98%AF%E6%8C%87%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%8D%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E5%85%B6%E5%AF%B9%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%88%B0%E6%9C%9F%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1,%E5%8F%88%E4%B8%8D%E4%BB%A5%E8%AF%89%E8%AE%BC%E6%96%B9%E5%BC%8F%E6%88%96%E8%80%85%E4%BB%B2%E8%A3%81%E6%96%B9%E5%BC%8F%E5%90%91%E5%85%B6%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%BB%E5%BC%A0%E5%85%B6%E4%BA%AB%E6%9C%89%E7%9A%84%E5%85%B7%E6%9C%89%E9%87%91%E9%92%B1%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9%E7%9A%84%E5%88%B0%E6%9C%9F%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%EF%BC%8C%E8%87%B4%E4%BD%BF%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%88%B0%E6%9C%9F%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E6%9C%AA%E8%83%BD%E5%AE%9E%E7%8E%B0%E3%80%82">

		<outline text="(4) 债务人对第三人的债权为非专属性权利和可以强制执行的权利。" _mubu_text="(4)%20%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E5%AF%B9%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%B8%BA%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E9%9D%9E%E4%B8%93%E5%B1%9E%E6%80%A7%3C/span%3E%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E5%92%8C%E5%8F%AF%E4%BB%A5%E5%BC%BA%E5%88%B6%E6%89%A7%E8%A1%8C%E7%9A%84%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E3%80%82">
		<outline text="通常而言,基于扶养关系、抚养关系、赡养关系、继承关系产生的给付请求权和劳动报酬、退休金、养老金、抚恤金、安置费、人寿保险、人身伤害赔偿请求权等权利属于专属于债务人自身的债权。" _mubu_text="%E9%80%9A%E5%B8%B8%E8%80%8C%E8%A8%80,%E5%9F%BA%E4%BA%8E%E6%89%B6%E5%85%BB%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E3%80%81%E6%8A%9A%E5%85%BB%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E3%80%81%E8%B5%A1%E5%85%BB%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E3%80%81%E7%BB%A7%E6%89%BF%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E4%BA%A7%E7%94%9F%E7%9A%84%E7%BB%99%E4%BB%98%E8%AF%B7%E6%B1%82%E6%9D%83%E5%92%8C%E5%8A%B3%E5%8A%A8%E6%8A%A5%E9%85%AC%E3%80%81%E9%80%80%E4%BC%91%E9%87%91%E3%80%81%E5%85%BB%E8%80%81%E9%87%91%E3%80%81%E6%8A%9A%E6%81%A4%E9%87%91%E3%80%81%E5%AE%89%E7%BD%AE%E8%B4%B9%E3%80%81%E4%BA%BA%E5%AF%BF%E4%BF%9D%E9%99%A9%E3%80%81%E4%BA%BA%E8%BA%AB%E4%BC%A4%E5%AE%B3%E8%B5%94%E5%81%BF%E8%AF%B7%E6%B1%82%E6%9D%83%E7%AD%89%E6%9D%83%E5%88%A9%E5%B1%9E%E4%BA%8E%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E4%B8%93%E5%B1%9E%E4%BA%8E%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E8%87%AA%E8%BA%AB%E7%9A%84%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%3C/span%3E%E3%80%82" _note="@考点" _mubu_note="%3Cspan%20class=%22tag%22%20style=%22text-decoration-line:%20underline;%20opacity:%200.6;%20color:%20inherit;%22%3E@%E8%80%83%E7%82%B9%3C/span%3E">

		<outline text="（4）债权人向第三人即次债务人提起的代位权诉讼，经人民法院审理后认定代位权成立的，由第三人向债权人履行清偿义务，债权人与债务人、债务人与第三人之间相应的债权债务关系消灭。" _mubu_text="%EF%BC%884%EF%BC%89%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E5%90%91%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%E5%8D%B3%E6%AC%A1%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E6%8F%90%E8%B5%B7%E7%9A%84%E4%BB%A3%E4%BD%8D%E6%9D%83%E8%AF%89%E8%AE%BC%EF%BC%8C%E7%BB%8F%E4%BA%BA%E6%B0%91%E6%B3%95%E9%99%A2%E5%AE%A1%E7%90%86%E5%90%8E%E8%AE%A4%E5%AE%9A%E4%BB%A3%E4%BD%8D%E6%9D%83%E6%88%90%E7%AB%8B%E7%9A%84%EF%BC%8C%E7%94%B1%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%E5%90%91%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E5%B1%A5%E8%A1%8C%E6%B8%85%E5%81%BF%E4%B9%89%E5%8A%A1%EF%BC%8C%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%8E%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E3%80%81%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E4%BA%BA%E4%B8%8E%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%E4%B9%8B%E9%97%B4%3Cspan%20class=%22bold%22%20style=%22font-weight:%20bold;%22%3E%E7%9B%B8%E5%BA%94%E7%9A%84%3C/span%3E%E5%80%BA%E6%9D%83%E5%80%BA%E5%8A%A1%E5%85%B3%E7%B3%BB%E6%B6%88%E7%81%AD%E3%80%82">
